## ✨ 本课程与您在网上找到的任何 Amazon Web Services Certified (AWS Certified) Developer Associate (DVA-C02) 课程都不同。

✋ 加入实时在线社区和由行业专家讲授的课程，自信地通过亚马逊网络服务认证 (AWS Certified) 开发人员助理 (DVA-C02)。我们旨在与技术行业合作，构建信息技术 (IT) 认证和在线课程的生态系统。我们相信，这将使我们的学生在开源环境中对节奏市场有 100% 的信心。我们才刚刚起步，所以您现在加入会更好！

[![加入我们的 Discord](images/discord.png '加入我们的 Discord')](https://discord.gg/RFjtXKfJy3)

## ⌛️ 简明扼要；你为什么要参加这门课程

1. 非常乐意回答您在 Udemy 问答系统内外提出的问题 :)
2. 失败了？请提交考试结果的截图并申请退款（通过我们即将推出的平台，Udemy 上无法实现）；我们始终会接受您的申请。
3. 了解以下主题：
   -亚马逊 API 网关；
   - 亚马逊 Aurora；
   - 亚马逊CloudFront；
   -亚马逊CloudWatch；
   - 亚马逊 Cognito；
   -亚马逊 DynamoDB；
   - 亚马逊弹性块存储（Amazon EBS）；
   - 亚马逊弹性计算云（Amazon EC2）；
   -亚马逊 Kinesis；
   - 亚马逊 Redshift；
   - 亚马逊关系数据库服务（Amazon RDS）；
   - 亚马逊简单存储服务（Amazon S3）；
   - 亚马逊简单队列服务（Amazon SQS）；
   - 身份验证和授权；
   -AWS 云形成；
   -AWS 云Trail；
   -AWS CodeCommit；
   -AWS CodeDeploy；
   -AWS 命令​​行界面（AWS CLI）；
   -AWS 身份和访问管理（AWS IAM）；
   -AWS 密钥管理服务（AWS KMS）；
   -AWS Lambda；
   - 云概念；
   - 公共云和私有云；
   - 无服务器；
   - 虚拟私有云（VPC）；
   - **更多！**
4. 问题与实际考试相似，没有重复（与其他课程一样;-)）。
5. 模拟考试模拟实际考试的内容、时间和通过考试所需的百分比。
6. 本课程**不是** Amazon Web Services Certified (AWS Certified) Developer Associate (DVA-C02) 考试题库。有些人使用脑筋急转弯或考试题库，但这是荒谬的，我们不会这样做。
7. 385 个**独特**问题。

## 本课程适合哪些人：

- 👨‍🎓 正在准备参加亚马逊 Web 服务认证（AWS Certified）开发人员助理（DVA-C02）考试的学生；
- 👨‍🎓 亚马逊网络服务 (AWS) 工程师；
- 👨‍🎓 Azure 工程师；
- 👨‍🎓 云架构师；
- 👨‍🎓 云工程师；
- 👨‍🎓 DevOps 工程师；
- 👨‍🎓 企业架构师；
- 👨‍🎓 Google 云平台 (GCP) 工程师；
- 👨‍🎓 基础设施工程师；
- 👨‍🎓 首席工程师；
- 👨‍🎓 产品架构师；
- 👨‍🎓 安全工程师；
- 👨‍🎓 站点可靠性工程师；
- 👨‍🎓 软件开发人员/工程师；
- 👨‍🎓 解决方案架构师；
- 👨‍🎓 团队负责人。

＃＃ 要求

- 🤩 学习很兴奋！
- 0️⃣ 需要先前的知识；
-✅ 您可以仅根据我们的实践测试考试通过 Amazon Web Services Certified (AWS Certified) Developer Associate (DVA-C02) 考试。

|	4	|	 [A company's ecommerce website is experiencing massive traffic spikes, which are causing performance problems in the company database. Users are reporting that accessing the website takes a long time. A developer wants to implement a caching layer using Amazon ElastiCache. The website is required to be responsive no matter which product a user views, and the updates to product information and prices must be strongly consistent. Which cache writing policy will satisfy these requirements?](#a-companys-ecommerce-website-is-experiencing-massive-traffic-spikes-which-are-causing-performance-problems-in-the-company-database-users-are-reporting-that-accessing-the-website-takes-a-long-time-a-developer-wants-to-implement-a-caching-layer-using-amazon-elasticache-the-website-is-required-to-be-responsive-no-matter-which-product-a-user-views-and-the-updates-to-product-information-and-prices-must-be-strongly-consistent-which-cache-writing-policy-will-satisfy-these-requirements)	<br />	一家公司的电子商务网站正在经历巨大的流量高峰，这导致公司数据库出现性能问题。用户报告称访问网站需要很长时间。开发人员希望使用 Amazon ElastiCache 实现缓存层。无论用户查看哪种产品，网站都必须响应迅速，并且产品信息和价格的更新必须保持高度一致。哪种缓存写入策略可以满足这些要求？
|	5	|	 [A Developer wants to upload data to Amazon S3 and must encrypt the data in transit. Which of the following solutions will accomplish this task? (Choose TWO)](#a-developer-wants-to-upload-data-to-amazon-s3-and-must-encrypt-the-data-in-transit-which-of-the-following-solutions-will-accomplish-this-task-choose-two)	<br />	开发人员想要将数据上传到 Amazon S3，并且必须对传输中的数据进行加密。以下哪种解决方案可以完成此任务？（选择两个）
|	6	|	 [A Developer wants to encrypt new objects that are being uploaded to an Amazon S3 bucket by an application. There must be an audit trail of who has used the key during this process. There should be no change to the performance of the application. Which type of encryption meets these requirements?](#a-developer-wants-to-encrypt-new-objects-that-are-being-uploaded-to-an-amazon-s3-bucket-by-an-application-there-must-be-an-audit-trail-of-who-has-used-the-key-during-this-process-there-should-be-no-change-to-the-performance-of-the-application-which-type-of-encryption-meets-these-requirements)	<br />	开发人员想要加密应用程序上传到 Amazon S3 存储桶的新对象。必须有审计跟踪记录，记录在此过程中谁使用了密钥。应用程序的性能不应发生变化。哪种加密类型符合这些要求？
|	7	|	 [An application is being developed to audit several AWS accounts. The application will run in Account A and must access AWS services in Accounts B and C. What is the MOST secure way to allow the application to call AWS services in each audited account?](#an-application-is-being-developed-to-audit-several-aws-accounts-the-application-will-run-in-account-a-and-must-access-aws-services-in-accounts-b-and-c-what-is-the-most-secure-way-to-allow-the-application-to-call-aws-services-in-each-audited-account)	<br />	正在开发一个应用程序来审计多个 AWS 账户。该应用程序将在账户 A 中运行，并且必须访问账户 B 和 C 中的 AWS 服务。允许应用程序在每个受审计账户中调用 AWS 服务的最安全方法是什么？
|	8	|	 [A company uses a third-party tool to build, bundle, and package rts applications on-premises and store them locally. The company uses Amazon EC2 instances to run its front-end applications. How can an application be deployed from the source control system onto the EC2 instances?](#a-company-uses-a-third-party-tool-to-build-bundle-and-package-rts-applications-on-premises-and-store-them-locally-the-company-uses-amazon-ec2-instances-to-run-its-front-end-applications-how-can-an-application-be-deployed-from-the-source-control-system-onto-the-ec2-instances)	<br />	一家公司使用第三方工具在本地构建、捆绑和打包 rts 应用程序并将其存储在本地。该公司使用 Amazon EC2 实例来运行其前端应用程序。如何将应用程序从源代码控制系统部署到 EC2 实例上？
|	9	|	 [A company is building a compute-intensive application that will run on a fleet of Amazon EC2 instances. The application uses attached Amazon EBS disks for storing data. The application will process sensitive information and all the data must be encrypted. What should a developer do to ensure the data is encrypted on disk without impacting performance?](#a-company-is-building-a-compute-intensive-application-that-will-run-on-a-fleet-of-amazon-ec2-instances-the-application-uses-attached-amazon-ebs-disks-for-storing-data-the-application-will-process-sensitive-information-and-all-the-data-must-be-encrypted-what-should-a-developer-do-to-ensure-the-data-is-encrypted-on-disk-without-impacting-performance)	<br />	一家公司正在构建一个计算密集型应用程序，该应用程序将在一组 Amazon EC2 实例上运行。该应用程序使用附加的 Amazon EBS 磁盘来存储数据。该应用程序将处理敏感信息，并且所有数据都必须加密。开发人员应该怎么做才能确保数据在磁盘上加密而不影响性能？
|	10	|	 [A global company has an application running on Amazon EC2 instances that serves image files from Amazon S3. User requests from the browser are causing high traffic, which results in degraded performance. Which optimization solution should a Developer implement to increase application performance?](#a-global-company-has-an-application-running-on-amazon-ec2-instances-that-serves-image-files-from-amazon-s3-user-requests-from-the-browser-are-causing-high-traffic-which-results-in-degraded-performance-which-optimization-solution-should-a-developer-implement-to-increase-application-performance)	<br />	一家跨国公司在 Amazon EC2 实例上运行一个应用程序，该应用程序提供来自 Amazon S3 的图像文件。来自浏览器的用户请求导致高流量，从而导致性能下降。开发人员应实施哪种优化解决方案来提高应用程序性能？
|	11	|	 [An AWS Lambda function generates a 3MB JSON file and then uploads it to an Amazon S3 bucket daily. The file contains sensitive information, so the Developer must ensure that it is encrypted before uploading to the bucket. Which of the following modifications should the Developer make to ensure that the data is encrypted before uploading it to the bucket?](#an-aws-lambda-function-generates-a-3mb-json-file-and-then-uploads-it-to-an-amazon-s3-bucket-daily-the-file-contains-sensitive-information-so-the-developer-must-ensure-that-it-is-encrypted-before-uploading-to-the-bucket-which-of-the-following-modifications-should-the-developer-make-to-ensure-that-the-data-is-encrypted-before-uploading-it-to-the-bucket)	<br />	AWS Lambda 函数每天生成一个 3MB 的 JSON 文件，然后将其上传到 Amazon S3 存储桶。该文件包含敏感信息，因此开发人员必须确保在将其上传到存储桶之前对其进行加密。开发人员应进行以下哪项修改以确保在将数据上传到存储桶之前对其进行加密？
|	12	|	 [Company D is running their corporate website on Amazon S3 accessed from http://www.companyd.com. Their marketing team has published new web fonts to a separate S3 bucket accessed by the S3 endpoint https://s3-us-west-1.amazonaws.com/cdfonts. While testing the new web fonts, Company D recognized the web fonts are being blocked by the browser. What should Company D do to prevent the web fonts from being blocked by the browser?](#company-d-is-running-their-corporate-website-on-amazon-s3-accessed-from-httpwwwcompanydcom-their-marketing-team-has-published-new-web-fonts-to-a-separate-s3-bucket-accessed-by-the-s3-endpoint-httpss3-us-west-1amazonawscomcdfonts-while-testing-the-new-web-fonts-company-d-recognized-the-web-fonts-are-being-blocked-by-the-browser-what-should-company-d-do-to-prevent-the-web-fonts-from-being-blocked-by-the-browser)	<br />	D 公司在 Amazon S3 上运行其公司网站，可从 http://www.companyd.com 访问。其营销团队已将新的 Web 字体发布到单独的 S3 存储桶中，可通过 S3 端点 https://s3-us-west-1.amazonaws.com/cdfonts 访问。在测试新的 Web 字体时，D 公司发现 Web 字体已被浏览器阻止。 D 公司应该怎么做才能防止网页字体被浏览器屏蔽？

Which combination of commands must the developer use to redeploy the AWS SAM application? |	14	|	 [An application deployed on AWS Elastic Beanstalk experiences increased error rates during deployments of new application versions, resulting in service degradation for users. The Development team believes that this is because of the reduction in capacity during the deployment steps. The team would like to change the deployment policy configuration of the environment to an option that maintains full capacity during deployment while using the existing instances. Which deployment policy will meet these requirements while using the existing instances?](#an-application-deployed-on-aws-elastic-beanstalk-experiences-increased-error-rates-during-deployments-of-new-application-versions-resulting-in-service-degradation-for-users-the-development-team-believes-that-this-is-because-of-the-reduction-in-capacity-during-the-deployment-steps-the-team-would-like-to-change-the-deployment-policy-configuration-of-the-environment-to-an-option-that-maintains-full-capacity-during-deployment-while-using-the-existing-instances-which-deployment-policy-will-meet-these-requirements-while-using-the-existing-instances)	<br />	部署在 AWS Elastic Beanstalk 上的应用程序在部署新应用程序版本时会遇到错误率增加的问题，从而导致用户的服务质量下降。开发团队认为这是由于部署步骤中的容量减少所致。团队希望将环境的部署策略配置更改为在使用现有实例的同时在部署期间保持满负荷容量的选项。哪种部署策略可以在使用现有实例的同时满足这些要求？实例？

|	16	|	 [The development team is working on an API that will be served from Amazon API gateway. The API will be served from three environments: development, test, and production. The API Gateway is configured to use 237 GB of cache in all three stages. Which is the MOST cost-efficient deployment strategy?](#the-development-team-is-working-on-an-api-that-will-be-served-from-amazon-api-gateway-the-api-will-be-served-from-three-environments-development-test-and-production-the-api-gateway-is-configured-to-use-237-gb-of-cache-in-all-three-stages-which-is-the-most-cost-efficient-deployment-strategy)	<br />	开发团队正在开发一个 API，该 API 将由 Amazon API 网关提供服务。该 API 将由三个环境提供服务：开发、测试和生产。API 网关配置为在所有三个阶段使用 237 GB 的缓存。哪种部署策略最具成本效益？
|	17	|	 [A company is migrating its on-premises database to Amazon RDS for MySQL. The company has read-heavy workloads, and wants to make sure it re-factors its code to achieve optimum read performance for its queries. How can this objective be met?](#a-company-is-migrating-its-on-premises-database-to-amazon-rds-for-mysql-the-company-has-read-heavy-workloads-and-wants-to-make-sure-it-re-factors-its-code-to-achieve-optimum-read-performance-for-its-queries-how-can-this-objective-be-met)	<br />	一家公司正在将其本地数据库迁移到 Amazon RDS for MySQL。该公司的读取工作量很大，并希望确保其代码能够重新分解，以实现查询的最佳读取性能。如何实现这一目标？

### Which of the following are good use cases for how Amazon ElastiCache can help an application? (Select TWO)

- [ ] Improve the latency of deployments performed by AWS CodeDeploy. `改善 AWS CodeDeploy 执行部署的延迟。`

- [ ] Reduce the time required to merge AWS CodeCommit branches. `减少合并 AWS CodeCommit 分支所需的时间。`
- [x] Improve performance of compute-intensive applications. `提高计算密集型应用程序的性能。`

### A developer wants to send multi-value headers to an AWS Lambda function that is registered as a target with an Application Load Balancer (ALB). What should the developer do to achieve this?
> 一位开发人员希望将多值标头发送到注册为应用负载均衡器 (ALB) 目标的 AWS Lambda 函数。开发人员应如何实现这一点？

- [ ] Place the Lambda function and target group in the same account. `将 Lambda 函数和目标组放在同一账户中。`
- [ ] Send the request body to the Lambda function with a size less than 1 MB. `将请求正文大小小于 1 MB 的数据发送到 Lambda 函数。`
- [ ] Include the Base64 encoding status, status code, status description, and headers in the Lambda function. `在 Lambda 函数中包含 Base64 编码状态、状态码、状态描述和标头。`
- [x] Enable the multi-value headers on the ALB. `在 ALB 上启用多值标头。`

### A company's ecommerce website is experiencing massive traffic spikes, which are causing performance problems in the company database. Users are reporting that accessing the website takes a long time. A developer wants to implement a caching layer using Amazon ElastiCache. The website is required to be responsive no matter which product a user views, and the updates to product information and prices must be strongly consistent. Which cache writing policy will satisfy these requirements?
> 一家公司的电子商务网站正经历巨大的流量激增，导致公司数据库的性能问题。用户报告访问网站需要很长时间。开发人员希望使用 Amazon ElastiCache 实现缓存层。无论用户查看哪个产品，网站都需要保持响应，产品信息和价格的更新必须具有强一致性。哪种缓存写入策略可以满足这些要求？

- [ ] Write to the cache directly and sync the backend at a later time. `直接写入缓存，稍后同步后端。`
- [ ] Write to the backend first and wait for the cache to expire. `先写入后端，等待缓存过期。`
- [ ] Write to the cache and the backend at the same time. `同时写入缓存和后端。`
- [x] Write to the backend first and invalidate the cache. `先写入后端，然后使缓存失效。`

### A Developer wants to upload data to Amazon S3 and must encrypt the data in transit. Which of the following solutions will accomplish this task? (Choose TWO)
> 一位开发人员希望将数据上传到 Amazon S3，并且必须在传输过程中对数据进行加密。以下哪些解决方案可以完成此任务？（选择两个）

- [ ] Set up hardware VPN tunnels to a VPC and access S3 through a VPC endpoint. `设置硬件 VPN 隧道到 VPC，并通过 VPC 终端节点访问 S3。`
- [x] Set up Client-Side Encryption with an AWS KMS-Managed Customer Master Key. `使用 AWS KMS 管理的客户主密钥设置客户端加密。`
- [ ] Set up Server-Side Encryption with AWS KMS-Managed Keys. `使用 AWS KMS 管理的密钥设置服务器端加密。`
- [x] Transfer the data over an SSL connection. `通过 SSL 连接传输数据。`
- [ ] Set up Server-Side Encryption with S3-Managed Keys. `使用 S3 管理的密钥设置服务器端加密。`

### A Developer wants to encrypt new objects that are being uploaded to an Amazon S3 bucket by an application. There must be an audit trail of who has used the key during this process. There should be no change to the performance of the application. Which type of encryption meets these requirements?
> 一位开发人员希望对由应用程序上传到 Amazon S3 存储桶的新对象进行加密。在此过程中，必须有使用密钥的审计记录，并且不应对应用程序性能产生任何变化。哪种类型的加密可以满足这些要求？

- [ ] Server-side encryption using S3-managed keys. `使用 S3 管理的密钥进行服务器端加密。`
- [x] Server-side encryption with AWS KMS-managed keys. `使用 AWS KMS 管理的密钥进行服务器端加密。`
- [ ] Client-side encryption with a client-side symmetric master key. `使用客户端对称主密钥进行客户端加密。`
- [ ] Client-side encryption with AWS KMS-managed keys. `使用 AWS KMS 管理的密钥进行客户端加密。`

### An application is being developed to audit several AWS accounts. The application will run in Account A and must access AWS services in Accounts B and C. What is the MOST secure way to allow the application to call AWS services in each audited account?
> 一个应用程序正在开发中，目的是审核多个 AWS 账户。该应用程序将在账户 A 中运行，并且必须访问账户 B 和 C 中的 AWS 服务。允许应用程序调用每个被审计账户中的 AWS 服务的最安全方法是什么？

- [x] Configure cross-account roles in each audited account. Write code in Account A that assumes those roles. `在每个被审计的账户中配置跨账户角色。在账户 A 中编写代码以假设这些角色。`
- [ ] Use S3 cross-region replication to communicate among accounts, with Amazon S3 event notifications to trigger Lambda functions. `使用 S3 跨区域复制在账户之间进行通信，并使用 Amazon S3 事件通知触发 Lambda 函数。`
- [ ] Deploy an application in each audited account with its own role. Have Account A authenticate with the application. `在每个被审计的账户中部署一个应用程序，并为其配置自己的角色。让账户 A 对应用程序进行身份验证。`
- [ ] Create an IAM user with an access key in each audited account. Write code in Account A that uses those access keys. `在每个被审计的账户中创建一个带有访问密钥的 IAM 用户，并在账户 A 中编写使用这些访问密钥的代码。`

### A company uses a third-party tool to build, bundle, and package rts applications on-premises and store them locally. The company uses Amazon EC2 instances to run its front-end applications. How can an application be deployed from the source control system onto the EC2 instances?
> 一家公司使用第三方工具在本地构建、打包和包装 rts 应用程序，并将其存储在本地。该公司使用 Amazon EC2 实例来运行前端应用程序。如何将应用程序从源代码管理系统部署到 EC2 实例上？

- [ ] Use AWS CodeDeploy and point it to the local storage to directly deploy a bundle m a zip. tar. or tar.gz format. `使用 AWS CodeDeploy 指向本地存储，以直接部署 zip、tar 或 tar.gz 格式的包。`
- [x] Upload the bundle to an Amazon S3 bucket and specify the S3 location when doing a deployment using AWS CodeDeploy. `将包上传到 Amazon S3 存储桶，并在使用 AWS CodeDeploy 进行部署时指定 S3 位置。`
- [ ] Create a repository using AWS CodeCommit to automatically trigger a deployment to the EC2 instances. `使用 AWS CodeCommit 创建一个仓库，以自动触发对 EC2 实例的部署。`
- [ ] Use AWS CodeBuild to automatically deploy the latest build to the latest EC2 instances. `使用 AWS CodeBuild 自动将最新构建部署到最新的 EC2 实例。`

### A company is building a compute-intensive application that will run on a fleet of Amazon EC2 instances. The application uses attached Amazon EBS disks for storing data. The application will process sensitive information and all the data must be encrypted. What should a developer do to ensure the data is encrypted on disk without impacting performance?
> 一家公司正在构建一个计算密集型应用程序，该应用程序将在一组 Amazon EC2 实例上运行。该应用程序使用附加的 Amazon EBS 磁盘来存储数据。该应用程序将处理敏感信息，所有数据必须加密。开发人员应该怎么做，以确保数据在磁盘上加密而不影响性能？

- [x] Configure the Amazon EC2 instance fleet to use encrypted EBS volumes for storing data. `配置 Amazon EC2 实例组以使用加密的 EBS 卷来存储数据。`
- [ ] Add logic to write all data to an encrypted Amazon S3 bucket. `添加逻辑将所有数据写入加密的 Amazon S3 存储桶。`
- [ ] Add a custom encryption algorithm to the application that will encrypt and decrypt all data. `向应用程序添加自定义加密算法，以加密和解密所有数据。`
- [ ] Create a new Amazon Machine Image (AMI) with an encrypted root volume and store the data to ephemeral disks. `创建一个新的 Amazon Machine Image (AMI)，使用加密的根卷，并将数据存储到临时磁盘。`

**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A global company has an application running on Amazon EC2 instances that serves image files from Amazon S3. User requests from the browser are causing high traffic, which results in degraded performance. Which optimization solution should a Developer implement to increase application performance?
> 一家全球公司有一个应用程序在 Amazon EC2 实例上运行，从 Amazon S3 提供图像文件。来自浏览器的用户请求导致高流量，从而导致性能下降。开发人员应该实施哪个优化解决方案来提高应用程序性能？

- [ ] Create multiple prefix in the S3 bucket to increase the request rate. `在 S3 存储桶中创建多个前缀以提高请求速率。`
- [ ] Create an Amazon ElastiCache cluster to cache and serve frequently accessed items. `创建一个 Amazon ElastiCache 集群以缓存和提供频繁访问的项目。`
- [x] Use Amazon CloudFront to serve the content of images stored in Amazon S3. `使用 Amazon CloudFront 提供存储在 Amazon S3 中的图像内容。`
- [ ] Submit a ticket to AWS support to request a rate limit increase for the S3 bucket. `提交工单给 AWS 支持以请求提高 S3 存储桶的速率限制。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### An AWS Lambda function generates a 3MB JSON file and then uploads it to an Amazon S3 bucket daily. The file contains sensitive information, so the Developer must ensure that it is encrypted before uploading to the bucket. Which of the following modifications should the Developer make to ensure that the data is encrypted before uploading it to the bucket?
> 一个 AWS Lambda 函数每天生成一个 3MB 的 JSON 文件，然后将其上传到 Amazon S3 存储桶。该文件包含敏感信息，因此开发人员必须确保在上传到存储桶之前对其进行加密。开发人员应该做哪些修改以确保数据在上传到存储桶之前已加密？

- [ ] Use the default AWS KMS customer master key for S3 in the Lambda function code. `在 Lambda 函数代码中使用 S3 的默认 AWS KMS 客户主密钥。`
- [ ] Use the S3 managed key and call the GenerateDataKey API to encrypt the file. `使用 S3 管理密钥并调用 GenerateDataKey API 来加密文件。`
- [x] Use the GenerateDataKey API, then use that data key to encrypt the file in the Lambda function code. `使用 GenerateDataKey API，然后在 Lambda 函数代码中使用该数据密钥来加密文件。`
- [ ] Use a custom KMS customer master key created for S3 in the Lambda function code. `在 Lambda 函数代码中使用为 S3 创建的自定义 KMS 客户主密钥。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### Company D is running their corporate website on Amazon S3 accessed from http://www.companyd.com. Their marketing team has published new web fonts to a separate S3 bucket accessed by the S3 endpoint https://s3-us-west-1.amazonaws.com/cdfonts. While testing the new web fonts, Company D recognized the web fonts are being blocked by the browser. What should Company D do to prevent the web fonts from being blocked by the browser?
> D 公司正在使用 Amazon S3 运行其企业网站，访问地址为 http://www.companyd.com。他们的营销团队已将新网页字体发布到一个单独的 S3 存储桶，访问地址为 S3 端点 https://s3-us-west-1.amazonaws.com/cdfonts。在测试新网页字体时，D 公司发现网页字体被浏览器阻止。D 公司应该怎么做以防止网页字体被浏览器阻止？

- [ ] Enable versioning on the cdfonts bucket for each web font. `为每个网页字体在 cdfonts 存储桶上启用版本控制。`
- [ ] Create a policy on the cdfonts bucket to enable access to everyone. `在 cdfonts 存储桶上创建一个策略以允许所有人访问。`
- [ ] Add the Content-MD5 header to the request for webfonts in the cdfonts bucket from the website. `为来自网站的对 cdfonts 存储桶的网页字体请求添加 Content-MD5 头。`
- [x] Configure the cdfonts bucket to allow cross-origin requests by creating a CORS configuration. `通过创建 CORS 配置，配置 cdfonts 存储桶以允许跨域请求。`

- [ ] sam init. `sam init。`
- [ ] sam validate. `sam 验证。`
- [x] sam build. `sam 构建。`
- [x] sam deploy. `sam 部署。`
- [ ] sam publish. `sam 发布。`

### An application deployed on AWS Elastic Beanstalk experiences increased error rates during deployments of new application versions, resulting in service degradation for users. The Development team believes that this is because of the reduction in capacity during the deployment steps. The team would like to change the deployment policy configuration of the environment to an option that maintains full capacity during deployment while using the existing instances. Which deployment policy will meet these requirements while using the existing instances?
> 部署在 AWS Elastic Beanstalk 上的应用程序在新版本的应用程序部署期间经历了增加的错误率，导致用户服务质量下降。开发团队认为，这是由于部署步骤中容量的减少。团队希望将环境的部署策略配置更改为一种在使用现有实例的同时保持部署期间完全容量的选项。哪种部署策略可以在使用现有实例的情况下满足这些要求？

- [ ] All at once. `一次性全部。`
- [ ] Rolling. `滚动。`
- [x] Rolling with additional batch. `滚动并增加批次。`
- [ ] Immutable. `不可变。`

### A Developer is creating an application that needs to locate the public IPv4 address of the Amazon EC2 instance on which it runs. How can the application locate this information?
> 开发人员正在创建一个应用程序，需要定位运行它的 Amazon EC2 实例的公共 IPv4 地址。应用程序如何找到该信息？

- [x] Get the instance metadata by retrieving http://169.254.169.254/latest/metadata/. `通过检索 http://169.254.169.254/latest/metadata/ 获取实例元数据。`
- [ ] Get the instance user data by retrieving http://169.254.169.254/latest/userdata/. `通过检索 http://169.254.169.254/latest/userdata/ 获取实例用户数据。`
- [ ] Get the application to run IFCONFIG to get the public IP address. `让应用程序运行 IFCONFIG 以获取公共 IP 地址。`
- [ ] Get the application to run IPCONFIG to get the public IP address. `让应用程序运行 IPCONFIG 以获取公共 IP 地址。`

### The development team is working on an API that will be served from Amazon API gateway. The API will be served from three environments: development, test, and production. The API Gateway is configured to use 237 GB of cache in all three stages. Which is the MOST cost-efficient deployment strategy?
> 开发团队正在开发一个将通过 Amazon API Gateway 提供的 API。该 API 将在三个环境中提供：开发、测试和生产。API Gateway 配置为在所有三个阶段使用 237 GB 的缓存。哪种是最具成本效益的部署策略？

- [ ] Create a single API Gateway with all three stages. `创建一个包含所有三个阶段的单一 API Gateway。`
- [ ] Create three API Gateways, one for each stage in a single AWS account. `创建三个 API Gateway，每个阶段一个，放在单个 AWS 账户中。`
- [ ] Create an API Gateway in three separate AWS accounts. `在三个单独的 AWS 账户中创建 API Gateway。`
- [x] Enable the cache for development and test environments only when needed. `仅在需要时为开发和测试环境启用缓存。`

### A company is migrating its on-premises database to Amazon RDS for MySQL. The company has read-heavy workloads, and wants to make sure it re-factors its code to achieve optimum read performance for its queries. How can this objective be met?
> 一家公司正在将其本地数据库迁移到 Amazon RDS for MySQL。该公司有大量的读取工作负载，想要确保重构代码以实现查询的最佳读取性能。如何实现这一目标？

- [ ] Add database retries to effectively use RDS with vertical scaling. `添加数据库重试以有效地使用 RDS 垂直扩展。`
- [ ] Use RDS with multi-AZ deployment. `使用多可用区部署的 RDS。`
- [x] Add a connection string to use an RDS read replica for read queries. `添加连接字符串以使用 RDS 只读副本进行读取查询。`
- [ ] Add a connection string to use a read replica on an EC2 instance. `添加连接字符串以使用 EC2 实例上的只读副本。`

### A developer needs to modify an application architecture to meet new functional requirements. Application data is stored in Amazon DynamoDB and processed for analysis in a nightly batch. - [ ] Client served driven. `客户端服务驱动。`
- [ ] Fan-out driven. `扇出驱动。`
- [ ] Schedule driven. `计划驱动。`

### A software company needs to make sure user-uploaded documents are securely stored in Amazon S3. The documents must be encrypted at rest in Amazon S3. The company does not want to manage the security infrastructure in-house, but the company still needs extra protection to ensure it has control over its encryption keys due to industry regulations. Which encryption strategy should a developer use to meet these requirements?
> 一家软件公司需要确保用户上传的文档安全存储在 Amazon S3 中。文档必须在 Amazon S3 中进行静态加密。公司不想在内部管理安全基础设施，但由于行业规定，公司仍然需要额外的保护以确保对其加密密钥的控制。开发人员应使用哪种加密策略来满足这些要求？

- [ ] Server-side encryption with Amazon S3 managed keys (SSE-S3). `使用 Amazon S3 管理密钥的服务器端加密 (SSE-S3)。`
- [ ] Server-side encryption with customer-provided encryption keys (SSE-C). `使用客户提供的加密密钥的服务器端加密 (SSE-C)。`
- [x] Server-side encryption with AWS KMS managed keys (SSE-KMS). `使用 AWS KMS 管理密钥的服务器端加密 (SSE-KMS)。`
- [ ] Client-side encryption. `客户端加密。`

### An application uses Amazon Kinesis Data Streams to ingest and process large streams of data records in real time. Amazon EC2 instances consume and process the data from the shards of the Kinesis data stream by using Amazon Kinesis Client Library (KCL). The application handles the failure scenarios and does not require standby workers. The application reports that a specific shard is receiving more data than expected. To adapt to the changes in the rate of data flow, the 'hot' shard is resharded. Assuming that the initial number of shards in the Kinesis data stream is 4, and after resharding the number of shards increased to 6, what is the maximum number of EC2 instances that can be deployed to process data from all the shards?
> 一个应用程序使用 Amazon Kinesis Data Streams 实时摄取和处理大量数据记录。Amazon EC2 实例使用 Amazon Kinesis Client Library (KCL) 从 Kinesis 数据流的分片中消费并处理数据。该应用程序处理故障场景，并且不需要备用工作程序。应用程序报告某个特定分片接收到的数据超过预期。为了适应数据流速率的变化，对“热点”分片进行了重新分片。假设 Kinesis 数据流中的初始分片数为 4，重新分片后分片数增加到 6，最多可以部署多少个 EC2 实例来处理所有分片的数据？

- [ ] 12.
- [x] 6. 
- [ ] 4. 
- [ ] 1.

### A Developer is making changes to a custom application that is currently using AWS Elastic Beanstalk. After the Developer completes the changes, what solutions will update the Elastic Beanstalk environment with the new application version? (Choose TWO)
> 开发人员正在对当前使用 AWS Elastic Beanstalk 的自定义应用程序进行更改。开发人员完成更改后，哪些解决方案可以使用新应用程序版本更新 Elastic Beanstalk 环境？（选择两个）

- [x] Package the application code into a .zip file, and upload, then deploy the packaged application from the AWS Management Console. `将应用程序代码打包成 .zip 文件，上传，然后从 AWS 管理控制台部署打包的应用程序。`
- [ ] Package the application code into a .tar file, create a new application version from the AWS Management Console, then update the environment by using AWS CLI. `将应用程序代码打包成 .tar 文件，从 AWS 管理控制台创建一个新的应用程序版本，然后使用 AWS CLI 更新环境。`
- [ ] Package the application code into a .tar file, and upload and deploy the packaged application from the AWS Management Console. `将应用程序代码打包成 .tar 文件，然后从 AWS 管理控制台上传并部署打包的应用程序。`
- [x] Package the application code into a .zip file, create a new application version from the packaged application by using AWS CLI, then update the environment by using AWS CLI. `将应用程序代码打包成 .zip 文件，使用 AWS CLI 从打包的应用程序创建一个新版本，然后使用 AWS CLI 更新环境。`
- [ ] Package the application code into a .zip file, create a new application version from the AWS Management Console, then rebuild the environment by using AWS CLI. `将应用程序代码打包成 .zip 文件，从 AWS 管理控制台创建一个新应用程序版本，然后使用 AWS CLI 重建环境。`

### A company is running an application built on AWS Lambda functions. One Lambda function has performance issues when it has to download a 50MB file from the Internet in every execution. This function is called multiple times a second. What solution would give the BEST performance increase?
> 一家公司正在运行一个基于 AWS Lambda 函数构建的应用程序。一个 Lambda 函数在每次执行时都需要从 Internet 下载一个 50MB 的文件，导致性能问题。该函数每秒被多次调用。哪种解决方案可以提供最佳的性能提升？

- [x] Cache the file in the /tmp directory. `将文件缓存在 /tmp 目录中。`
- [ ] Increase the Lambda maximum execution time. `增加 Lambda 的最大执行时间。`
- [ ] Put an Elastic Load Balancer in front of the Lambda function. `在 Lambda 函数前放置一个弹性负载均衡器。`
- [ ] Cache the file in Amazon S3. `将文件缓存在 Amazon S3 中。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### Queries to an Amazon DynamoDB table are consuming a large amount of read capacity. The table has a significant number of large attributes. The application does not need all of the attribute data. How can DynamoDB costs be minimized while maximizing application performance?
> 对 Amazon DynamoDB 表的查询消耗了大量读取容量。该表包含大量的属性，而应用程序不需要所有的属性数据。如何在最大化应用程序性能的同时，最小化 DynamoDB 成本？

- [ ] Batch all the writes, and perform the write operations when no or few reads are being performed. `批量执行所有写入操作，并在没有或很少读取操作时执行写入操作。`
- [x] Create a global secondary index with a minimum set of projected attributes. `创建一个带有最少投影属性的全局二级索引。`
- [ ] Implement exponential backoffs in the application. `在应用程序中实现指数退避。`
- [ ] Load balance the reads to the table using an Application Load Balancer. `使用应用负载均衡器对表的读取操作进行负载均衡。`

### A Developer is writing a REST service that will add items to a shopping list. The service is built on Amazon API Gateway with AWS Lambda integrations. The shopping list items are sent as query string parameters in the method request. How should the Developer convert the query string parameters to arguments for the Lambda function?
> 开发人员正在编写一个 REST 服务，该服务将商品添加到购物清单中。该服务基于 Amazon API Gateway，集成了 AWS Lambda。购物清单项目作为查询字符串参数发送到方法请求中。开发人员应如何将查询字符串参数转换为 Lambda 函数的参数？

- [ ] Enable request validation. `启用请求验证。`
- [ ] Include the Amazon Resource Name (ARN) of the Lambda function. `包含 Lambda 函数的 Amazon 资源名称 (ARN)。`
- [ ] Change the integration type. `更改集成类型。`
- [x] Create a mapping template. `创建一个映射模板。`

### A development team is creating a new application designed to run on AWS. While the test and production environments will run on Amazon EC2 instances, developers will each run their own environment on their laptops. Which of the following is the simplest and MOST secure way to access AWS services from the local development machines?
> 开发团队正在创建一个设计为在 AWS 上运行的新应用程序。虽然测试和生产环境将在 Amazon EC2 实例上运行，但每位开发人员将在他们的笔记本电脑上运行自己的环境。以下哪种方式是从本地开发机器访问 AWS 服务的最简单且最安全的方式？

- [ ] Use an IAM role to assume a role and execute API calls using the role. `使用 IAM 角色来承担角色，并使用该角色执行 API 调用。`
- [x] Create an IAM user to be shared with the entire development team, provide the development team with the access key. `为整个开发团队创建一个 IAM 用户，并为开发团队提供访问密钥。`
- [ ] Create an IAM user for each developer on the team: provide each developer with a unique access key. `为团队中的每个开发人员创建一个 IAM 用户：为每个开发人员提供唯一的访问密钥。`
- [ ] Set up a federation through an Amazon Cognito user pool. `通过 Amazon Cognito 用户池设置联合身份验证。`

### How is provisioned throughput affected by the chosen consistency model when reading data from a DynamoDB table?
> 在从 DynamoDB 表中读取数据时，所选一致性模型如何影响预配置的吞吐量？

- [ ] Strongly consistent reads use the same amount of throughput as eventually consistent reads. `强一致性读取使用与最终一致性读取相同的吞吐量。`
- [x] Strongly consistent reads use more throughput than eventually consistent reads. `强一致性读取使用的吞吐量比最终一致性读取多。`
- [ ] Strongly consistent reads use less throughput than eventually consistent reads. `强一致性读取使用的吞吐量少于最终一致性读取。`
- [ ] Strongly consistent reads use variable throughput depending on read activity. `强一致性读取使用的吞吐量取决于读取活动，具有可变性。`

The users are allowed to update their names only if a user is authenticated by web identity federation. Which set of conditions should be added in the policy attached to the role for the DynamoDB: PutItem API call?

### A developer wants the ability to roll back to a previous version of an AWS Lambda function in the event of errors caused by a new deployment. How can the developer achieve this with MINIMAL impact on users?
> 开发人员希望能够在新部署导致错误的情况下回滚到 AWS Lambda 函数的先前版本。开发人员如何以对用户影响最小的方式实现这一目标？

- [ ] Change the application to use an alias that points to the current version. Deploy the new version of the code. Update the alias to use the newly deployed version. If too many errors are encountered, point the alias back to the previous version. `更改应用程序以使用指向当前版本的别名。部署新版本的代码。更新别名以使用新部署的版本。如果遇到过多错误，将别名指向先前版本。`
- [x] Change the application to use an alias that points to the current version. Deploy the new version of the code. Update the alias to direct 10% of users to the newly deployed version. If too many errors are encountered, send 100% of traffic to the previous version. `更改应用程序以使用指向当前版本的别名。部署新版本的代码。更新别名，将 10% 的用户指向新部署的版本。如果遇到过多错误，将 100% 的流量发送到先前版本。`
- [ ] Do not make any changes to the application Deploy the new version of the code. If too many errors are encountered, point the application back to the previous version using the version number in the Amazon Resource Name (ARN). `不对应用程序进行任何更改，部署新版本的代码。如果遇到过多错误，使用 Amazon 资源名称 (ARN) 中的版本号将应用程序指回先前版本。`
- [ ] Create three aliases: new, existing, and router. Point the existing alias to the current version. Have the router alias direct 100% of users to the existing alias. Update the application to use the router alias. Deploy the new version of the code. Point the new alias to this version. Update the router alias to direct 10% of users to the new alias. If too many errors are encountered, send 100% of traffic to the existing alias. `创建三个别名：新、现有和路由。将现有别名指向当前版本。让路由别名将 100% 的用户指向现有别名。更新应用程序以使用路由别名。部署新版本的代码。将新别名指向此版本。更新路由别名，将 10% 的用户指向新别名。如果遇到过多错误，将 100% 的流量发送到现有别名。`

### An application contains two components: one component to handle HTTP requests, and another component to handle background processing tasks. Each component must scale independently. The developer wants to deploy this application using AWS Elastic Beanstalk. How should this application be deployed, based on these requirements?
> 一个应用程序包含两个组件：一个组件处理 HTTP 请求，另一个组件处理后台处理任务。每个组件必须独立扩展。开发人员希望使用 AWS Elastic Beanstalk 部署此应用程序。根据这些要求，应该如何部署该应用程序？

- [ ] Deploy the application in a single Elastic Beanstalk environment. `在单个 Elastic Beanstalk 环境中部署应用程序。`
- [x] Deploy each component in a separate Elastic Beanstalk environment. `在单独的 Elastic Beanstalk 环境中部署每个组件。`
- [ ] Use multiple Elastic Beanstalk environments for the HTTP component but one environment for the background task component. `对 HTTP 组件使用多个 Elastic Beanstalk 环境，但对后台任务组件使用一个环境。`
- [ ] Use multiple Elastic Beanstalk environments for the background task component but one environment for the HTTP component. `对后台任务组件使用多个 Elastic Beanstalk 环境，但对 HTTP 组件使用一个环境。`

### A company is using AWS CloudFormation templates to deploy AWS resources. The company needs to update one of its AWS CloudFormation stacks. What can the company do to find out how the changes will impact the resources that are running?
> 一家公司正在使用 AWS CloudFormation 模板来部署 AWS 资源。该公司需要更新其 AWS CloudFormation 堆栈之一。公司可以采取什么措施来了解更改将如何影响正在运行的资源？

- [x] Investigate the change sets. `调查变更集。`
- [ ] Investigate the stack policies. `调查堆栈策略。`
- [ ] Investigate the Metadata section. `调查元数据部分。`
- [ ] Investigate the Resources section. `调查资源部分。`

### A developer is creating a serverless web application and maintains different branches of code. The developer wants to avoid updating the Amazon API Gateway target endpoint each time a new code push is performed. What solution would allow the developer to perform a code push efficiently, without the need to update the API Gateway?
> 开发人员正在创建一个无服务器 Web 应用程序，并维护不同的代码分支。开发人员希望避免在每次代码推送时更新 Amazon API Gateway 目标端点。什么解决方案可以让开发人员高效地进行代码推送，而无需更新 API Gateway？

- [ ] Associate different AWS Lambda functions to an API Gateway target endpoint. `将不同的 AWS Lambda 函数关联到 API Gateway 目标端点。`
- [ ] Create different stages in API Gateway, then associate API Gateway with AWS Lambda. `在 API Gateway 中创建不同的阶段，然后将 API Gateway 与 AWS Lambda 关联。`
- [x] Create aliases and versions in AWS Lambda. `在 AWS Lambda 中创建别名和版本。`
- [ ] Tag the AWS Lambda functions with different names. `使用不同名称标记 AWS Lambda 函数。`

### An application running on EC2 instances is storing data in an S3 bucket. Security policy mandates that all data must be encrypted in transit. How can the Developer ensure that all traffic to the S3 bucket is encrypted?
> 运行在 EC2 实例上的应用程序正在将数据存储在 S3 存储桶中。安全策略规定，所有数据在传输过程中必须加密。开发人员如何确保所有流量到 S3 存储桶都被加密？

- [ ] Install certificates on the EC2 instances. `在 EC2 实例上安装证书。`
- [x] Create a bucket policy that allows traffic where SecureTransport is true. `创建一个桶策略，允许 SecureTransport 为 true 的流量。`
- [ ] Create an HTTPS redirect on the EC2 instances. `在 EC2 实例上创建 HTTPS 重定向。`
- [ ] Create a bucket policy that denies traffic where SecureTransport is false. `创建一个桶策略，拒绝 SecureTransport 为 false 的流量。`

- [x] the /tmp directory.

### A website's page load times are gradually increasing as more users access the system at the same time. Analysis indicates that a user profile is being loaded from a database in all the web pages being visited by each user and this is increasing the database load and the page load latency. To address this issue the Developer decides to cache the user profile data. Which caching strategy will address this situation MOST efficiently?
> 随着更多用户同时访问系统，网站页面加载时间逐渐增加。分析表明，用户个人资料在每个用户访问的所有网页中都从数据库加载，这增加了数据库负载和页面加载延迟。为了解决这个问题，开发人员决定缓存用户个人资料数据。哪种缓存策略最有效地解决此情况？

- [ ] Create a new Amazon EC2 Instance and run a NoSQL database on it. Cache the profile data within this database using the write-through caching strategy. `创建一个新的 Amazon EC2 实例并在其上运行 NoSQL 数据库。使用写入透传缓存策略在此数据库中缓存个人资料数据。`
- [x] Create an Amazon ElastiCache cluster to cache the user profile data. Use a cache-aside caching strategy. `创建一个 Amazon ElastiCache 集群来缓存用户个人资料数据。使用旁路缓存策略。`
- [ ] Use a dedicated Amazon RDS instance for caching profile data. Use a write-through caching strategy. `使用专用的 Amazon RDS 实例缓存个人资料数据。使用写入透传缓存策略。`
- [ ] Create an ElastiCache cluster to cache the user profile data. Use a write-through caching strategy. `创建一个 ElastiCache 集群来缓存用户个人资料数据。使用写入透传缓存策略。`

### An advertising company has a dynamic website with heavy traffic. The company wants to migrate the website infrastructure to AWS to handle everything except website development. Which solution BEST meets these requirements?
> 一家广告公司拥有一个流量很大的动态网站。该公司希望将网站基础设施迁移到 AWS，以处理除网站开发之外的所有内容。哪种解决方案最符合这些要求？

- [ ] Use AWS VM Import to migrate a web server image to AWS Launch the image on a compute-optimized Amazon EC2 instance. `使用 AWS VM 导入将 web 服务器镜像迁移到 AWS，在计算优化的 Amazon EC2 实例上启动该镜像。`
- [ ] Launch multiple Amazon Lightsail instance behind a load balancer. Set up the website on those instances. `在负载均衡器后启动多个 Amazon Lightsail 实例。在这些实例上设置网站。`
- [x] Deploy the website code in an AWS Elastic Beanstalk environment. Use Auto Scaling to scale the numbers of instance. `将网站代码部署到 AWS Elastic Beanstalk 环境中。使用自动扩展来扩展实例数量。`
- [ ] Use Amazon S3 to host the website. Use Amazon CloudFront to deliver the content at scale. `使用 Amazon S3 托管网站。使用 Amazon CloudFront 按需交付内容。`

### A developer is writing an AWS Lambda function. The developer wants to log key events that occur during the Lambda function and include a unique identifier to associate the events with a specific function invocation. Which of the following will help the developer accomplish this objective?
> 一名开发人员正在编写一个 AWS Lambda 函数。开发人员希望记录在 Lambda 函数执行期间发生的关键事件，并包括一个唯一标识符以将这些事件与特定的函数调用关联起来。以下哪项将帮助开发人员实现这个目标？

- [x] Obtain the request identifier from the Lambda context object. Architect the application to write logs to the console. `从 Lambda 上下文对象中获取请求标识符。设计应用程序以将日志写入控制台。`

- [ ] Obtain the request identifier from the Lambda event object. Architect the application to write logs to the console. `从 Lambda 事件对象中获取请求标识符。设计应用程序以将日志写入控制台。`
- [ ] Obtain the request identifier from the Lambda context object. Architect the application to write logs to a file. `从 Lambda 上下文对象中获取请求标识符。设计应用程序以将日志写入文件。`

### A company stores all personally identifiable information (PII) in an Amazon DynamoDB table named PII in Account A. An application running on Amazon EC2 instances in Account B requires access to the PII table. An administrators in Account A created an IAM role named AccessPII with privileges to access the PII table, and made account B a trusted entity. Which combination of actional steps should Developers take to access the table? (Select TWO)
> 一家公司在 A 账户中的 Amazon DynamoDB 表 PII 中存储所有个人可识别信息 (PII)。在 B 账户中的 Amazon EC2 实例上运行的应用程序需要访问 PII 表。A 账户中的管理员创建了一个名为 AccessPII 的 IAM 角色，拥有访问 PII 表的权限，并将 B 账户设置为受信实体。开发人员应采取哪些组合步骤来访问该表？（选择两个）

- [x] Allow the EC2 IAM role the permission to assume the AccessPII role. `允许 EC2 IAM 角色有权限假设 AccessPII 角色。`
- [ ] Allow the EC2 IAM role the permission to access the PII table. `允许 EC2 IAM 角色有权限访问 PII 表。`
- [ ] Include the AWS API in the application code logic to obtain temporary credentials from the EC2 IAM role to access the PII table. `在应用程序代码逻辑中包含 AWS API，以从 EC2 IAM 角色获取临时凭证以访问 PII 表。`
- [x] Include the AssumeRole API operation in the application code logic to obtain temporary credentials to access the PII table. `在应用程序代码逻辑中包含 AssumeRole API 操作，以获取临时凭证以访问 PII 表。`
- [ ] Include the GetSessionToken API operation in the application code logic to obtain temporary credentials to access the PII table. `在应用程序代码逻辑中包含 GetSessionToken API 操作，以获取临时凭证以访问 PII 表。`

### An AWS Lambda function accesses two Amazon DynamoDB tables. A developer wants to improve the performance of the Lambda function by identifying bottlenecks in the function. How can the developer inspect the timing of the DynamoDB API calls?
> 一个 AWS Lambda 函数访问两个 Amazon DynamoDB 表。开发人员希望通过识别函数中的瓶颈来提高 Lambda 函数的性能。开发人员如何检查 DynamoDB API 调用的时间？

- [ ] Add DynamoDB as an event source to the Lambda function. View the performance with Amazon CloudWatch metrics. `将 DynamoDB 添加为 Lambda 函数的事件源。通过 Amazon CloudWatch 指标查看性能。`
- [ ] Place an Application Load Balancer (ALB) in front of the two DynamoDB tables. Inspect the ALB logs. `在两个 DynamoDB 表前放置一个应用程序负载均衡器 (ALB)。检查 ALB 日志。`
- [ ] Limit Lambda to no more than five concurrent invocations. Monitor from the Lambda console. `将 Lambda 的并发调用限制为不超过五次。通过 Lambda 控制台进行监控。`
- [x] Enable AWS X-Ray tracing for the function. View the traces from the X-Ray service. `为该函数启用 AWS X-Ray 跟踪。从 X-Ray 服务查看跟踪记录。`

### An Amazon RDS database instance is used by many applications to look up historical data. The query rate is relatively constant. When the historical data is updated each day, the resulting write traffic slows the read query performance and affects all application users. What can be done to eliminate the performance impact on application users?
> 一个 Amazon RDS 数据库实例被许多应用程序用于查找历史数据。查询速率相对稳定。当历史数据每天更新时，导致的写入流量减慢了读取查询性能，并影响所有应用程序用户。可以采取什么措施消除对应用程序用户的性能影响？

- [ ] Make sure Amazon RDS is Multi-AZ so it can better absorb increased traffic. `确保 Amazon RDS 是 Multi-AZ，以便更好地吸收增加的流量。`
- [x] Create an RDS Read Replica and direct all read traffic to the replica. `创建一个 RDS 只读副本，并将所有读取流量定向到该副本。`
- [ ] Implement Amazon ElastiCache in front of Amazon RDS to buffer the write traffic. `在 Amazon RDS 前面实施 Amazon ElastiCache 以缓冲写入流量。`
- [ ] Use Amazon DynamoDB instead of Amazon RDS to buffer the read traffic. `使用 Amazon DynamoDB 替代 Amazon RDS 以缓冲读取流量。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A company is developing a serverless ecommerce web application. The application needs to make coordinated, all-or-nothing changes to multiple items in the company's inventory table in Amazon DynamoDB. Which solution will meet these requirements?
> 一家公司正在开发一个无服务器的电子商务网页应用程序。该应用程序需要对公司在 Amazon DynamoDB 中的库存表中的多个项目进行协调的、全或无的更改。哪种解决方案可以满足这些要求？

- [ ] Enable transactions for the DynamoDB table. Use the BatchWriteItem operation to update the items. `为 DynamoDB 表启用事务。使用 BatchWriteItem 操作来更新项目。`
- [x] Use the TransactWriteItems operation to group the changes. Update the items in the table. `使用 TransactWriteItems 操作来分组更改。更新表中的项目。`
- [ ] Set up a FIFO queue using Amazon SQS. Group the changes in the queue. Update the table based on the grouped changes. `使用 Amazon SQS 设置 FIFO 队列。将更改分组到队列中。根据分组更改更新表。`
- [ ] Create a transaction table in an Amazon Aurora DB cluster to manage the transactions. Write a backend process to sync the Aurora DB table and the DynamoDB table. `在 Amazon Aurora 数据库集群中创建一个事务表以管理事务。编写后端进程以同步 Aurora 数据库表和 DynamoDB 表。`

### An application is running on an EC2 instance. The Developer wants to store an application metric in Amazon CloudWatch. What is the best practice for implementing this requirement?
> 一个应用程序正在 EC2 实例上运行。开发人员希望将应用程序指标存储在 Amazon CloudWatch 中。实现该要求的最佳实践是什么？

- [ ] Use the PUT Object API call to send data to an S3 bucket. Use an event notification to invoke a Lambda function to publish data to CloudWatch. `使用 PUT Object API 调用将数据发送到 S3 存储桶。使用事件通知调用 Lambda 函数将数据发布到 CloudWatch。`
- [ ] Publish the metric data to an Amazon Kinesis Stream using a PutRecord API call. Subscribe a Lambda function that publishes data to CloudWatch. `使用 PutRecord API 调用将指标数据发布到 Amazon Kinesis 流。订阅一个发布数据到 CloudWatch 的 Lambda 函数。`
- [ ] Use the CloudWatch PutMetricData API call to submit a custom metric to CloudWatch. Provide the required credentials to enable the API call. `使用 CloudWatch PutMetricData API 调用将自定义指标提交到 CloudWatch。提供所需的凭证以启用 API 调用。`
- [x] Use the CloudWatch PutMetricData API call to submit a custom metric to CloudWatch. Launch the EC2 instance with the required IAM role to enable the API call. `使用 CloudWatch PutMetricData API 调用将自定义指标提交到 CloudWatch。以所需的 IAM 角色启动 EC2 实例以启用 API 调用。`

### A Developer needs to design an application running on AWS that will be used to consume Amazon SQS messages that range from 1 KB up to 1GB in size. How should the Amazon SQS messages be managed?

### A developer has written a multi-threaded application that is running on a fleet of Amazon EC2 instances. The operations team has requested a graphical method to monitor the number of running threads over time. What is the MOST efficient way to fulfill this request?
> 开发人员编写了一个多线程应用程序，该应用程序正在一组 Amazon EC2 实例上运行。运维团队请求一种图形化的方法来监控运行线程的数量。满足此请求的最有效方法是什么？

- [ ] Periodically send the thread count to AWS X-Ray segments, then generate a service graph on demand. `定期将线程计数发送到 AWS X-Ray 段，然后按需生成服务图。`
- [x] Create a custom Amazon CloudWatch metric and periodically perform a PutMetricData call with the current thread count. `创建自定义的 Amazon CloudWatch 指标，并定期使用当前线程计数执行 PutMetricData 调用。`
- [ ] Periodically log thread count data to Amazon S3. Use Amazon Kinesis to process the data into a graph. `定期将线程计数数据记录到 Amazon S3。使用 Amazon Kinesis 处理数据生成图形。`
- [ ] Periodically write the current thread count to a table using Amazon DynamoDB and use Amazon CloudFront to create a graph. `定期使用 Amazon DynamoDB 将当前线程计数写入表，并使用 Amazon CloudFront 创建图形。`

### A company has written a Java AWS Lambda function to be triggered whenever a user uploads an image to an Amazon S3 bucket. The function converts the original image to several different formats and then copies the resulting images to another Amazon S3 bucket. The Developers find that no images are being copied to the second Amazon S3 bucket. They have tested the code on an Amazon EC2 instance with 1GB of RAM, and it takes an average of 500 seconds to complete. What is the MOST likely cause of the problem?
> 一家公司编写了一个 Java AWS Lambda 函数，以便在用户上传图像到 Amazon S3 存储桶时触发。该函数将原始图像转换为几种不同格式，然后将生成的图像复制到另一个 Amazon S3 存储桶。开发人员发现没有图像被复制到第二个 Amazon S3 存储桶。他们在一台具有 1GB 内存的 Amazon EC2 实例上测试了代码，平均需要 500 秒才能完成。问题最可能的原因是什么？

- [ ] The Lambda function has insufficient memory and needs to be increased to 1 GB to match the Amazon EC2 instance. `Lambda 函数的内存不足，需要增加到 1GB，以匹配 Amazon EC2 实例。`
- [ ] Files need to be copied to the same Amazon S3 bucket for processing, so the second bucket needs to be deleted. `文件需要复制到同一个 Amazon S3 存储桶进行处理，因此需要删除第二个存储桶。`
- [x] Lambda functions have a maximum execution limit of 15 minutes, therefore the function is not completing. `Lambda 函数的最大执行限制为 15 分钟，因此该函数没有完成。`
- [ ] There is a problem with the Java runtime for Lambda, and the function needs to be converted to node.js. `Lambda 的 Java 运行时存在问题，需要将函数转换为 Node.js。`

### A web application is using Amazon Kinesis Streams for clickstream data that may not be consumed for up to 12 hours. How can the Developer implement encryption at rest for data within the Kinesis Streams?
> 一个网络应用程序正在使用 Amazon Kinesis Streams 处理点击流数据，这些数据可能在长达 12 小时内未被消费。开发人员如何在 Kinesis Streams 中实现静态数据加密？

- [ ] Enable SSL connections to Kinesis. `启用对 Kinesis 的 SSL 连接。`
- [ ] Use Amazon Kinesis Consumer Library. `使用 Amazon Kinesis 消费者库。`
- [ ] Encrypt the data once it is at rest with a Lambda function. `使用 Lambda 函数对静态数据进行加密。`
- [x] Enable server-side encryption in Kinesis Streams. `在 Kinesis Streams 中启用服务器端加密。`

### A Developer is creating a mobile application with a limited budget. Which AWS service should be used to meet these requirements?

- [ ] AWS Lambda. 
- [x] Amazon Cognito. 
- [ ] AWS IAM. 
- [ ] Amazon EC2.

### A company wants to migrate its web application to AWS and leverage Auto Scaling to handle peak workloads. The Solutions Architect determined that the best metric for an Auto Scaling event is the number of concurrent users. Based on this information, what should the Developer use to autoscale based on concurrent users?
> 一家公司希望将其Web应用程序迁移到AWS，并利用自动扩展来处理峰值工作负载。解决方案架构师确定，自动扩展事件的最佳指标是并发用户的数量。基于此信息，开发人员应使用什么来根据并发用户进行自动扩展？

- [ ] An Amazon SNS topic to be triggered when a concurrent user threshold is met. `当达到并发用户阈值时触发的Amazon SNS主题。`
- [ ] An Amazon Cloudwatch NetworkIn metric. `Amazon Cloudwatch的NetworkIn指标。`
- [ ] Amazon CloudFront to leverage AWS Edge Locations. `使用Amazon CloudFront利用AWS边缘位置。`
- [x] A Custom Amazon CloudWatch metric for concurrent users. `用于并发用户的自定义Amazon CloudWatch指标。`

### A Developer has written a serverless application using multiple AWS services. The business logic is written as a Lambda function which has dependencies on third-party libraries. The Lambda function endpoints will be exposed using Amazon API Gateway. The Lambda function will write the information to Amazon DynamoDB. The Developer is ready to deploy the application but must have the ability to rollback. How can this deployment be automated, based on these requirements?
> 开发人员使用多个AWS服务编写了一个无服务器应用程序。业务逻辑写成一个Lambda函数，并依赖第三方库。Lambda函数的端点将通过Amazon API Gateway公开。Lambda函数将信息写入Amazon DynamoDB。开发人员准备部署应用程序，但必须能够回滚。基于这些要求，如何自动化此部署？

- [ ] Deploy using Amazon Lambda API operations to create the Lambda function by providing a deployment package. `使用Amazon Lambda API操作，通过提供部署包来创建Lambda函数。`
- [ ] Use an AWS CloudFormation template and use CloudFormation syntax to define the Lambda function resource in the template. `使用AWS CloudFormation模板，并使用CloudFormation语法在模板中定义Lambda函数资源。`
- [x] Use syntax conforming to the Serverless Application Model in the AWS CloudFormation template to define the Lambda function resource. `在AWS CloudFormation模板中使用符合无服务器应用程序模型的语法来定义Lambda函数资源。`
- [ ] Create a bash script which uses AWS CLI to package and deploy the application. `创建一个使用AWS CLI打包和部署应用程序的bash脚本。`

### A game stores user game data in an Amazon DynamoDB table. Individual users should not have access to other users' game data. How can this be accomplished?
> 一款游戏将用户游戏数据存储在Amazon DynamoDB表中。单个用户不应访问其他用户的游戏数据。如何实现这一点？

- [ ] Encrypt the game data with individual user keys. `使用单独的用户密钥加密游戏数据。`
- [x] Restrict access to specific items based on certain primary key values. `根据特定的主键值限制对特定项的访问。`
- [ ] Stage data in SQS queues to inject metadata before accessing DynamoDB. `将数据放置在SQS队列中，以在访问DynamoDB之前注入元数据。`
- [ ] Read records from DynamoDB and discard irrelevant data client-side. `从DynamoDB读取记录并在客户端丢弃不相关的数据。`

### A Developer is creating a web application that requires authentication, but also needs to support guest access to provide users limited access without having to authenticate. What service can provide support for the application to allow guest access?
> 开发人员正在创建一个需要身份验证的Web应用程序，但还需要支持访客访问，以便用户在不进行身份验证的情况下获得有限的访问权限。哪个服务可以支持该应用程序以允许访客访问？

- [ ] IAM temporary credentials using AWS STS. `使用AWS STS的IAM临时凭证。`
- [ ] Amazon Directory Service. `Amazon目录服务。`
- [x] Amazon Cognito with unauthenticated access enabled. `启用匿名访问的Amazon Cognito。`
- [ ] IAM with SAML integration. `与SAML集成的IAM。`

### Given the source code for an AWS Lambda function in the local store.py containing a handler function called get_store and the following AWS CloudFormation template. What should be done to prepare the template so that it can be deployed using the AWS CLI command aws cloudformation deploy?
> 给定本地的store.py中的AWS Lambda函数源代码，其中包含名为get_store的处理程序函数，以及以下AWS CloudFormation模板。应该如何准备模板，以便使用AWS CLI命令aws cloudformation deploy进行部署？

![Question 59](images/question59.jpg)

- [ ] Use AWS CloudFormation compile to base64 encode and embed the source file into a modified CloudFormation template. `使用AWS CloudFormation compile进行base64编码并将源文件嵌入到修改后的CloudFormation模板中。`
- [x] Use AWS CloudFormation package to upload the source code to an Amazon S3 bucket and produce a modified CloudFormation template. `使用AWS CloudFormation package将源代码上传到Amazon S3桶并生成修改后的CloudFormation模板。`
- [ ] Use AWS Lambda zip to package the source file together with the CloudFormation template and deploy the resulting zip archive. `使用AWS Lambda zip将源文件与CloudFormation模板打包在一起，并部署生成的zip档案。`
- [ ] Use AWS Serverless create-package to embed the source file directly into the existing CloudFormation template. `使用AWS Serverless create-package将源文件直接嵌入到现有的CloudFormation模板中。`

### A Developer has created a large Lambda function, and deployment is failing with the following error:ClientError: An error occurred (InvalidParameterValueException) when calling the CreateFunction operation: Unzipped size must be smaller than XXXXXXXXX bytes', where XXXXXXXXX is the current Lambda limit. What can the Developer do to fix this problem?
> 一名开发者创建了一个较大的Lambda函数，部署失败并出现以下错误：ClientError：在调用CreateFunction操作时发生错误（InvalidParameterValueException）：解压缩后的大小必须小于XXXXXXXXX字节，其中XXXXXXXXX是当前Lambda限制。开发者可以做什么来解决这个问题？

- [ ] Submit a limit increase request to AWS Support to increase the function to the size needed. `向AWS支持提交限制增加请求，以增加函数到所需的大小。`
- [ ] Use a compression algorithm that is more efficient than ZIP. `使用比ZIP更高效的压缩算法。`
- [x] Break the function into multiple smaller Lambda functions. `将函数拆分为多个较小的Lambda函数。`
- [ ] ZIP the ZIP file twice to compress it further. `将ZIP文件进行双重压缩以进一步压缩。`

### A serverless application uses an API Gateway and AWS Lambda. Where should the Lambda function store its session information across function calls?
> 一个无服务器应用程序使用API Gateway和AWS Lambda。Lambda函数应在何处存储其跨函数调用的会话信息？

- [x] In an Amazon DynamoDB table. `在Amazon DynamoDB表中。`

- [ ] In the local filesystem. `在本地文件系统中。`

### An application reads data from an Amazon DynamoDB table. Several times a day, for a period of 15 seconds, the application receives multiple ProvisionedThroughputExceeded errors. How should this exception be handled?
> 一个应用程序从Amazon DynamoDB表中读取数据。每天有几次，在15秒的时间内，应用程序会收到多个ProvisionedThroughputExceeded错误。该异常应如何处理？

- [ ] Create a new global secondary index for the table to help with the additional requests. `为表创建一个新的全局二级索引以帮助处理额外的请求。`
- [x] Retry the failed read requests with exponential backoff. `使用指数退避法重试失败的读取请求。`
- [ ] Immediately retry the failed read requests. `立即重试失败的读取请求。`
- [ ] Use the DynamoDB 'UpdateItem' API to increase the provisioned throughput capacity of the table. `使用DynamoDB的'UpdateItem' API来增加表的预配置吞吐量。`

### A Developer is writing a Linux-based application to run on AWS Elastic Beanstalk. Application requirements state that the application must maintain full capacity during updates while minimizing cost. > 开发人员正在编写一个基于Linux的应用程序，以在AWS Elastic Beanstalk上运行。应用程序的要求是，在更新期间必须保持全容量，同时最小化成本。开发人员应该为环境指定哪种类型的Elastic Beanstalk部署策略？

- [ ] Immutable. `不可变。`
- [ ] Rolling. `滚动。`
- [ ] All at Once. `一次性。`
- [x] Rolling with additional batch. `带额外批次的滚动。`

### When writing a Lambda function, what is the benefit of instantiating AWS clients outside the scope of the handler?
> 在编写Lambda函数时，在处理程序的范围外实例化AWS客户端的好处是什么？

- [ ] Legibility and stylistic convention. `可读性和风格规范。`
- [x] Taking advantage of connection re-use. `利用连接重用。`
- [ ] Better error handling. `更好的错误处理。`
- [ ] Creating a new instance per invocation. `每次调用创建一个新实例。`

### A company is developing a new online game that will run on top of Amazon ECS. Four distinct Amazon ECS services will be part of the architecture, each requiring specific permissions to various AWS services. The company wants to optimize the use of the underlying Amazon EC2 instances by bin packing the containers based on memory reservation. Which configuration would allow the Development team to meet these requirements MOST securely?
> 一家公司正在开发一款新的在线游戏，该游戏将在Amazon ECS上运行。四个不同的Amazon ECS服务将成为架构的一部分，每个服务都需要对各种AWS服务的特定权限。公司希望通过基于内存保留来优化底层Amazon EC2实例的使用，采用容器的紧凑打包。哪种配置可以使开发团队最安全地满足这些要求？

- [ ] Create a new Identity and Access Management (IAM) instance profile containing the required permissions for the various ECS services, then associate that instance role with the underlying EC2 instances. `创建一个新的身份与访问管理（IAM）实例配置文件，其中包含各个ECS服务所需的权限，然后将该实例角色与底层EC2实例关联。`
- [ ] Create four distinct IAM roles, each containing the required permissions for the associated ECS service, then configure each ECS service to reference the associated IAM role. `创建四个不同的IAM角色，每个角色包含与相关ECS服务所需的权限，然后配置每个ECS服务以引用相关的IAM角色。`
- [ ] Create four distinct IAM roles, each containing the required permissions for the associated ECS service, then, create an IAM group and configure the ECS cluster to reference that group. `创建四个不同的IAM角色，每个角色包含与相关ECS服务所需的权限，然后创建一个IAM组并配置ECS集群以引用该组。`
- [x] Create four distinct IAM roles, each containing the required permissions for the associated ECS service, then configure each ECS task definition to reference the associated IAM role. `创建四个不同的IAM角色，每个角色包含与相关ECS服务所需的权限，然后配置每个ECS任务定义以引用相关的IAM角色。`

### A Developer must re-implement the business logic for an order fulfilment system. The business logic has to make requests to multiple vendors to decide where to purchase an item. The whole process can take up to a week to complete. What is the MOST efficient and SIMPLEST way to implement a system that meets these requirements?
> 开发者必须重新实现订单履行系统的业务逻辑。业务逻辑需要向多个供应商发出请求，以决定在哪里购买商品。整个过程可能需要长达一周的时间来完成。实现满足这些要求的系统的最有效和最简单的方法是什么？

- [x] Use AWS Step Functions to execute parallel Lambda functions, and join the results. `使用AWS Step Functions并行执行Lambda函数，并合并结果。`
- [ ] Create an AWS SQS for each vendor, poll the queue from a worker instance, and joint the results. `为每个供应商创建一个AWS SQS，从工作实例轮询队列，并合并结果。`
- [ ] Use AWS Lambda to asynchronously call a Lambda function for each vendor, and join the results. `使用AWS Lambda异步调用每个供应商的Lambda函数，并合并结果。`
- [ ] Use Amazon CloudWatch Events to orchestrate the Lambda functions. `使用Amazon CloudWatch Events编排Lambda函数。`

### A Developer is receiving HTTP 400: ThrottlingException errors intermittently when calling the Amazon CloudWatch API. When a call fails, no data is retrieved. What best practice should first be applied to address this issue?
> 开发者在调用Amazon CloudWatch API时间歇性地收到HTTP 400: ThrottlingException错误。当调用失败时，没有数据被检索。应首先应用什么最佳实践来解决此问题？

- [ ] Contact AWS Support for a limit increase. `联系AWS支持以申请增加限制。`
- [ ] Use the AWS CLI to get the metrics. `使用AWS CLI获取指标。`
- [ ] Analyze the applications and remove the API call. `分析应用程序并删除API调用。`
- [x] Retry the call with exponential backoff. `使用指数退避重试调用。`

### An application is real-time processing millions of events that are received through an API. What service could be used to allow multiple consumers to process the data concurrently and MOST cost-effectively?
> 一个应用程序实时处理通过API接收的数百万个事件。可以使用什么服务允许多个消费者并发处理数据，并且是最具成本效益的？

- [ ] Amazon SNS with fanout to an SQS queue for each application. `为每个应用程序使用带有扇出功能的Amazon SNS到SQS队列。`
- [ ] Amazon SNS with fanout to an SQS FIFO (first-in, first-out) queue for each application. `为每个应用程序使用带有扇出功能的Amazon SNS到SQS FIFO（先进先出）队列。`
- [ ] Amazon Kinesis Firehouse. 
- [x] Amazon Kinesis Streams.

### A Developer is creating a Lambda function and will be using external libraries that are not included in the standard Lambda libraries. What action would minimize the Lambda compute time consumed?
> 开发人员正在创建一个Lambda函数，并将使用标准Lambda库中未包含的外部库。哪项操作可以最小化Lambda消耗的计算时间？

- [ ] Install the dependencies and external libraries at the beginning of the Lambda function. `在Lambda函数开始时安装依赖项和外部库。`
- [ ] Create a Lambda deployment package that includes the external libraries. `创建一个包含外部库的Lambda部署包。`
- [ ] Copy the external libraries to Amazon S3, and reference the external libraries to the S3 location. `将外部库复制到Amazon S3，并引用S3位置的外部库。`
- [x] Install the external libraries in Lambda to be available to all Lambda functions. `在Lambda中安装外部库，使其可供所有Lambda函数使用。`

### During non-peak hours, a Developer wants to minimize the execution time of a full Amazon DynamoDB table scan without affecting normal workloads. The workloads average half of the strongly consistent read capacity units during non-peak hours. How would the Developer optimize this scan?
> 在非高峰时段，开发人员希望在不影响正常工作负载的情况下最小化全Amazon DynamoDB表扫描的执行时间。在非高峰时段，工作负载平均使用一半的强一致性读取容量单位。开发人员将如何优化此扫描？

- [x] Use parallel scans while limiting the rate. `使用并行扫描，同时限制速率。`
- [ ] Use sequential scans. `使用顺序扫描。`
- [ ] Increase read capacity units during the scan operation. `在扫描操作期间增加读取容量单位。`
- [ ] Change consistency to eventually consistent during the scan operation. `在扫描操作期间将一致性更改为最终一致性。`

### A large e-commerce site is being designed to deliver static objects from Amazon S3. The Amazon S3 bucket will serve more than 300 GET requests per second. What should be done to optimize performance? (Choose TWO)
> 一个大型电子商务网站正在设计从Amazon S3交付静态对象。Amazon S3桶将每秒处理超过300个GET请求。应该采取哪些措施来优化性能？（选择两个）

- [x] Integrate Amazon CloudFront with Amazon S3. `将Amazon CloudFront与Amazon S3集成。`
- [x] Enable Amazon S3 cross-region replication. `启用Amazon S3跨区域复制。`
- [ ] Delete expired Amazon S3 server log files. `删除过期的Amazon S3服务器日志文件。`
- [ ] Configure Amazon S3 lifecycle rules. `配置Amazon S3生命周期规则。`
- [ ] Randomize Amazon S3 key name prefixes. `随机化Amazon S3键名称前缀。`

### A legacy service has an XML-based SOAP interface. The Developer wants to expose the functionality of the service to external clients with the Amazon API Gateway. Which technique will accomplish this?
> 一个遗留服务具有基于XML的SOAP接口。开发人员希望通过Amazon API Gateway向外部客户公开该服务的功能。哪种技术可以实现这一点？

- [x] Create a RESTful API with the API Gateway; transform the incoming JSON into a valid XML message for the SOAP interface using mapping templates. `使用API Gateway创建RESTful API；使用映射模板将传入的JSON转换为SOAP接口的有效XML消息。`
- [ ] Create a RESTful API with the API Gateway; pass the incoming JSON to the SOAP interface through an Application Load Balancer. `使用API Gateway创建RESTful API；通过应用程序负载均衡器将传入的JSON传递给SOAP接口。`
- [ ] Create a RESTful API with the API Gateway; pass the incoming XML to the SOAP interface through an Application Load Balancer. `使用API Gateway创建RESTful API；通过应用程序负载均衡器将传入的XML传递给SOAP接口。`
- [ ] Create a RESTful API with the API Gateway; transform the incoming XML into a valid message for the SOAP interface using mapping templates. `使用API Gateway创建RESTful API；使用映射模板将传入的XML转换为SOAP接口的有效消息。`

**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Developer has an application that can upload tens of thousands of objects per second to Amazon S3 in parallel within a single AWS account. As part of new requirements, data stored in S3 must use server side encryption with AWS KMS (SSE-KMS). After creating this change, performance of the application is slower. Which of the following is MOST likely the cause of the application latency?
> 开发人员有一个应用程序，可以在单个AWS帐户内以并行方式每秒上传数万对象。根据新要求，存储在S3中的数据必须使用AWS KMS的服务器端加密（SSE-KMS）。在进行此更改后，应用程序的性能变得较慢。以下哪个最有可能是导致应用程序延迟的原因？

- [ ] Amazon S3 throttles the rate at which uploaded objects can be encrypted using Customer Master Keys. `Amazon S3限制使用客户主密钥加密上传对象的速率。`
- [x] The AWS KMS API calls limit is less than needed to achieve the desired performance. `AWS KMS API调用限制低于实现所需性能所需的限制。`
- [ ] The client encryption of the objects is using a poor algorithm. `客户端对对象的加密使用了较差的算法。`
- [ ] KMS requires that an alias be used to create an independent display name that can be mapped to a CM. `KMS要求使用别名来创建一个独立的显示名称，可以映射到CM。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A customer wants to deploy its source code on an AWS Elastic Beanstalk environment. The customer needs to perform deployment with minimal outage and should only use existing instances to retain application access log. What deployment policy would satisfy these requirements?
> 客户希望在AWS Elastic Beanstalk环境中部署其源代码。客户需要以最小的停机时间进行部署，并且应该仅使用现有实例以保留应用程序访问日志。哪种部署策略可以满足这些要求？

- [x] Rolling. `滚动更新。`
- [ ] All at once. `一次性全部更新。`
- [ ] Rolling with an additional batch. `带有额外批次的滚动更新。`
- [ ] Immutable. `不可变更新。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Developer has setup an Amazon Kinesis Stream with 4 shards to ingest a maximum of 2500 records per second. A Lambda function has been configured to process these records. In which order will these records be processed?
> 开发人员已经设置了一个具有4个分片的Amazon Kinesis流，以每秒最大吞吐量2500条记录。已配置一个Lambda函数来处理这些记录。这些记录将以何种顺序进行处理？

- [ ] Lambda will receive each record in the reverse order it was placed into the stream following a LIFO (last-in, first-out) method. `Lambda将以LIFO（后进先出）方法接收每条记录，顺序为放入流中的反向顺序。`
- [ ] Lambda will receive each record in the exact order it was placed into the stream following a FIFO (first­-in, first-out) method. `Lambda将以FIFO（先进先出）方法接收每条记录，顺序为放入流中的精确顺序。`
- [x] Lambda will receive each record in the exact order it was placed into the shard following a FIFO (first-in, first-out) method. There is no guarantee of order across shards. `Lambda将按照FIFO（先进先出）方法接收每条记录，顺序为放入分片中的精确顺序。跨分片之间没有顺序保证。`
- [ ] The Developer can select FIFO, (first-in, first-out), LIFO (last-in, last-out), random, or request specific record using the getRecords API. `开发人员可以选择FIFO（先进先出）、LIFO（后进先出）、随机，或使用getRecords API请求特定记录。`

**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### An organization must store thousands of sensitive audio and video files in an Amazon S3 bucket. Organizational security policies require that all data written to this bucket be encrypted. How can compliance with this policy be ensured?
> 一家组织必须将数千个敏感的音频和视频文件存储在Amazon S3桶中。组织安全政策要求所有写入此桶的数据都必须加密。如何确保遵守该政策？

- [ ] Use AWS Lambda to send notifications to the security team if unencrypted objects are put in the bucket. `使用AWS Lambda向安全团队发送通知，如果未加密的对象被放入桶中。`
- [x] Configure an Amazon S3 bucket policy to prevent the upload of objects that do not contain the x-amz-server-side-encryption header. `配置Amazon S3桶策略，以防止上传不包含x-amz-server-side-encryption标头的对象。`
- [ ] Create an Amazon CloudWatch event rule to verify that all objects stored in the Amazon S3 bucket are encrypted. `创建Amazon CloudWatch事件规则，以验证存储在Amazon S3桶中的所有对象是否已加密。`
- [ ] Configure an Amazon S3 bucket policy to prevent the upload of objects that contain the x-amz-server-side-encryption header. `配置Amazon S3桶策略，以防止上传包含x-amz-server-side-encryption标头的对象。`

**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### An application is designed to use Amazon SQS to manage messages from many independent senders. Each sender's messages must be processed in the order they are received. Which SQS feature should be implemented by the Developer?
> 应用程序设计为使用Amazon SQS管理来自许多独立发送者的消息。每个发送者的消息必须按接收顺序处理。开发人员应该实现哪个SQS功能？

- [ ] Configure each sender with a unique MessageGroupId. `为每个发送者配置唯一的MessageGroupId。`
- [ ] Enable MessageDeduplicationIds on the SQS queue. `在SQS队列上启用MessageDeduplicationIds。`
- [x] Configure each message with unique MessageGroupIds. `为每条消息配置唯一的MessageGroupIds。`
- [ ] Enable ContentBasedDeduplication on the SQS queue. `在SQS队列上启用基于内容的重复消除。`

### An application takes 40 seconds to process instructions received in an Amazon SQS message. Assuming the SQS queue is configured with the default VisibilityTimeout value, what is the BEST way, upon receiving a message, to ensure that no other instances can retrieve a message that has already been processed or is currently being processed?
> 一个应用程序需要 40 秒来处理收到的 Amazon SQS 消息中的指令。假设 SQS 队列配置了默认的 VisibilityTimeout 值，那么在收到消息时，确保没有其他实例可以检索已经处理或正在处理的消息的最佳方法是什么？

- [x] Use the ChangeMessageVisibility API to increase the VisibilityTimeout, then use the DeleteMessage API to delete the message. `使用 ChangeMessageVisibility API 增加 VisibilityTimeout，然后使用 DeleteMessage API 删除消息。`
- [ ] Use the DeleteMessage API call to delete the message from the queue, then call DeleteQueue API to remove the queue. `使用 DeleteMessage API 调用从队列中删除消息，然后调用 DeleteQueue API 删除队列。`
- [ ] Use the ChangeMessageVisibility API to decrease the timeout value, then use the DeleteMessage API to delete the message. `使用 ChangeMessageVisibility API 减少超时值，然后使用 DeleteMessage API 删除消息。`
- [ ] Use the DeleteMessageVisibility API to cancel the VisibilityTimeout, then use the DeleteMessage API to delete the message. `使用 DeleteMessageVisibility API 取消 VisibilityTimeout，然后使用 DeleteMessage API 删除消息。`

### A Developer is writing transactions into a DynamoDB table called 'SystemUpdates' that has 5 write capacity units. Which option has the highest read throughput?

### A Developer has created an S3 bucket s3://mycoolapp and has enabled server access logging that points to the folder s3://mycoolapp/logs. The Developer moved 100 KB of Cascading Style Sheets (CSS) documents to the folder s3://mycoolapp/css, and then stopped work. When the developer came back a few days later, the bucket was 50 GB. What is the MOST likely cause of this situation?
> 开发人员创建了一个 S3 存储桶 s3://mycoolapp，并启用了指向文件夹 s3://mycoolapp/logs 的服务器访问日志。开发人员将 100 KB 的层叠样式表（CSS）文档移动到文件夹 s3://mycoolapp/css，然后停止工作。当开发人员几天后回来时，存储桶的大小达到了 50 GB。造成这种情况的最可能原因是什么？

- [ ] The CSS files were not compressed and S3 versioning was enabled. `CSS 文件未压缩，并且启用了 S3 版本控制。`
- [ ] S3 replication was enabled on the bucket. `存储桶上启用了 S3 复制。`
- [x] Logging into the same bucket caused exponential log growth. `日志记录到同一存储桶导致日志的指数增长。`
- [ ] An S3 lifecycle policy has moved the entire CSS file to S3 Infrequent Access. `S3 生命周期策略已将整个 CSS 文件移动到 S3 不频繁访问。`

### A Developer uses AWS CodeDeploy to automate application deployment that connects to an external MySQL database. The Developer wants to securely access the encrypted secrets, such as API keys and database passwords. Which of the following solutions would involve the LEAST administrative effort?
> 一位开发者使用 AWS CodeDeploy 自动化应用程序部署，并连接到外部 MySQL 数据库。开发者希望安全地访问加密的秘密，例如 API 密钥和数据库密码。以下哪个解决方案涉及最少的管理工作？

- [ ] Save the secrets in Amazon S3 with AWS KMS server-side encryption, and use a signed URL to access them by using the IAM role from Amazon EC2 instances. `将秘密保存在启用 AWS KMS 服务器端加密的 Amazon S3 中，并使用签名 URL 通过 Amazon EC2 实例的 IAM 角色访问它们。`
- [ ] Use the instance metadata to store the secrets and to programmatically access the secrets from EC2 instances. `使用实例元数据存储秘密，并从 EC2 实例中以编程方式访问秘密。`
- [ ] Use the Amazon DynamoDB client-side encryption library to save the secrets in DynamoDB and to programmatically access the secrets from EC2 instances. `使用 Amazon DynamoDB 客户端加密库将秘密保存在 DynamoDB 中，并从 EC2 实例中以编程方式访问秘密。`
- [x] Use AWS SSM Parameter Store to store the secrets and to programmatically access them by using the IAM role from EC2 instances. `使用 AWS SSM 参数存储来存储秘密，并通过 EC2 实例的 IAM 角色以编程方式访问它们。`

### An application stops working with the following error: The specified bucket does not exist. Where is the BEST place to start the root cause analysis?
> 应用程序停止工作，并出现以下错误：指定的桶不存在。进行根本原因分析的最佳起点在哪里？

- [ ] Check the Elastic Load Balancer logs for DeleteBucket requests. `检查 Elastic Load Balancer 日志以查找 DeleteBucket 请求。`
- [ ] Check the application logs in Amazon CloudWatch Logs for Amazon S3 DeleteBucket errors. `检查 Amazon CloudWatch Logs 中的应用程序日志以查找 Amazon S3 DeleteBucket 错误。`
- [ ] Check AWS X-Ray for Amazon S3 DeleteBucket alarms. `检查 AWS X-Ray 中的 Amazon S3 DeleteBucket 警报。`
- [x] Check AWS CloudTrail for a DeleteBucket event. `检查 AWS CloudTrail 中的 DeleteBucket 事件。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Developer will be using the AWS CLI on a local development server to manage AWS services. What can be done to ensure that the CLI uses the Developer's IAM permissions when making commands?
> 开发者将在本地开发服务器上使用 AWS CLI 管理 AWS 服务。可以采取什么措施确保 CLI 在执行命令时使用开发者的 IAM 权限？

- [ ] Specify the Developer's IAM access key ID and secret access key as parameters for each CLI command. `在每个 CLI 命令中指定开发者的 IAM 访问密钥 ID 和秘密访问密钥作为参数。`
- [x] Run the aws configure CLI command, and provide the Developer's IAM access key ID and secret access key. `运行 aws configure CLI 命令，并提供开发者的 IAM 访问密钥 ID 和秘密访问密钥。`
- [ ] Specify the Developer's IAM user name and password as parameters for each CLI command. `在每个 CLI 命令中指定开发者的 IAM 用户名和密码作为参数。`
- [ ] Use the Developer's IAM role when making the CLI command. `在执行 CLI 命令时使用开发者的 IAM 角色。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### An application stores images in an S3 bucket. Amazon S3 event notifications are used to trigger a Lambda function that resizes the images. Processing each image takes less than a second. How will AWS Lambda handle the additional traffic?
> 一个应用程序将图像存储在 S3 存储桶中。使用 Amazon S3 事件通知触发 Lambda 函数来调整图像大小。处理每个图像的时间少于一秒。AWS Lambda 将如何处理额外的流量？

- [x] Lambda will scale out to execute the requests concurrently. `Lambda 将扩展以并发执行请求。`
- [ ] Lambda will handle the requests sequentially in the order received. `Lambda 将按接收顺序顺序处理请求。`
- [ ] Lambda will process multiple images in a single execution. `Lambda 将在一次执行中处理多个图像。`
- [ ] Lambda will add more compute to each execution to reduce processing time. `Lambda 将为每次执行增加更多计算以减少处理时间。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A company is building a stock trading application that requires sub-millisecond latency in processing trading requests. Amazon DynamoDB is used to store all the trading data that is used to process each request. After load testing the application, the development team found that due to data retrieval times, the latency requirement is not satisfied. Because of sudden high spikes in the number of requests, DynamoDB read capacity has to be significantly over-provisioned to avoid throttling. What steps should be taken to meet latency requirements and reduce the cost of running the application?
> 一家公司正在构建一个股票交易应用程序，需要在处理交易请求时达到亚毫秒延迟。Amazon DynamoDB 用于存储所有用于处理每个请求的交易数据。在对应用程序进行负载测试后，开发团队发现由于数据检索时间，延迟要求没有得到满足。由于请求数量突然高峰，DynamoDB 读取容量必须显著过度配置以避免限流。应采取哪些步骤以满足延迟要求并降低运行应用程序的成本？

- [x] Add Global Secondary Indexes for trading data. `为交易数据添加全局二级索引。`
- [ ] Store trading data in Amazon S3 and use Transfer Acceleration. `将交易数据存储在 Amazon S3 中并使用传输加速。`
- [ ] Add retries with exponential back-off for DynamoDB queries. `为 DynamoDB 查询添加带有指数退避的重试。`
- [ ] Use DynamoDB Accelerator to cache trading data. `使用 DynamoDB 加速器缓存交易数据。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Developer created a Lambda function for a web application backend. When testing the Lambda function from the AWS Lambda console, the Developer can see that the function is being executed, but there is no log data being generated in Amazon CloudWatch Logs, even after several minutes. What could cause this situation?
> 一名开发人员为一个 web 应用程序后端创建了一个 Lambda 函数。在 AWS Lambda 控制台测试 Lambda 函数时，开发人员可以看到该函数正在执行，但在 Amazon CloudWatch Logs 中没有生成任何日志数据，即使过了几分钟。这种情况可能是什么原因？

- [ ] The Lambda function does not have any explicit log statements for the log data to send it to CloudWatch Logs. `Lambda 函数没有任何明确的日志语句来将日志数据发送到 CloudWatch Logs。`
- [ ] The Lambda function is missing CloudWatch Logs as a source trigger to send log data. `Lambda 函数缺少 CloudWatch Logs 作为源触发器来发送日志数据。`
- [x] The execution role for the Lambda function is missing permissions to write log data to the CloudWatch Logs. `Lambda 函数的执行角色缺少将日志数据写入 CloudWatch Logs 的权限。`
- [ ] The Lambda function is missing a target CloudWatch Log group. `Lambda 函数缺少目标 CloudWatch Log 组。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Developer wants to use AWS X-Ray to trace a user request end-to-end throughput the software stack. The Developer made the necessary changes in the application tested it, and found that the application is able to send the traces to AWS X-Ray. However, when the application is deployed to an EC2 instance, the traces are not available. Which of the following could create this situation? (Choose TWO)
> 一名开发人员希望使用 AWS X-Ray 追踪用户请求在软件堆栈中的端到端吞吐量。开发人员对应用程序进行了必要的更改并进行了测试，发现应用程序能够将追踪信息发送到 AWS X-Ray。然而，当应用程序部署到 EC2 实例时，追踪信息不可用。以下哪些情况可能导致这种情况？（选择两个）

- [ ] The traces are reaching X-Ray, but the Developer does not have access to view the records. `追踪信息已到达 X-Ray，但开发人员没有权限查看记录。`
- [x] The X-Ray daemon is not installed on the EC2 instance. `EC2 实例上未安装 X-Ray 守护进程。`
- [ ] The X-Ray endpoint specified in the application configuration is incorrect. `应用程序配置中指定的 X-Ray 端点不正确。`
- [ ] The instance role does not have 'xray:BatchGetTraces' and 'xray:GetTraceGraph' permissions. The instance role does not have 'xray:PutTraceSegments' and 'xray:PutTelemetryRecords' permissions. `实例角色没有 'xray:BatchGetTraces' 和 'xray:GetTraceGraph' 权限。实例角色没有 'xray:PutTraceSegments' 和 'xray:PutTelemetryRecords' 权限。`
- [x] The instance role does not have 'xray:PutTraceSegments' and 'xray:PutTelemetryRecords' permissions. `实例角色没有 'xray:PutTraceSegments' 和 'xray:PutTelemetryRecords' 权限。`

**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### An application has hundreds of users. Each user may use multiple devices to access the application. The Developer wants to assign unique identifiers to these users regardless of the device they use. Which of the following methods should be used to obtain unique identifiers?
> 一个应用程序有数百个用户。每个用户可能使用多个设备访问该应用程序。开发人员希望为这些用户分配唯一标识符，无论他们使用哪个设备。以下哪些方法应被用于获取唯一标识符？

- [ ] Create a user table in Amazon DynamoDB as key-value pairs of users and their devices. Use these keys as unique identifiers. `在 Amazon DynamoDB 中创建一个用户表，将用户及其设备作为键值对。使用这些键作为唯一标识符。`
- [ ] Use IAM-generated access key IDs for the users as the unique identifier, but do not store secret keys. `使用 IAM 生成的访问密钥 ID 作为用户的唯一标识符，但不存储密钥。`
- [ ] Implement developer-authenticated identities by using Amazon Cognito, and get credentials for these identities. `通过使用 Amazon Cognito 实现开发者认证身份，并为这些身份获取凭证。`
- [x] Assign IAM users and roles to the users. Use the unique IAM resource ID as the unique identifier. `为用户分配 IAM 用户和角色。使用唯一的 IAM 资源 ID 作为唯一标识符。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### What are the steps to using the AWS CLI to launch a templatized serverless application?
> 使用 AWS CLI 启动模板化无服务器应用程序的步骤是什么？

- [ ] Use AWS CloudFormation get-template then CloudFormation execute-change-set. `使用 AWS CloudFormation 获取模板，然后执行更改集。`
- [ ] Use AWS CloudFormation validate-template then CloudFormation create-change-set. `使用 AWS CloudFormation 验证模板，然后创建更改集。`
- [x] Use AWS CloudFormation package then CloudFormation deploy. `使用 AWS CloudFormation 打包，然后部署。`
- [ ] Use AWS CloudFormation create-stack then CloudFormation update-stack. `使用 AWS CloudFormation 创建堆栈，然后更新堆栈。`
