### A deployment package uses the AWS CLI to copy files into any S3 bucket in the account, using access keys stored in environment variables. The package is running on EC2 instances, and the instances have been modified to run with an assumed IAM role and a more restrictive policy that allows access to only one bucket. After the change, the Developer logs into the host and still has the ability to write into all of the S3 buckets in that account. What is the MOST likely cause of this situation?
> 部署包使用 AWS CLI 将文件复制到帐户中的任何 S3 存储桶，使用存储在环境变量中的访问密钥。该包在 EC2 实例上运行，实例已被修改为使用假定的 IAM 角色和更严格的策略，该策略仅允许访问一个存储桶。在更改后，开发人员登录主机，仍然能够写入该帐户中的所有 S3 存储桶。导致这种情况的最可能原因是什么？

- [ ] An IAM inline policy is being used on the IAM role. `正在 IAM 角色上使用 IAM 内联策略。`
- [x] An IAM managed policy is being used on the IAM role. `正在 IAM 角色上使用 IAM 托管策略。`
- [ ] The AWS CLI is corrupt and needs to be reinstalled. `AWS CLI 损坏，需要重新安装。`
- [ ] The AWS credential provider looks for instance profile credentials last. `AWS 凭证提供程序最后查找实例配置文件凭证。`

### An application overwrites an object in Amazon S3, and then immediately reads the same object. Why would the application sometimes retrieve the old version of the object?
> 应用程序在 Amazon S3 中覆盖了一个对象，然后立即读取同一对象。为什么应用程序有时会检索到对象的旧版本？

- [x] S3 overwrite PUTS are eventually consistent, so the application may read the old object. `S3 的覆盖 PUT 操作是最终一致性的，因此应用程序可能会读取旧对象。`
- [ ] The application needs to add extra metadata to label the latest version when uploading to Amazon S3. `应用程序在上传到 Amazon S3 时需要添加额外的元数据以标记最新版本。`
- [ ] All S3 PUTS are eventually consistent, so the application may read the old object. `所有 S3 PUT 操作都是最终一致性的，因此应用程序可能会读取旧对象。`
- [ ] The application needs to explicitly specify latest version when retrieving the object. `应用程序在检索对象时需要明确指定最新版本。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### An application under development is required to store hundreds of video files. The data must be encrypted within the application prior to storage, with a unique key for each video file. How should the Developer code the application?
> 开发中的应用程序需要存储数百个视频文件。数据必须在存储之前在应用程序内加密，并且每个视频文件都需要一个唯一的密钥。开发者应该如何编写应用程序？

- [ ] Use the KMS Encrypt API to encrypt the data. Store the encrypted data key and data. `使用 KMS 加密 API 来加密数据。存储加密的数据密钥和数据。`
- [ ] Use a cryptography library to generate an encryption key for the application. Use the encryption key to encrypt the data. Store the encrypted data. `使用加密库为应用程序生成一个加密密钥。使用加密密钥加密数据。存储加密的数据。`
- [x] Use the KMS GenerateDataKey API to get a data key. Encrypt the data with the data key. Store the encrypted data key and data. `使用 KMS GenerateDataKey API 获取数据密钥。使用数据密钥加密数据。存储加密的数据密钥和数据。`
- [ ] Upload the data to an S3 bucket using server side-encryption with an AWS KMS key. `使用 AWS KMS 密钥的服务器端加密将数据上传到 S3 存储桶。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A developer is testing an application that invokes an AWS Lambda function asynchronously. During the testing phase, the Lambda function fails to process after two retries. How can the developer troubleshoot the failure?
> 开发者正在测试一个异步调用 AWS Lambda 函数的应用程序。在测试阶段，Lambda 函数在两次重试后未能处理。开发者如何排查失败？

- [ ] Configure AWS CloudTrail logging to investigate the invocation failures. `配置 AWS CloudTrail 日志以调查调用失败。`
- [x] Configure Dead Letter Queues by sending events to Amazon SQS for investigation. `通过将事件发送到 Amazon SQS 配置死信队列以进行调查。`
- [ ] Configure Amazon Simple Workflow Service to process any direct unprocessed events. `配置 Amazon 简单工作流服务来处理任何直接未处理的事件。`
- [ ] Configure AWS Config to process any direct unprocessed events. `配置 AWS Config 来处理任何直接未处理的事件。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A developer is setting up Amazon API Gateway for their company's products. The API will be used by registered developers to query and update their environments. The company wants to limit the amount of requests end users can send for both cost and security reasons. Management wants to offer registered developers the option of buying larger packages that allow for more requests. How can the developer accomplish this with the LEAST amount of overhead management?
> 开发者正在为他们公司的产品设置 Amazon API Gateway。该 API 将被注册开发者用来查询和更新他们的环境。公司希望限制最终用户可以发送的请求数量，以便控制成本和安全原因。管理层希望为注册开发者提供购买允许更多请求的更大套餐的选项。开发者如何以最少的管理开销来实现这一目标？

- [ ] Enable throttling for the API Gateway stage. Set a value for both the rate and burst capacity. If a registered user chooses a larger package, create a stage for them, adjust the values, and share the new URL with them. `为 API Gateway 阶段启用限流。为速率和突发容量设置值。如果注册用户选择了更大的套餐，为他们创建一个阶段，调整值，并与他们共享新 URL。`
- [ ] Set up Amazon CloudWatch API logging in API Gateway. Create a filter based on the user and requestTime fields and create an alarm on this filter. Write an AWS Lambda function to analyze the values and requester information, and respond accordingly. Set up the function as the target for the alarm. If a registered user chooses a larger package, update the Lambda code with the values. `在 API Gateway 中设置 Amazon CloudWatch API 日志。基于用户和请求时间字段创建过滤器并在该过滤器上创建警报。编写一个 AWS Lambda 函数来分析值和请求者信息，并做出相应的响应。将该函数设置为警报的目标。如果注册用户选择了更大的套餐，请用新值更新 Lambda 代码。`
- [ ] Enable Amazon CloudWatch metrics for the API Gateway stage. Set up CloudWatch alarms based off the Count metric and the ApiName, Method, Resource, and Stage dimensions to alerts when request rates pass the threshold. Set the alarm action to Deny. If a registered user chooses a larger package, create a user-specific alarm and adjust the values. `为 API Gateway 阶段启用 Amazon CloudWatch 指标。基于计数指标和 API 名称、方法、资源和阶段维度设置 CloudWatch 警报，以在请求速率超过阈值时发出警报。将警报动作设置为拒绝。如果注册用户选择了更大的套餐，请创建一个用户特定的警报并调整值。`
- [x] Set up a default usage plan, specify values for the rate and burst capacity, and associate it with a stage. If a registered user chooses a larger package, create a custom plan with the appropriate values and associate the plan with the user. `设置默认使用计划，指定速率和突发容量的值，并将其与阶段关联。如果注册用户选择了更大的套餐，请创建一个具有适当值的自定义计划，并将该计划与用户关联。`

**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A developer is refactoring a monolithic application. The application takes a POST request and performs several operations. Some of the operations are in parallel while others run sequentially. These operations have been refactored into individual AWS Lambda functions. The POST request will be processed by Amazon API Gateway. How should the developer invoke the Lambda functions in the same sequence using API Gateway?
> 开发者正在重构一个单体应用。该应用接受一个 POST 请求并执行多个操作。部分操作是并行进行的，而其他操作则是顺序执行的。这些操作已被重构为单独的 AWS Lambda 函数。POST 请求将由 Amazon API Gateway 处理。开发者应该如何通过 API Gateway 按照相同的顺序调用 Lambda 函数？

- [ ] Use Amazon SQS to invoke the Lambda functions. `使用 Amazon SQS 调用 Lambda 函数。`
- [ ] Use an AWS Step Functions activity to run the Lambda functions. `使用 AWS Step Functions 活动来运行 Lambda 函数。`
- [ ] Use Amazon SNS to trigger the Lambda functions. `使用 Amazon SNS 触发 Lambda 函数。`
- [x] Use an AWS Step Functions state machine to orchestrate the Lambda functions. `使用 AWS Step Functions 状态机来编排 Lambda 函数。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A company is adding stored value (or gift card) capability to its highly popular casual gaming website. Users need to be able to trade this value for other users' items on the platform. This would require both users' records be updated as a single transaction, or both users' records to be completely rolled back. Which AWS database options can provide the transactional capability required for this new feature? (Choose TWO)
> 一家公司正在为其非常受欢迎的休闲游戏平台添加储值（或礼品卡）功能。用户需要能够用该价值交换其他用户在平台上的物品。这需要同时更新两个用户的记录作为一个事务，或者完全回滚两个用户的记录。哪些 AWS 数据库选项可以提供该新功能所需的事务能力？（选择两个）

- [ ] Amazon DynamoDB with operations made with the ConsistentRead parameter set to true. `将 ConsistentRead 参数设置为 true 的 Amazon DynamoDB 进行操作。`
- [ ] Amazon ElastiCache for Memcached with operations made within a transaction block. `在事务块内进行操作的 Amazon ElastiCache for Memcached。`
- [x] Amazon Aurora MySQL with operations made within a transaction block. `在事务块内进行操作的 Amazon Aurora MySQL。`
- [x] Amazon DynamoDB with reads and writes made using Transact* operations. `使用 Transact* 操作进行读写的 Amazon DynamoDB。`
- [ ] Amazon Redshift with operations made within a transaction block. `在事务块内进行操作的 Amazon Redshift。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A developer is creating an AWS Lambda function that generates a new file each time it runs. Each new file must be checked into an AWS CodeCommit repository hosted in the same AWS account. How should the developer accomplish this?
> 一名开发人员正在创建一个 AWS Lambda 函数，每次运行时都会生成一个新文件。每个新文件必须被提交到同一 AWS 账户中托管的 AWS CodeCommit 存储库。开发人员应该如何完成此任务？

- [x] When the Lambda function starts, use the Git CLI to clone the repository. Check the new file into the cloned repository and push the change. `当 Lambda 函数启动时，使用 Git CLI 克隆存储库。将新文件提交到克隆的存储库并推送更改。`
- [ ] After the new file is created in Lambda, use cURL to invoke the CodeCommit API. Send the file to the repository. `在 Lambda 中创建新文件后，使用 cURL 调用 CodeCommit API。将文件发送到存储库。`
- [ ] Use an AWS SDK to instantiate a CodeCommit client. Invoke the put_file method to add the file to the repository. `使用 AWS SDK 实例化一个 CodeCommit 客户端。调用 put_file 方法将文件添加到存储库。`
- [ ] Upload the new file to an Amazon S3 bucket. Create an AWS Step Function to accept S3 events. In the Step Function, add the new file to the repository. `将新文件上传到 Amazon S3 存储桶。创建一个 AWS Step Function 来接受 S3 事件。在 Step Function 中，将新文件添加到存储库。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A developer must ensure that the IAM credentials used by an application in Amazon EC2 are not misused or compromised. What should the developer use to keep user credentials secure?
> 开发人员必须确保在 Amazon EC2 中使用的应用程序的 IAM 凭证不被滥用或泄露。开发人员应该使用什么来保持用户凭证的安全？

- [ ] Environment variables. `环境变量。`
- [ ] AWS credentials file. `AWS 凭证文件。`
- [ ] Instance profile credentials. `实例配置文件凭证。`
- [x] Command line options. `命令行选项。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A company has an application where reading objects from Amazon S3 is based on the type of user. The user types are registered user and guest user. The company has 25,000 users and is growing. Information is pulled from an S3 bucket depending on the user type. Which approaches are recommended to provide access to both user types? (Choose TWO)
> 一家公司有一个应用程序，读取 Amazon S3 中的对象是基于用户类型的。用户类型为注册用户和访客用户。该公司有 25,000 名用户，并且还在增长。信息根据用户类型从 S3 存储桶中提取。推荐哪些方法为这两种用户提供访问权限？（选择两个）

- [x] Provide a different access key and secret access key in the application code for registered users and guest users to provide read access to the objects. `在应用程序代码中为注册用户和访客用户提供不同的访问密钥和秘密访问密钥，以提供对象的读取访问。`
- [x] Use S3 bucket policies to restrict read access to specific IAM users. `使用 S3 存储桶策略限制特定 IAM 用户的读取访问。`
- [ ] Use Amazon Cognito to provide access using authenticated and unauthenticated roles. `使用 Amazon Cognito 提供通过身份验证和未身份验证角色的访问。`
- [ ] Create a new IAM user for each user and grant read access. `为每个用户创建一个新的 IAM 用户并授予读取访问权限。`
- [ ] Use the AWS IAM service and let the application assume the different roles using the AWS Security Token Service (AWS STS) AssumeRole action depending on the type of user and provide read access to Amazon S3 using the assumed role. `使用 AWS IAM 服务，并让应用程序根据用户类型使用 AWS Security Token Service (AWS STS) AssumeRole 操作假设不同的角色，并使用假设的角色提供对 Amazon S3 的读取访问。`

**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A company has 25,000 employees and is growing. The company is creating an application that will be accessible to its employees only. A developer is using Amazon S3 to store images and Amazon RDS to store application data. The company requires that all employee information remain in the legacy Security Assertion Markup Language (SAML) employee directory only and is not interested in mirroring any employee information on AWS. How can the developer provide authorized access for the employees who will be using this application so each employee can access their own application data only?
> 一家公司有 25,000 名员工，并且还在增长。该公司正在创建一个仅员工可访问的应用程序。开发人员正在使用 Amazon S3 存储图像，使用 Amazon RDS 存储应用程序数据。公司要求所有员工信息仅保留在遗留的安全声明标记语言（SAML）员工目录中，并且不想在 AWS 上镜像任何员工信息。开发人员如何为使用该应用程序的员工提供授权访问，以便每位员工只能访问自己的应用程序数据？

- [ ] Use Amazon VPC and keep all resources inside the VPC, and use a VPC link for the S3 bucket with the bucket policy. `使用 Amazon VPC 并将所有资源保留在 VPC 内，并使用带有存储桶策略的 VPC 链接访问 S3 存储桶。`
- [ ] Use Amazon Cognito user pools, federate with the SAML provider, and use user pool groups with an IAM policy. `使用 Amazon Cognito 用户池，与 SAML 提供商进行联合，并使用带有 IAM 策略的用户池组。`
- [x] Use an Amazon Cognito identity pool, federate with the SAML provider, and use an IAM condition key with a value for the cognito-identity.amazonaws.com:sub variable to grant access to the employees. `使用 Amazon Cognito 身份池，与 SAML 提供商进行联合，并使用 IAM 条件键，值为 cognito-identity.amazonaws.com:sub 变量，授予员工访问权限。`
- [ ] Create a unique IAM role for each employee and have each employee assume the role to access the application so they can access their personal data only. `为每个员工创建一个唯一的 IAM 角色，并让每个员工假设该角色以访问应用程序，这样他们只能访问自己的个人数据。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A company has developed a new serverless application using AWS Lambda functions that will be deployed using the AWS Serverless Application Model (AWS SAM) CLI. Which step should the developer complete prior to deploying the application?
> 一家公司使用 AWS Lambda 函数开发了一个新的无服务器应用程序，该应用程序将使用 AWS 无服务器应用程序模型（AWS SAM）CLI 部署。开发人员在部署应用程序之前应该完成哪一步？

- [ ] Compress the application to a .zip file and upload it into AWS Lambda. `将应用程序压缩为 .zip 文件并上传到 AWS Lambda。`
- [ ] Test the new AWS Lambda function by first tracing it in AWS X-Ray. `通过先在 AWS X-Ray 中跟踪它来测试新的 AWS Lambda 函数。`
- [x] Bundle the serverless application using a SAM package. `使用 SAM 包装无服务器应用程序。`
- [ ] Create the application environment using the eb create my-env command. `使用 eb create my-env 命令创建应用程序环境。`

### An application needs to encrypt data that is written to Amazon S3 where the keys are managed in an on-premises data center, and the encryption is handled by S3. Which type of encryption should be used?
> 一个应用程序需要加密写入 Amazon S3 的数据，其中密钥在本地数据中心管理，且加密由 S3 处理。应该使用哪种类型的加密？

- [ ] Use server-side encryption with Amazon S3-managed keys. `使用 Amazon S3 管理的密钥进行服务器端加密。`
- [ ] Use server-side encryption with AWS KMS-managed keys. `使用 AWS KMS 管理的密钥进行服务器端加密。`
- [x] Use client-side encryption with customer master keys. `使用客户主密钥进行客户端加密。`
- [ ] Use server-side encryption with customer-provided keys. `使用客户提供的密钥进行服务器端加密。`

**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A development team is working on a mobile app that allows users to upload pictures to Amazon S3. The team expects the app will be used by hundreds of thousands of users during a single event simultaneously. Once the pictures are uploaded, the backend service will scan and parse the pictures for inappropriate content. Which approach is the MOST resilient way to achieve this goal, which also smooths out temporary volume spikes for the backend service?
> 一个开发团队正在开发一款移动应用，允许用户将图片上传到 Amazon S3。团队预计该应用将在单个事件中被数十万用户同时使用。上传图片后，后端服务将扫描和解析这些图片以检测不当内容。哪种方法是实现这一目标的最具弹性的方式，同时平滑后端服务的临时流量峰值？

- [ ] Develop an AWS Lambda function to check the upload folder in the S3 bucket. If new uploaded pictures are detected, the Lambda function will scan and parse them. `开发一个 AWS Lambda 函数以检查 S3 存储桶中的上传文件夹。如果检测到新上传的图片，Lambda 函数将扫描和解析它们。`
- [x] Once a picture is uploaded to Amazon S3, publish the event to an Amazon SQS queue. Use the queue as an event source to trigger an AWS Lambda function. In the Lambda function, scan and parse the picture. `一旦图片上传到 Amazon S3，将事件发布到 Amazon SQS 队列。使用该队列作为事件源触发 AWS Lambda 函数。在 Lambda 函数中，扫描和解析图片。`
- [ ] When the user uploads a picture, invoke an API hosted in Amazon API Gateway. The API will invoke an AWS Lambda function to scan and parse the picture. `当用户上传图片时，调用托管在 Amazon API Gateway 中的 API。该 API 将调用 AWS Lambda 函数扫描和解析图片。`
- [ ] Create a state machine in AWS Step Functions to check the upload folder in the S3 bucket. If a new picture is detected, invoke an AWS Lambda function to scan and parse it. `在 AWS Step Functions 中创建一个状态机以检查 S3 存储桶中的上传文件夹。如果检测到新图片，调用 AWS Lambda 函数进行扫描和解析。`

**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A development team wants to run their container workloads on Amazon ECS. Each application container needs to share data with another container to collect logs and metrics. What should the developer team do to meet these requirements?
> 一个开发团队希望在 Amazon ECS 上运行他们的容器工作负载。每个应用容器需要与另一个容器共享数据以收集日志和指标。开发团队应该如何做才能满足这些要求？

- [x] Create two pod specifications. Make one to include the application container and the other to include the other container. Link the two pods together. `创建两个 pod 规格。一个包含应用容器，另一个包含其他容器。将两个 pod 连接在一起。`
- [ ] Create two task definitions. Make one to include the application container and the other to include the other container. Mount a shared volume between the two tasks. `创建两个任务定义。一个包含应用容器，另一个包含其他容器。在两个任务之间挂载一个共享卷。`
- [ ] Create one task definition. Specify both containers in the definition. Mount a shared volume between those two containers. `创建一个任务定义。在定义中指定两个容器。在这两个容器之间挂载一个共享卷。`
- [ ] Create a single pod specification. Include both containers in the specification. Mount a persistent volume to both containers. `创建一个单一的 pod 规格。在规格中包括两个容器。为这两个容器挂载一个持久卷。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### An ecommerce startup is preparing for an annual sales event. As the traffic to the company's application increases, the development team wants to be notified when the Amazon EC2 instance's CPU utilization exceeds 80%. Which solution will meet this requirement?
> 一家电子商务初创公司正在为年度销售活动做准备。随着公司应用程序的流量增加，开发团队希望在 Amazon EC2 实例的 CPU 利用率超过 80% 时收到通知。哪种解决方案可以满足这一需求？

- [x] Create a custom Amazon CloudWatch alarm that sends a notification to an Amazon SNS topic when the CPU utilization exceeds 80%. `创建一个自定义的 Amazon CloudWatch 警报，当 CPU 利用率超过 80% 时，向 Amazon SNS 主题发送通知。`
- [ ] Create a custom AWS Cloud Trail alarm that sends a notification to an Amazon SNS topic when the CPU utilization exceeds 80%. `创建一个自定义的 AWS CloudTrail 警报，当 CPU 利用率超过 80% 时，向 Amazon SNS 主题发送通知。`
- [ ] Create a cron job on the EC2 instance that executes the –describe-instance-information command on the host instance every 15 minutes and sends the results to an Amazon SNS topic. `在 EC2 实例上创建一个 cron 作业，每 15 分钟在主机实例上执行 –describe-instance-information 命令，并将结果发送到 Amazon SNS 主题。`
- [ ] Create an AWS Lambda function that queries the AWS CloudTrail logs for the CPUUtilization metric every 15 minutes and sends a notification to an Amazon SNS topic when the CPU utilization exceeds 80%. `创建一个 AWS Lambda 函数，每 15 分钟查询一次 AWS CloudTrail 日志中的 CPUUtilization 指标，当 CPU 利用率超过 80% 时，向 Amazon SNS 主题发送通知。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### An application running on Amazon EC2 opens connections to an Amazon RDS SQL Server database. The developer does not want to store the user name and password for the database in the code. The developer would also like to automatically rotate the credentials. What is the MOST secure way to store and access the database credentials?
> 在 Amazon EC2 上运行的应用程序打开与 Amazon RDS SQL Server 数据库的连接。开发人员不希望在代码中存储数据库的用户名和密码。开发人员还希望自动轮换凭据。存储和访问数据库凭据的最安全方式是什么？

- [ ] Create an IAM role that has permissions to access the database. Attach the role to the EC2 instance. `创建一个具有访问数据库权限的 IAM 角色。将角色附加到 EC2 实例。`
- [x] Use AWS Secrets Manager to store the credentials. Retrieve the credentials from Secrets Manager as needed. `使用 AWS Secrets Manager 存储凭据。根据需要从 Secrets Manager 检索凭据。`
- [ ] Store the credentials in an encrypted text file in an Amazon S3 bucket. Configure the EC2 instance's user data to download the credentials from Amazon S3 as the instance boots. `将凭据存储在 Amazon S3 存储桶中的加密文本文件中。配置 EC2 实例的用户数据，在实例启动时从 Amazon S3 下载凭据。`
- [ ] Store the user name and password credentials directly in the source code. No further action is needed because the source code is stored in a private repository. `将用户名和密码凭据直接存储在源代码中。不需要进一步操作，因为源代码存储在私有存储库中。`

### A developer is updating an application deployed on AWS Elastic Beanstalk. The new version is incompatible with the old version. To successfully deploy the update, a full cutover to the new, updated version must be performed on all instances at one time, with the ability to roll back changes in case of a deployment failure in the new version. How can this be performed with the LEAST amount of downtime?
> 开发人员正在更新部署在 AWS Elastic Beanstalk 上的应用程序。新版本与旧版本不兼容。为了成功部署更新，必须在所有实例上同时执行完全切换到新的更新版本，并且在新版本部署失败的情况下能够回滚更改。如何在最少的停机时间内执行此操作？

- [ ] Use the Elastic Beanstalk All at once deployment policy to update all instances simultaneously. `使用 Elastic Beanstalk "一次性全部" 部署策略同时更新所有实例。`
- [ ] Perform an Elastic Beanstalk Rolling with additional batch deployment. `执行 Elastic Beanstalk "滚动附加批次" 部署。`
- [x] Deploy the new version in a new Elastic Beanstalk environment and swap environment URLs. `在一个新的 Elastic Beanstalk 环境中部署新版本并交换环境 URL。`
- [ ] Perform an Elastic Beanstalk Rolling deployment. `执行 Elastic Beanstalk "滚动" 部署。`

### A developer is writing a web application that must share secure documents with end users. The documents are stored in a private Amazon S3 bucket. The application must allow only authenticated users to download specific documents when requested, and only for a duration of 15 minutes. How can the developer meet these requirements?
> 开发人员正在编写一个 Web 应用程序，该应用程序必须与最终用户共享安全文档。文档存储在一个私有的 Amazon S3 存储桶中。应用程序必须仅允许经过身份验证的用户在请求时下载特定文档，并且仅限于 15 分钟的时间。开发人员应如何满足这些要求？

- [ ] Copy the documents to a separate S3 bucket that has a lifecycle policy for deletion after 15 minutes. `将文档复制到一个具有 15 分钟后删除生命周期策略的单独 S3 存储桶中。`
- [x] Create a presigned S3 URL using the AWS SDK with an expiration time of 15 minutes. `使用 AWS SDK 创建带有 15 分钟过期时间的 S3 预签名 URL。`
- [ ] Use server-side encryption with AWS KMS managed keys (SSE-KMS) and download the documents using HTTPS. `使用服务器端加密和 AWS KMS 管理的密钥 (SSE-KMS) 并通过 HTTPS 下载文档。`
- [ ] Modify the S3 bucket policy to only allow specific users to download the documents. Revert the change after 15 minutes. `修改 S3 存储桶策略以仅允许特定用户下载文档。15 分钟后还原更改。`

### A company is developing a report executed by AWS Step Functions, Amazon CloudWatch shows errors in the Step Functions task state machine. To troubleshoot each task, the state input needs to be included along with the error message in the state output. Which coding practice can preserve both the original input and the error for the state?
> 一家公司正在开发一个通过 AWS Step Functions 执行的报告，Amazon CloudWatch 显示 Step Functions 任务状态机中的错误。为了排查每个任务，状态输入需要和错误信息一起包含在状态输出中。哪种编码实践可以同时保留原始输入和错误信息？

- [x] Use ResultPath in a Catch statement to include the error with the original input. `在 Catch 语句中使用 ResultPath 以将错误与原始输入一起包含。`
- [ ] Use InputPath in a Catch statement and set the value to null. `在 Catch 语句中使用 InputPath 并将值设置为 null。`
- [ ] Use Error Equals in a Retry statement to include the error with the original input. `在 Retry 语句中使用 Error Equals 将错误与原始输入一起包含。`
- [ ] Use OutputPath in a Retry statement and set the value to $. `在 Retry 语句中使用 OutputPath 并将值设置为 $。`

### A developer receives the following error message when trying to launch or terminate an Amazon EC2 instance using a boto3 script. What should the developer do to correct this error message?
> 开发人员在尝试使用 boto3 脚本启动或终止 Amazon EC2 实例时收到以下错误消息。开发人员应如何纠正此错误？

- [ ] Assign an IAM role to the EC2 instance to allow necessary API calls on behalf of the client. `为 EC2 实例分配一个 IAM 角色，以允许代表客户端进行必要的 API 调用。`

- [ ] Increase the overall network bandwidth to handle higher API request rates. `增加整体网络带宽以处理更高的 API 请求速率。`
- [ ] Upgrade to the latest AWS CLI version so that boto3 can handle higher request rates. `升级到最新的 AWS CLI 版本，以便 boto3 可以处理更高的请求速率。`

### Given the following AWS CloudFormation template. What is the MOST efficient way to reference the new Amazon S3 bucket from another AWS CloudFormation template?
> 鉴于以下 AWS CloudFormation 模板，从另一个 AWS CloudFormation 模板中引用新的 Amazon S3 存储桶的最有效方式是什么？

![Question 130](images/question130.jpg)

- [ ] Add an Export declaration to the Outputs section of the original template and use ImportValue in other templates. `在原始模板的 Outputs 部分添加 Export 声明，并在其他模板中使用 ImportValue。`
- [ ] Add Exported: true to the Contentbucket in the original template and use ImportResource in other templates. `在原始模板中的 Contentbucket 中添加 Exported: true，并在其他模板中使用 ImportResource。`
- [x] Create a custom AWS CloudFormation resource that gets the bucket name from the ContentBucket resource of the first stack. `创建一个自定义 AWS CloudFormation 资源，从第一个堆栈的 ContentBucket 资源中获取存储桶名称。`
- [ ] Use Fn::Include to include the existing template in other templates and use the ContentBucket resource directly. `使用 Fn::Include 将现有模板包含在其他模板中，并直接使用 ContentBucket 资源。`

### A developer is creating a script to automate the deployment process for a serverless application. The developer wants to use an existing AWS Serverless Application Model (AWS SAM) template for the application. What should the developer use for the project? (Choose TWO)
> 开发人员正在创建一个脚本以自动化无服务器应用程序的部署过程。开发人员希望使用现有的 AWS Serverless Application Model (AWS SAM) 模板来构建应用程序。开发人员应该在项目中使用什么？（选择两个）

- [x] Call aws cloudformation package to create the deployment package. Call aws cloudformation deploy to deploy the package afterward. `调用 aws cloudformation package 创建部署包。然后调用 aws cloudformation deploy 部署该包。`
- [x] Call sam package to create the deployment package. Call sam deploy to deploy the package afterward. `调用 sam package 创建部署包。然后调用 sam deploy 部署该包。`
- [ ] Call aws s3 cp to upload the AWS SAM template to Amazon S3. Call aws lambda update-function-code to create the application. `调用 aws s3 cp 将 AWS SAM 模板上传到 Amazon S3。调用 aws lambda update-function-code 创建应用程序。`
- [ ] Create a ZIP package locally and call aws serverlessrepo create-application to create the application. `在本地创建 ZIP 包，并调用 aws serverlessrepo create-application 创建应用程序。`
- [ ] Create a ZIP package and upload it to Amazon S3. Call aws cloudformation create-stack to create the application. `创建一个 ZIP 包并将其上传到 Amazon S3。调用 aws cloudformation create-stack 创建应用程序。`

### A development team is designing a mobile app that requires multi-factor authentication. Which steps should be taken to achieve this? (Choose TWO)
> 开发团队正在设计一个需要多因素身份验证的移动应用程序。应该采取哪些步骤来实现这一点？（选择两个）

- [x] Use Amazon Cognito to create a user pool and create users in the user pool. `使用 Amazon Cognito 创建用户池并在用户池中创建用户。`
- [ ] Send multi-factor authentication text codes to users with the Amazon SNS Publish API call in the app code. `通过应用代码中的 Amazon SNS Publish API 调用向用户发送多因素身份验证文本代码。`
- [x] Enable multi-factor authentication for the Amazon Cognito user pool. `为 Amazon Cognito 用户池启用多因素身份验证。`
- [ ] Use AWS IAM to create IAM users. `使用 AWS IAM 创建 IAM 用户。`
- [ ] Enable multi-factor authentication for the users created in AWS IAM. `为在 AWS IAM 中创建的用户启用多因素身份验证。`

### Two containerized microservices are hosted on Amazon EC2 ECS. The first microservice reads an Amazon RDS Aurora database instance, and the second microservice reads an Amazon DynamoDB table. How can each microservice be granted the minimum privileges?
> 两个容器化微服务托管在 Amazon EC2 ECS 上。第一个微服务读取 Amazon RDS Aurora 数据库实例，第二个微服务读取 Amazon DynamoDB 表。如何为每个微服务授予最小权限？

- [ ] Set ECS_ENABLE_TASK_IAM_ROLE to false on EC2 instance boot in ECS agent configuration file. Run the first microservice with an IAM role for ECS tasks with read-only access for the Aurora database. Run the second microservice with an IAM role for ECS tasks with read-only access to DynamoDB. `在 ECS 代理配置文件中将 ECS_ENABLE_TASK_IAM_ROLE 设置为 false。使用具有只读访问 Aurora 数据库的 ECS 任务 IAM 角色运行第一个微服务。使用具有只读访问 DynamoDB 的 ECS 任务 IAM 角色运行第二个微服务。`
- [ ] Set ECS_ENABLE_TASK_IAM_ROLE to false on EC2 instance boot in the ECS agent configuration file. Grant the instance profile role read-only access to the Aurora database and DynamoDB. `在 ECS 代理配置文件中将 ECS_ENABLE_TASK_IAM_ROLE 设置为 false。将实例配置文件角色授予对 Aurora 数据库和 DynamoDB 的只读访问权限。`
- [x] Set ECS_ENABLE_TASK_IAM_ROLE to true on EC2 instance boot in the ECS agent configuration file. Run the first microservice with an IAM role for ECS tasks with read-only access for the Aurora database. Run the second microservice with an IAM role for ECS tasks with read-only access to DynamoDB. `在 ECS 代理配置文件中将 ECS_ENABLE_TASK_IAM_ROLE 设置为 true。使用具有只读访问 Aurora 数据库的 ECS 任务 IAM 角色运行第一个微服务。使用具有只读访问 DynamoDB 的 ECS 任务 IAM 角色运行第二个微服务。`
- [ ] Set ECS_ENABLE_TASK_IAM_ROLE to true on EC2 instance boot in the ECS agent configuration file. Grant the instance profile role read-only access to the Aurora database and DynamoDB. `在 ECS 代理配置文件中将 ECS_ENABLE_TASK_IAM_ROLE 设置为 true。将实例配置文件角色授予对 Aurora 数据库和 DynamoDB 的只读访问权限。`

**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A developer has written an AWS Lambda function using Java as the runtime environment. The developer wants to isolate a performance bottleneck in the code. Which steps should be taken to reveal the bottleneck?
> 开发人员使用 Java 作为运行时环境编写了一个 AWS Lambda 函数。开发人员希望隔离代码中的性能瓶颈。应采取哪些步骤来揭示瓶颈？

- [ ] Use the Amazon CloudWatch API to write timestamps to a custom CloudWatch metric. Use the CloudWatch console to analyze the resulting data. `使用 Amazon CloudWatch API 将时间戳写入自定义 CloudWatch 指标。使用 CloudWatch 控制台分析生成的数据。`
- [ ] Use the AWS X-Ray API to write trace data into X-Ray from strategic places within the code. Use the Amazon CloudWatch console to analyze the resulting data. `使用 AWS X-Ray API 从代码中的战略位置写入跟踪数据到 X-Ray。使用 Amazon CloudWatch 控制台分析生成的数据。`
- [x] Use the AWS X-Ray API to write trace data into X-Ray from strategic places within the code. Use the X-Ray console to analyze the resulting data. `使用 AWS X-Ray API 从代码中的战略位置写入跟踪数据到 X-Ray。使用 X-Ray 控制台分析生成的数据。`
- [ ] Use the Amazon CloudWatch API to write timestamps to a custom CloudWatch metric. Use the AWS X-Ray console to analyze the resulting data. `使用 Amazon CloudWatch API 将时间戳写入自定义 CloudWatch 指标。使用 AWS X-Ray 控制台分析生成的数据。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A developer added a new feature to an application running on an Amazon EC2 instance that uses Amazon SQS. After deployment, the developer noticed a significant increase in Amazon SQS costs. When monitoring the Amazon SQS metrics on Amazon CloudWatch, the developer found that on average one message per minute is posted on this queue. What can be done to reduce Amazon SQS costs for this application?
> 开发人员在运行 Amazon EC2 实例的应用程序中添加了新功能，该应用程序使用 Amazon SQS。部署后，开发人员注意到 Amazon SQS 成本显著增加。当监控 Amazon CloudWatch 上的 Amazon SQS 指标时，开发人员发现平均每分钟在该队列中发布一条消息。为了降低此应用程序的 Amazon SQS 成本，可以采取哪些措施？

- [x] Increase the Amazon SQS queue polling timeout. `增加 Amazon SQS 队列轮询超时。`
- [ ] Scale down the Amazon SQS queue to the appropriate size for low traffic demand. `将 Amazon SQS 队列缩小到适合低流量需求的适当大小。`
- [ ] Configure push delivery via Amazon SNS instead of polling the Amazon SQS queue. `配置通过 Amazon SNS 进行推送交付，而不是轮询 Amazon SQS 队列。`
- [ ] Use an Amazon SQS first-in, first-out (FIFO) queue instead of a standard queue. `使用 Amazon SQS 先进先出 (FIFO) 队列而不是标准队列。`

### A developer is building an application using an Amazon API Gateway REST API backend by an AWS Lambda function that interacts with an Amazon DynamoDB table. During testing, the developer observes high latency when making requests to the API. How can the developer evaluate the end-to-end latency and identify performance bottlenecks?
> 开发人员正在构建一个应用程序，使用 Amazon API Gateway REST API 作为后端，并通过 AWS Lambda 函数与 Amazon DynamoDB 表进行交互。在测试过程中，开发人员注意到在向 API 发出请求时延迟很高。开发人员如何评估端到端的延迟并识别性能瓶颈？

- [ ] Enable AWS CloudTrail logging and use the logs to map each latency and bottleneck. `启用 AWS CloudTrail 日志记录，并使用日志来映射每个延迟和瓶颈。`
- [x] Enable and configure AWS X-Ray tracing on API Gateway and the Lambda function. Use X-Ray to trace and analyze user requests. `在 API Gateway 和 Lambda 函数上启用并配置 AWS X-Ray 跟踪。使用 X-Ray 跟踪和分析用户请求。`
- [ ] Enable Amazon CloudWatch Logs for the Lambda function. Enable execution logs for API Gateway to view and analyze user request logs. `为 Lambda 函数启用 Amazon CloudWatch 日志。启用 API Gateway 的执行日志以查看和分析用户请求日志。`
- [ ] Enable VPC Flow Logs to capture and analyze network traffic within the VPC. `启用 VPC 流日志以捕获和分析 VPC 内的网络流量。`

### An IAM role is attached to an Amazon EC2 instance that explicitly denies access to all Amazon S3 API actions. The EC2 instance credentials file specifies the IAM access key and secret access key, which allow full administrative access. Given that multiple modes of IAM access are present for this EC2 instance, which of the following is correct?
> 一个 IAM 角色已附加到一个 Amazon EC2 实例，该角色明确拒绝对所有 Amazon S3 API 操作的访问。EC2 实例凭证文件指定了 IAM 访问密钥和秘密访问密钥，这些密钥允许完全管理访问。考虑到此 EC2 实例存在多种 IAM 访问模式，以下哪个是正确的？

- [ ] The EC2 instance will only be able to list the S3 buckets. `EC2 实例只能列出 S3 存储桶。`
- [ ] The EC2 instance will only be able to list the contents of one S3 bucket at a time. `EC2 实例只能一次列出一个 S3 存储桶的内容。`
- [ ] The EC2 instance will be able to perform all actions on any S3 bucket. `EC2 实例将能够对任何 S3 存储桶执行所有操作。`
- [x] The EC2 instance will not be able to perform any S3 action on any S3 bucket. `EC2 实例将无法对任何 S3 存储桶执行任何 S3 操作。`

### A development team uses AWS Elastic Beanstalk for application deployment. The team has configured the application version lifecycle policy to limit the number of application versions to 25. However, even with the lifecycle policy, the source bundle is deleted from the Amazon S3 source bucket. What should a developer do in the Elastic Beanstalk application version lifecycle settings to retain the source code in the S3 bucket?
> 开发团队使用 AWS Elastic Beanstalk 进行应用程序部署。团队已配置应用程序版本生命周期策略，以限制应用程序版本的数量为 25。然而，即使有生命周期策略，源捆绑包仍会从 Amazon S3 源存储桶中删除。开发人员应该在 Elastic Beanstalk 应用程序版本生命周期设置中采取什么措施来保留 S3 存储桶中的源代码？

- [ ] Change the Set the application versions limit by total count setting to zero. `将按总数设置应用程序版本限制的设置更改为零。`
- [ ] Disable the Lifecycle policy setting. `禁用生命周期策略设置。`
- [ ] Change the Set the application version limit by age setting to zero. `将按年龄设置应用程序版本限制的设置更改为零。`
- [x] Set Retention to Retain source bundle in S3. `设置保留以保留 S3 中的源捆绑包。`

### A developer has built a market application that stores pricing data in Amazon DynamoDB with Amazon ElastiCache in front. The prices of items in the market change frequently. Sellers have begun complaining that, after they update the price of an item, the price does not actually change in the product listing. What could be causing this issue?
> 开发人员构建了一个市场应用程序，将定价数据存储在 Amazon DynamoDB 中，并在前面使用 Amazon ElastiCache。市场上商品的价格变化频繁。卖家开始抱怨，在他们更新商品价格后，商品列表中的价格并未实际改变。这可能是什么原因导致的？

- [x] The cache is not being invalidated when the price of the item is changed. `在商品价格更改时，缓存未被失效。`
- [ ] The price of the item is being retrieved using a write-through ElastiCache cluster. `商品的价格是通过写入 ElastiCache 集群获取的。`
- [ ] The DynamoDB table was provisioned with insufficient read capacity. `DynamoDB 表的预置读取容量不足。`
- [ ] The DynamoDB table was provisioned with insufficient write capacity. `DynamoDB 表的预置写入容量不足。`

### A developer is provided with an HTTPS clone URL for an AWS CodeCommit repository. What needs to be configured before cloning this repository?
> 开发人员获得了 AWS CodeCommit 存储库的 HTTPS 克隆 URL。在克隆此存储库之前需要配置什么？

- [ ] Use AWS KMS to set up public and private keys for use with AWS CodeCommit. `使用 AWS KMS 设置公钥和私钥以供 AWS CodeCommit 使用。`
- [x] Set up the Git credential helper to use an AWS credential profile, and enable the helper to send the path to the repositories. `设置 Git 凭证助手以使用 AWS 凭证配置文件，并启用助手发送到存储库的路径。`
- [ ] Use AWS Certificate Manager to provision public and private SSL/TLS certificates. `使用 AWS Certificate Manager 提供公有和私有 SSL/TLS 证书。`
- [ ] Generate encryption keys using AWS CloudHSM, then export the key for use with AWS CodeCommit. `使用 AWS CloudHSM 生成加密密钥，然后导出该密钥以供 AWS CodeCommit 使用。`

### What is required to trace Lambda-based applications with AWS X-Ray?

- [ ] Update and add AWS X-Ray daemon code to relevant parts of the Lambda function to set up the trace. `在 Lambda 函数的相关部分更新并添加 AWS X-Ray 守护进程代码以设置跟踪。`

### A development team is building a new application that will run on Amazon EC2 and use Amazon DynamoDB as a storage layer. The developers all have assigned IAM user accounts in the same IAM group. The developers currently can launch EC2 instances, and they need to be able to launch EC2 instances with an instance role allowing access to Amazon DynamoDB. Which AWS IAM changes are needed when creating an instance role to provide this functionality?
> 开发团队正在构建一个将在 Amazon EC2 上运行并使用 Amazon DynamoDB 作为存储层的新应用程序。开发人员都有分配的 IAM 用户帐户，位于同一个 IAM 组中。开发人员当前可以启动 EC2 实例，他们需要能够启动带有允许访问 Amazon DynamoDB 的实例角色的 EC2 实例。创建实例角色以提供此功能时需要哪些 AWS IAM 更改？

- [ ] Create an IAM permission policy attached to the role that allows access to DynamoDB. Add a trust policy to the role that allows DynamoDB to assume the role. Attach a permissions policy to the development group in AWS IAM that allows developers to use the iam:GetRole and iam:PassRole permissions for the role. `创建一个附加到角色的 IAM 权限策略，以允许访问 DynamoDB。向角色添加信任策略，允许 DynamoDB 假设该角色。将权限策略附加到 AWS IAM 中的开发组，允许开发人员使用 iam:GetRole 和 iam:PassRole 权限。`
- [x] Create an IAM permissions policy attached to the role that allows access to DynamoDB. Add a trust policy to the role that allows Amazon EC2 to assume the role. Attach a permissions policy to the development group in AWS IAM that allows developers to use the iam:PassRole permission for the role. `创建一个附加到角色的 IAM 权限策略，以允许访问 DynamoDB。向角色添加信任策略，允许 Amazon EC2 假设该角色。将权限策略附加到 AWS IAM 中的开发组，允许开发人员使用 iam:PassRole 权限。`
- [ ] Create an IAM permission policy attached to the role that allows access to Amazon EC2. Add a trust policy to the role that allows DynamoDB to assume the role. Attach a permissions policy to the development group in AWS IAM that allows developers to use the iam:PassRole permission for the role. `创建一个附加到角色的 IAM 权限策略，以允许访问 Amazon EC2。向角色添加信任策略，允许 DynamoDB 假设该角色。将权限策略附加到 AWS IAM 中的开发组，允许开发人员使用 iam:PassRole 权限。`
- [ ] Create an IAM permissions policy attached to the role that allows access to DynamoDB. Add a trust policy to the role that allows Amazon EC2 to assume the role. Attach a permissions policy to the development group in AWS IAM that allows developers to use the iam:GetRole permission for the role. `创建一个附加到角色的 IAM 权限策略，以允许访问 DynamoDB。向角色添加信任策略，允许 Amazon EC2 假设该角色。将权限策略附加到 AWS IAM 中的开发组，允许开发人员使用 iam:GetRole 权限。`

### A developer converted an existing program to an AWS Lambda function in the console. The program runs properly on a local laptop, but shows an 'Unable to import module' error when tested in the Lambda console. Which of the following can fix the error?
> 开发人员将现有程序转换为 AWS Lambda 控制台中的 Lambda 函数。该程序在本地笔记本电脑上正常运行，但在 Lambda 控制台测试时显示“无法导入模块”错误。以下哪项可以修复该错误？

- [x] Install the missing module and specify the current directory as the target. Create a ZIP file to include all files under the current directory, and upload the ZIP file. `安装缺少的模块并指定当前目录作为目标。创建一个 ZIP 文件以包含当前目录下的所有文件，并上传该 ZIP 文件。`
- [ ] Install the missing module in a lib directory. Create a ZIP file to include all files under the lib directory, and upload the ZIP file as dependency file. `在 lib 目录中安装缺少的模块。创建一个 ZIP 文件以包含 lib 目录下的所有文件，并将 ZIP 文件作为依赖文件上传。`
- [ ] In the Lambda code, invoke a Linux command to install the missing modules under the /usr/lib directory. `在 Lambda 代码中，调用 Linux 命令以在 /usr/lib 目录下安装缺少的模块。`
- [ ] In the Lambda console, create a LB_LIBRARY_PATH environment and specify the value for the system library plan. `在 Lambda 控制台中，创建一个 LB_LIBRARY_PATH 环境并为系统库计划指定值。`

### A front-end web application is using Amazon Cognito user pools to handle the user authentication flow. A developer is integrating Amazon DynamoDB into the application using the AWS SDK for JavaScript. How would the developer securely call the API without exposing the access or secret keys?
> 一个前端 web 应用程序使用 Amazon Cognito 用户池来处理用户身份验证流程。开发人员正在使用 AWS SDK for JavaScript 将 Amazon DynamoDB 集成到应用程序中。开发人员如何安全地调用 API 而不暴露访问密钥或秘密密钥？

- [x] Configure Amazon Cognito identity pools and exchange the JSON Web Token (JWT) for temporary credentials. `配置 Amazon Cognito 身份池，并用 JSON Web Token (JWT) 交换临时凭证。`
- [ ] Run the web application in an Amazon EC2 instance with the instance profile configured. `在配置了实例配置文件的 Amazon EC2 实例中运行 web 应用程序。`
- [ ] Hardcore the credentials, use Amazon S3 to host the web application, and enable server-side encryption. `硬编码凭证，使用 Amazon S3 托管 web 应用程序，并启用服务器端加密。`
- [ ] Use Amazon Cognito user pool JSON Web Tokens (JWITs) to access the DynamoDB APIs. `使用 Amazon Cognito 用户池 JSON Web Token (JWITs) 访问 DynamoDB API。`

### A developer needs to manage AWS infrastructure as code and must be able to deploy multiple identical copies of the infrastructure, stage changes, and revert to previous versions. Which approach addresses these requirements?

### A Developer needs to deploy an application running on AWS Fargate using Amazon ECS. The application has environment variables that must be passed to a container for the application to initialize. How should the environment variables be passed to the container?
> 开发人员需要部署一个运行在 AWS Fargate 上的应用程序，使用 Amazon ECS。应用程序有环境变量必须传递给容器以便应用程序初始化。应该如何将环境变量传递给容器？

- [ ] Define an array that includes the environment variables under the entryPoint parameter within the task definition. `在任务定义中定义一个数组，包含环境变量，作为 entryPoint 参数。`
- [ ] Define an array that includes the environment variables under the entryPoint parameter within the service definition. `在服务定义中定义一个数组，包含环境变量，作为 entryPoint 参数。`

### A company's fleet of Amazon EC2 instances receives data from millions of users through an API. The servers batch the data, add an object for each user, and upload the objects to an S3 bucket to ensure high access rates. The object attributes are Customer ID, Server ID, TS-Server (TimeStamp and Server ID), the size of the object, and a timestamp. A Developer wants to find all the objects for a given user collected during a specified time range. After creating an S3 object created event, how can the Developer achieve this requirement?
> 一家公司的 Amazon EC2 实例集通过 API 接收来自数百万用户的数据。服务器批量处理数据，为每个用户添加一个对象，并将对象上传到 S3 存储桶以确保高访问率。对象属性包括客户 ID、服务器 ID、TS-Server（时间戳和服务器 ID）、对象大小和时间戳。开发人员希望查找在指定时间范围内收集的给定用户的所有对象。在创建 S3 对象创建事件后，开发人员如何满足该要求？

- [ ] Execute an AWS Lambda function in response to the S3 object creation events that creates an Amazon DynamoDB record for every object with the Customer ID as the partition key and the Server ID as the sort key. Retrieve all the records using the Customer ID and Server ID attributes. `执行 AWS Lambda 函数响应 S3 对象创建事件，为每个对象创建一个 Amazon DynamoDB 记录，使用客户 ID 作为分区键，服务器 ID 作为排序键。使用客户 ID 和服务器 ID 属性检索所有记录。`
- [ ] Execute an AWS Lambda function in response to the S3 object creation events that creates an Amazon Redshift record for every object with the Customer ID as the partition key and TS-Server as the sort key. Retrieve all the records using the Customer ID and TS-Server attributes. `执行 AWS Lambda 函数响应 S3 对象创建事件，为每个对象创建一个 Amazon Redshift 记录，使用客户 ID 作为分区键，TS-Server 作为排序键。使用客户 ID 和 TS-Server 属性检索所有记录。`
- [x] Execute an AWS Lambda function in response to the S3 object creation events that creates an Amazon DynamoDB record for every object with the Customer ID as the partition key and TS-Server as the sort key. Retrieve all the records using the Customer ID and TS-Server attributes. `执行 AWS Lambda 函数响应 S3 对象创建事件，为每个对象创建一个 Amazon DynamoDB 记录，使用客户 ID 作为分区键，TS-Server 作为排序键。使用客户 ID 和 TS-Server 属性检索所有记录。`
- [ ] Execute an AWS Lambda function in response to the S3 object creation events that creates an Amazon Redshift record for every object with the Customer ID as the partition key and the Server ID as the sort key. Retrieve all the records using the Customer ID and Server ID attributes. `执行 AWS Lambda 函数响应 S3 对象创建事件，为每个对象创建一个 Amazon Redshift 记录，使用客户 ID 作为分区键，服务器 ID 作为排序键。使用客户 ID 和服务器 ID 属性检索所有记录。`

### A company is managing a NoSQL database on-premises to host a critical component of an application, which is starting to have scaling issues. The company wants to migrate the application to Amazon DynamoDB with the following considerations: Optimize frequent queries. Reduce read latencies. Plan for frequent queries on certain key attributes of the table. Which solution would help achieve these objectives?
> 一家公司正在管理一个本地的 NoSQL 数据库，以承载应用程序的关键组件，该组件开始出现扩展问题。该公司希望将应用程序迁移到 Amazon DynamoDB，并考虑以下因素：优化频繁查询。减少读取延迟。计划在表的某些关键属性上进行频繁查询。哪种解决方案可以帮助实现这些目标？

- [x] Create global secondary indexes on keys that are frequently queried. Add the necessary attributes into the indexes. `在频繁查询的键上创建全局二级索引。将必要的属性添加到索引中。`
- [ ] Create local secondary indexes on keys that are frequently queried. DynamoDB will fetch needed attributes from the table. `在频繁查询的键上创建本地二级索引。DynamoDB 将从表中提取所需属性。`
- [ ] Create DynamoDB global tables to speed up query responses. Use a scan to fetch data from the table. `创建 DynamoDB 全球表以加速查询响应。使用扫描从表中获取数据。`
- [ ] Create an AWS Auto Scaling policy for the DynamoDB table. `为 DynamoDB 表创建 AWS Auto Scaling 策略。`

### A developer is writing an application that will process data delivered into an Amazon S3 bucket. The data is delivered approximately 10 times a day, and the developer expects the data will be processed in less than 1 minute, on average. How can the developer deploy and invoke the application with the lowest cost and lowest latency?
> 一位开发人员正在编写一个应用程序，该应用程序将处理传送到 Amazon S3 存储桶的数据。数据每天大约交付 10 次，开发人员预计数据平均将在 1 分钟内处理完成。开发人员如何以最低的成本和最低的延迟部署和调用该应用程序？

- [ ] Deploy the application as an AWS Lambda function and invoke it with an Amazon CloudWatch alarm triggered by an S3 object upload. `将应用程序部署为 AWS Lambda 函数，并通过 S3 对象上传触发的 Amazon CloudWatch 警报调用它。`
- [x] Deploy the application as an AWS Lambda function and invoke it with an S3 event notification. `将应用程序部署为 AWS Lambda 函数，并通过 S3 事件通知调用它。`
- [ ] Deploy the application as an AWS Lambda function and invoke it with an Amazon CloudWatch scheduled event. `将应用程序部署为 AWS Lambda 函数，并通过 Amazon CloudWatch 定时事件调用它。`
- [ ] Deploy the application onto an Amazon EC2 instance and have it poll the S3 bucket for new objects. `将应用程序部署到 Amazon EC2 实例上，并让它轮询 S3 存储桶以获取新对象。`

### A company is using Amazon API Gateway to manage its public-facing API. The CISO requires that the APIs be used by test account users only. What is the MOST secure way to restrict API access to users of this particular AWS account?
> 一家公司正在使用 Amazon API Gateway 来管理其面向公众的 API。首席信息安全官要求仅允许测试账户用户使用这些 API。最安全的方式是什么来限制对特定 AWS 账户用户的 API 访问？

- [ ] Usage plans. `使用计划。`

### A Developer is migrating existing applications to AWS. These applications use MongoDB as their primary data store, and they will be deployed to Amazon EC2 instances. > 一位开发者正在将现有应用程序迁移到 AWS。这些应用程序使用 MongoDB 作为其主要数据存储，并将部署到 Amazon EC2 实例上。管理层要求开发者在使用 AWS 服务时最小化对应用程序的更改。开发者应该使用哪种解决方案在 AWS 中托管 MongoDB？

- [ ] Install MongoDB on the same instance where the application is running. `在与应用程序运行的同一实例上安装 MongoDB。`
- [x] Deploy Amazon DocumentDB in MongoDB compatibility mode. `以 MongoDB 兼容模式部署 Amazon DocumentDB。`
- [ ] Use Amazon API Gateway to translate API calls from MongoDB to Amazon DynamoDB. `使用 Amazon API Gateway 将 API 调用从 MongoDB 转换为 Amazon DynamoDB。`
- [ ] Replicate the existing MongoDB workload to Amazon DynamoDB. `将现有的 MongoDB 工作负载复制到 Amazon DynamoDB。`

### A Developer is writing an application that runs on Amazon EC2 instances in an Auto Scaling group. The application data is stored in an Amazon DynamoDB table and records are constantly updated by all instances. An instance sometimes retrieves old data. The Developer wants to correct this by making sure the reads are strongly consistent. How can the Developer accomplish this?
> 开发者正在编写一个运行在 Auto Scaling 组中的 Amazon EC2 实例上的应用程序。应用程序数据存储在 Amazon DynamoDB 表中，所有实例都在不断更新记录。某些实例有时会检索到旧数据。开发者希望通过确保读取强一致性来纠正这一点。开发者如何实现这一目标？

- [x] Set ConsistentRead to true when calling Getltem. `在调用 Getltem 时将 ConsistentRead 设置为 true。`
- [ ] Create a new DynamoDB Accelerator (DAX) table. `创建一个新的 DynamoDB Accelerator (DAX) 表。`
- [ ] Set Consistency to strong when calling UpdateTable. `在调用 UpdateTable 时将一致性设置为强。`
- [ ] Use the GetShardIterator command. `使用 GetShardIterator 命令。`

### An application is experiencing performance issues based on increased demand. This increased demand is on read-only historical records pulled from an Amazon RDS-hosted database with custom views and queries. A Developer must improve performance without changing the database structure. Which approach will improve performance and MINIMIZE management overhead?
> 一个应用程序由于需求增加而出现性能问题。这个增加的需求是针对从 Amazon RDS 托管的数据库中提取的只读历史记录，使用了自定义视图和查询。开发者必须在不更改数据库结构的情况下提高性能。哪种方法可以提高性能并最小化管理开销？

- [ ] Deploy Amazon DynamoDB, move all the data, and point to DynamoDB. `部署 Amazon DynamoDB，移动所有数据并指向 DynamoDB。`
- [x] Deploy Amazon ElastiCache for Redis and cache the data for the application. `部署 Amazon ElastiCache for Redis 并缓存应用程序的数据。`
- [ ] Deploy Memcached on Amazon EC2 and cache the data for the application. `在 Amazon EC2 上部署 Memcached 并缓存应用程序的数据。`
- [ ] Deploy Amazon DynamoDB Accelerator (DAX) on Amazon RDS to improve cache performance. `在 Amazon RDS 上部署 Amazon DynamoDB 加速器 (DAX) 以提高缓存性能。`

### A Developer has an Amazon DynamoDB table that must be in provisioned mode to comply with user requirements. > 开发者有一个必须处于预置模式的 Amazon DynamoDB 表，以符合用户要求。该应用程序需要支持以下内容：平均项大小：10 KB 每秒读取项：10 个强一致性 每秒写入项：2 个事务性。哪个读取和写入容量以成本效益的方式满足这些要求？

- [ ] Read 10; write 2. `读取 10；写入 2。`

- [ ] Read 300; write 400. `读取 300；写入 400。`

### A company wants to containerize an existing three-tier web application and deploy it to Amazon ECS Fargate. The application is using session data to keep track of user activities. Which approach would provide the BEST user experience?

### An application is using a single-node Amazon ElastiCache for Redis instance to improve read performance. > 一个应用程序正在使用单节点 Amazon ElastiCache for Redis 实例来提高读取性能。随着时间的推移，该应用程序的需求呈指数增长，增加了 ElastiCache 实例的负载。缓存层必须能够处理负载，并在节点发生故障时具备弹性。开发人员可以采取什么措施来满足负载和弹性要求？

### A Developer has discovered that an application responsible for processing messages in an Amazon SQS queue is routinely falling behind. The application is capable of processing multiple messages in one execution, but is only receiving one message at a time. What should the Developer do to increase the number of messages the application receives?
> 开发人员发现负责处理 Amazon SQS 队列中消息的应用程序经常落后。该应用程序能够在一次执行中处理多个消息，但一次只接收一条消息。开发人员应该怎么做才能增加应用程序接收的消息数量？

- [ ] Call the ChangeMessageVisibility API for the queue and set MaxNumberOfMessages to a value greater than the default of 1. `调用 ChangeMessageVisibility API 为队列设置 MaxNumberOfMessages 为大于默认值 1 的值。`
- [ ] Call the AddPermission API to set MaxNumberOfMessages for the ReceiveMessage action to a value greater than the default of 1. `调用 AddPermission API 为 ReceiveMessage 操作设置 MaxNumberOfMessages 为大于默认值 1 的值。`
- [x] Call the ReceiveMessage API to set MaxNumberOfMessages to a value greater than the default of 1. `调用 ReceiveMessage API 将 MaxNumberOfMessages 设置为大于默认值 1 的值。`
- [ ] Call the SetQueueAttributes API for the queue and set MaxNumberOfMessages to a value greater than the default of 1. `调用 SetQueueAttributes API 为队列设置 MaxNumberOfMessages 为大于默认值 1 的值。`

### A Developer registered an AWS Lambda function as a target for an Application Load Balancer (ALB) using a CLI command. However, the Lambda function is not being invoked when the client sends requests through the ALB. Why is the Lambda function not being invoked?
> 开发人员通过 CLI 命令将 AWS Lambda 函数注册为应用程序负载均衡器 (ALB) 的目标。然而，当客户端通过 ALB 发送请求时，Lambda 函数没有被调用。为什么 Lambda 函数没有被调用？

- [ ] A Lambda function cannot be registered as a target for an ALB. `Lambda 函数不能注册为 ALB 的目标。`
- [ ] A Lambda function can be registered with an ALB using AWS Management Console only. `Lambda 函数只能通过 AWS 管理控制台与 ALB 注册。`
- [x] The permissions to invoke the Lambda function are missing. `调用 Lambda 函数的权限缺失。`
- [ ] Cross-zone is not enabled on the ALB. `ALB 上未启用跨区域。`

### A company provides APIs as a service and commits to a service level agreement (SLA) with all its users. To comply with each SLA, what should the company do?

- [ ] Enable API rate limiting in Amazon Cognito for each user. `为每个用户在 Amazon Cognito 中启用 API 速率限制。`
- [x] Enable default throttling limits for each stage after deploying the APIs. `在部署 API 后，为每个阶段启用默认限流限制。`

### A Developer is preparing a deployment package using AWS CloudFormation. The package consists of two separate templates: one for the infrastructure and one for the application. The application has to be inside the VPC that is created from the infrastructure template. How can the application stack refer to the VPC created from the infrastructure template?
> 一位开发者正在使用 AWS CloudFormation 准备一个部署包。该包由两个单独的模板组成：一个用于基础设施，一个用于应用程序。应用程序必须位于从基础设施模板创建的 VPC 内。应用程序栈如何引用从基础设施模板创建的 VPC？

- [x] Use the Ref function to import the VPC into the application stack from the infrastructure template. `使用 Ref 函数从基础设施模板将 VPC 导入到应用程序栈中。`
- [ ] Use the export flag in the infrastructure template, and then use the Fn::ImportValue function in the application template. `在基础设施模板中使用 export 标志，然后在应用程序模板中使用 Fn::ImportValue 函数。`
- [ ] Use the DependsOn attribute to specify that the application instance depends on the VPC in the application template. `使用 DependsOn 属性指定应用程序实例依赖于应用程序模板中的 VPC。`
- [ ] Use the Fn::GetAtt function to include the attribute of the VPC in the application template. `使用 Fn::GetAtt 函数在应用程序模板中包含 VPC 的属性。`

### A Developer is trying to monitor an application's status by running a cron job that returns 1 if the service is up and 0 if the service is down. The Developer created code that uses an AWS CLI put-metric-alarm command to publish the custom metrics to Amazon CloudWatch and create an alarm. However, the Developer is unable to create an alarm as the custom metrics do not appear in the CloudWatch console. What is causing this issue?
> 开发者试图通过运行一个 cron 作业来监控应用程序的状态，该作业返回 1 表示服务正常，返回 0 表示服务关闭。开发者编写的代码使用 AWS CLI 的 put-metric-alarm 命令将自定义指标发布到 Amazon CloudWatch 并创建警报。然而，开发者无法创建警报，因为自定义指标未出现在 CloudWatch 控制台中。造成此问题的原因是什么？

- [ ] Sending custom metrics using the CLI is not supported. `使用 CLI 发送自定义指标不受支持。`
- [x] The Developer needs to use the put-metric-data command. `开发者需要使用 put-metric-data 命令。`
- [ ] The Developer must use a unified CloudWatch agent to publish custom metrics. `开发者必须使用统一的 CloudWatch 代理来发布自定义指标。`
- [ ] The code is not running on an Amazon EC2 instance. `代码未在 Amazon EC2 实例上运行。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Developer has written an application that runs on Amazon EC2 instances and generates a value every minute. The Developer wants to monitor and graph the values generated over time without logging in to the instance each time. Which approach should the Developer use to achieve this goal?
> 开发者编写了一个在 Amazon EC2 实例上运行的应用程序，每分钟生成一个值。开发者希望监控并绘制生成值的时间图表，而无需每次都登录到实例中。开发者应该使用哪种方法来实现这一目标？

- [ ] Use the Amazon CloudWatch metrics reported by default for all EC2 instances. View each value from the CloudWatch console. `使用默认报告的 Amazon CloudWatch 指标查看所有 EC2 实例的每个值。`
- [ ] Develop the application to store each value in a file on Amazon S3 every minute with the timestamp as the name. `开发应用程序每分钟将每个值存储在 Amazon S3 中的文件中，以时间戳作为文件名。`
- [x] Publish each generated value as a custom metric to Amazon CloudWatch using available AWS SDKs. `使用可用的 AWS SDK 将每个生成的值作为自定义指标发布到 Amazon CloudWatch。`
- [ ] Store each value as a variable and add the variable to the list of EC2 metrics that should be reported to the Amazon CloudWatch console. `将每个值存储为变量，并将该变量添加到应报告给 Amazon CloudWatch 控制台的 EC2 指标列表中。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Development team decides to adopt a continuous integration/continuous delivery (CI/CD) process using AWS CodePipeline and AWS CodeCommit for a new application. However, management wants a person to review and approve the code before it is deployed to production. How can the Development team add a manual approver to the CI/CD pipeline?
> 开发团队决定使用 AWS CodePipeline 和 AWS CodeCommit 为新应用程序采用持续集成/持续交付（CI/CD）流程。然而，管理层希望在将代码部署到生产环境之前，有人进行审核和批准。开发团队如何在 CI/CD 管道中添加手动批准者？

- [ ] Use AWS SES to send an email to approvers when their action is required. Develop a simple application that allows approvers to accept or reject a build. Invoke an AWS Lambda function to advance the pipeline when a build is accepted. `使用 AWS SES 在需要行动时向批准者发送电子邮件。开发一个简单的应用程序，允许批准者接受或拒绝构建。当构建被接受时调用 AWS Lambda 函数以推进管道。`
- [ ] If approved, add an approved tag when pushing changes to the CodeCommit repository. CodePipeline will proceed to build and deploy approved commits without interruption. `如果批准，在将更改推送到 CodeCommit 存储库时添加批准标签。CodePipeline 将继续构建和部署已批准的提交而不受干扰。`
- [ ] Add an approval step to CodeCommit. Commits will not be saved until approved. `向 CodeCommit 添加一个批准步骤。提交将在获得批准之前不会被保存。`
- [x] Add an approval action to the pipeline. Configure the approval action to publish to an Amazon SNS topic when approval is required. The pipeline execution will stop and wait for an approval. `向管道添加一个批准操作。当需要批准时，配置批准操作以发布到 Amazon SNS 主题。管道执行将停止并等待批准。`

### A Developer is building a serverless application using AWS Lambda and must create a REST API using an HTTP GET method. What needs to be defined to meet this requirement? (Choose TWO)
> 开发人员正在使用 AWS Lambda 构建无服务器应用程序，并必须使用 HTTP GET 方法创建 REST API。需要定义什么以满足此要求？（选择两个）

- [ ] A Lambda@Edge function. `一个 Lambda@Edge 函数。`
- [x] An Amazon API Gateway with a Lambda function. `一个带有 Lambda 函数的 Amazon API Gateway。`
- [x] An exposed GET method in an Amazon API Gateway. `在 Amazon API Gateway 中公开的 GET 方法。`
- [ ] An exposed GET method in the Lambda function. `在 Lambda 函数中公开的 GET 方法。`
- [ ] An exposed GET method in Amazon Route 53. `在 Amazon Route 53 中公开的 GET 方法。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Developer is writing an application in AWS Lambda. To simplify testing and deployments, the Developer needs the database connection string to be easily changed without modifying the Lambda code. How can this requirement be met?
> 开发人员正在 AWS Lambda 中编写应用程序。为了简化测试和部署，开发人员需要能够轻松更改数据库连接字符串，而无需修改 Lambda 代码。如何满足此要求？

- [x] Store the connection string as a secret in AWS Secrets Manager. `将连接字符串作为机密存储在 AWS Secrets Manager 中。`
- [ ] Store the connection string in an IAM user account. `将连接字符串存储在 IAM 用户帐户中。`
- [ ] Store the connection string in AWS KMS. `将连接字符串存储在 AWS KMS 中。`
- [ ] Store the connection string as a Lambda layer. `将连接字符串作为 Lambda 层存储。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A company is launching an ecommerce website and will host the static data in Amazon S3. The company expects approximately 1,000 transactions per second (TPS) for GET and PUT requests in total. Logging must be enabled to track all requests and must be retained for auditing purposes. What is the MOST cost-effective solution?
> 一家公司正在推出一个电子商务网站，将静态数据托管在 Amazon S3 中。该公司预计总共有大约 1,000 次每秒（TPS）的 GET 和 PUT 请求。必须启用日志记录以跟踪所有请求，并且必须保留以用于审计目的。最具成本效益的解决方案是什么？

- [ ] Enable AWS CloudTrail logging for the S3 bucket-level action and create a lifecycle policy to move the data from the log bucket to Amazon S3 Glacier in 90 days. `启用 AWS CloudTrail 日志记录以进行 S3 存储桶级别操作，并创建一个生命周期策略，将数据从日志存储桶移动到 Amazon S3 Glacier 中，保留 90 天。`
- [ ] Enable S3 server access logging and create a lifecycle policy to expire the data in 90 days. `启用 S3 服务器访问日志记录并创建一个生命周期策略，以在 90 天后过期数据。`
- [ ] Enable AWS CloudTrail logging for the S3 bucket-level action and create a lifecycle policy to expire the data in 90 days. `启用 AWS CloudTrail 日志记录以进行 S3 存储桶级别操作，并创建一个生命周期策略，以在 90 天后过期数据。`
- [x] Enable S3 server access logging and create a lifecycle policy to move the data to Amazon S3 Glacier in 90 days. `启用 S3 服务器访问日志记录并创建一个生命周期策略，将数据在 90 天后移动到 Amazon S3 Glacier。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Developer decides to store highly secure data in Amazon S3 and wants to implement server-side encryption (SSE) with granular control of who can access the master key. Company policy requires that the master key be created, rotated, and disabled easily when needed, all for security reasons. Which solution should be used to meet these requirements?
> 开发人员决定将高度安全的数据存储在 Amazon S3 中，并希望实现服务器端加密（SSE），以对谁可以访问主密钥进行精细控制。公司政策要求主密钥能够轻松创建、轮换和禁用，以确保安全性。应使用哪种解决方案来满足这些要求？

- [ ] SSE with Amazon S3 managed keys (SSE-S3). `使用 Amazon S3 管理密钥的 SSE（SSE-S3）。`
- [ ] SSE with AWS KMS managed keys (SSE-KMS). `使用 AWS KMS 管理密钥的 SSE（SSE-KMS）。`
- [x] SSE with AWS Secrets Manager. `使用 AWS Secrets Manager 的 SSE。`
- [ ] SSE with customer-provided encryption keys. `使用客户提供的加密密钥的 SSE。`

**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Developer is migrating an on-premises application to AWS. The application currently takes user uploads and saves them to a local directory on the server. All uploads must be saved and made immediately available to all instances in an Auto Scaling group. Which approach will meet these requirements?
> 开发人员正在将一个本地应用程序迁移到 AWS。该应用程序当前接收用户上传并将其保存到服务器上的本地目录中。所有上传必须保存并立即对 Auto Scaling 组中的所有实例可用。哪种方法可以满足这些要求？

- [ ] Use Amazon EBS and configure the application AMI to use a snapshot of the same EBS instance on boot. `使用 Amazon EBS，并配置应用程序 AMI 在启动时使用相同 EBS 实例的快照。`
- [x] Use Amazon S3 and rearchitect the application so all uploads are placed in S3. `使用 Amazon S3，并重新构建应用程序，使所有上传都放置在 S3 中。`
- [ ] Use instance storage and share it between instances launched from the same Amazon Machine Image (AMI). `使用实例存储并在从同一 Amazon Machine Image (AMI) 启动的实例之间共享。`
- [ ] Use Amazon EBS and file synchronization software to achieve eventual consistency among the Auto Scaling group. `使用 Amazon EBS 和文件同步软件在 Auto Scaling 组之间实现最终一致性。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Developer implemented a static website hosted in Amazon S3 that makes web service requests hosted in Amazon API Gateway and AWS Lambda. The site is showing an error that reads: 'No 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin' header is present on the requested resource. Origin 'null' is therefore not allowed access.' What should the Developer do to resolve this issue?
> 开发人员在 Amazon S3 中实现了一个静态网站，该网站向托管在 Amazon API Gateway 和 AWS Lambda 中的 Web 服务发送请求。该网站显示错误：“请求的资源上不存在 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin' 头。来源 'null' 因此不允许访问。”开发人员应如何解决此问题？

- [ ] Enable cross-origin resource sharing (CORS) on the S3 bucket. `在 S3 存储桶上启用跨源资源共享（CORS）。`
- [x] Enable cross-origin resource sharing (CORS) for the method in API Gateway. `在 API Gateway 中为该方法启用跨源资源共享（CORS）。`
- [ ] Add the Access-Control-Request-Method header to the request. `在请求中添加 Access-Control-Request-Method 头。`
- [ ] Add the Access-Control-Request-Headers header to the request. `在请求中添加 Access-Control-Request-Headers 头。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Developer is building an application that needs to store data in Amazon S3. Management requires that the data be encrypted before it is sent to Amazon S3 for storage. The encryption keys need to be managed by the Security team. Which approach should the Developer take to meet these requirements?
> 开发人员正在构建一个需要将数据存储在 Amazon S3 中的应用程序。管理层要求在将数据发送到 Amazon S3 进行存储之前对其进行加密。加密密钥需要由安全团队管理。开发人员应采取哪种方法来满足这些要求？

- [ ] Implement server-side encryption using customer-provided encryption keys (SSE-C). `使用客户提供的加密密钥（SSE-C）实施服务器端加密。`
- [ ] Implement server-side encryption by using a client-side master key. `使用客户端主密钥实施服务器端加密。`
- [x] Implement client-side encryption using an AWS KMS managed customer master key (CMK). `使用 AWS KMS 管理的客户主密钥（CMK）实施客户端加密。`
- [ ] Implement client-side encryption using Amazon S3 managed keys. `使用 Amazon S3 管理的密钥实施客户端加密。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Developer has written an Amazon Kinesis Data Streams application. As usage grows and traffic increases over time, the application is regularly receiving ProvisionedThroughputExceededException error messages. Which steps should the Developer take to resolve the error? (Choose TWO)
> 开发人员编写了一个 Amazon Kinesis Data Streams 应用程序。随着使用量的增长和流量的增加，该应用程序定期收到 ProvisionedThroughputExceededException 错误消息。开发人员应该采取哪些步骤来解决此错误？（选择两个）

- [ ] Use Auto Scaling to scale the stream for better performance. `使用自动缩放来扩展流以获得更好的性能。`
- [ ] Increase the delay between the GetRecords call and the PutRecords call. `增加 GetRecords 调用和 PutRecords 调用之间的延迟。`
- [x] Increase the number of shards in the data stream. `增加数据流中的分片数量。`
- [ ] Specify a shard iterator using the ShardIterator parameter. `使用 ShardIterator 参数指定分片迭代器。`
- [x] Implement exponential backoff on the GetRecords call and the PutRecords call. `在 GetRecords 调用和 PutRecords 调用中实现指数退避。`

### A Developer is publishing critical log data to a log group in Amazon CloudWatch Logs, which was created 2 months ago. The Developer must encrypt the log data using an AWS KMS customer master key (CMK) so future data can be encrypted to comply with the company's security policy. How can the Developer meet this requirement?
> 开发人员正在将关键日志数据发布到 2 个月前创建的 Amazon CloudWatch Logs 中的日志组。开发人员必须使用 AWS KMS 客户主密钥（CMK）加密日志数据，以便未来的数据能够加密以遵循公司的安全政策。开发人员如何满足此要求？

- [ ] Use the CloudWatch Logs console and enable the encrypt feature on the log group. `使用 CloudWatch Logs 控制台并在日志组上启用加密功能。`
- [ ] Use the AWS CLI create-log-group command and specify the key Amazon Resource Name (ARN). `使用 AWS CLI create-log-group 命令并指定密钥的 Amazon 资源名称（ARN）。`
- [ ] Use the KMS console and associate the CMK with the log group. `使用 KMS 控制台并将 CMK 与日志组关联。`
- [x] Use the AWS CLI associate-kms-key command and specify the key Amazon Resource Name (ARN). `使用 AWS CLI associate-kms-key 命令并指定密钥的 Amazon 资源名称（ARN）。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Developer has code running on Amazon EC2 instances that needs read-only access to an Amazon DynamoDB table. What is the MOST secure approach the Developer should take to accomplish this task?
> 开发人员在 Amazon EC2 实例上运行的代码需要对 Amazon DynamoDB 表具有只读访问权限。开发人员应该采取什么措施来实现这一任务，以确保安全性？

- [ ] Create a user access key for each EC2 instance with read-only access to DynamoDB. Place the keys in the code. Redeploy the code as keys rotate. `为每个 EC2 实例创建一个具有 DynamoDB 只读访问权限的用户访问密钥。将密钥放入代码中。随着密钥轮换重新部署代码。`
- [x] Use an IAM role with an AmazonDynamoDBReadOnlyAccess policy applied to the EC2 instances. `使用一个 IAM 角色，并将 AmazonDynamoDBReadOnlyAccess 策略应用于 EC2 实例。`
- [ ] Run all code with only AWS account root user access keys to ensure maximum access to services. `仅使用 AWS 账户根用户访问密钥运行所有代码，以确保对服务的最大访问。`
- [ ] Use an IAM role with Administrator access applied to the EC2 instance. `使用具有管理员访问权限的 IAM 角色应用于 EC2 实例。`

### A Developer migrated a web application to AWS. As part of the migration, the Developer implemented an automated continuous integration/continuous improvement (CI/CD) process using a blue/green deployment. The deployment provisions new Amazon EC2 instances in an Auto Scaling group behind a new Application Load Balancer. After the migration was completed, the Developer began receiving complaints from users getting booted out of the system. The system also requires users to log in after every new deployment. How can these issues be resolved?
> 开发人员将一个 Web 应用程序迁移到 AWS。作为迁移的一部分，开发人员实现了使用蓝绿部署的自动化持续集成/持续改进（CI/CD）过程。该部署在一个新的应用程序负载均衡器后面，在 Auto Scaling 组中配置新的 Amazon EC2 实例。迁移完成后，开发人员开始收到用户被踢出系统的投诉。该系统还要求用户在每次新部署后重新登录。如何解决这些问题？

- [ ] Use rolling updates instead of a blue/green deployment. `使用滚动更新而不是蓝绿部署。`
- [x] Externalize the user sessions to Amazon ElastiCache. `将用户会话外部化到 Amazon ElastiCache。`
- [ ] Turn on sticky sessions in the Application Load Balancer. `在应用程序负载均衡器中开启粘性会话。`
- [ ] Use multicast to replicate session information. `使用多播来复制会话信息。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Developer wants to insert a record into an Amazon DynamoDB table as soon as a new file is added to an Amazon S3 bucket. Which set of steps would be necessary to achieve this?
> 开发人员希望在将新文件添加到 Amazon S3 存储桶时立即向 Amazon DynamoDB 表中插入一条记录。为了实现这一目标，需要哪些步骤？

- [ ] Create an event with Amazon CloudWatch Events that will monitor the S3 bucket and then insert the records into DynamoDB. `使用 Amazon CloudWatch Events 创建一个事件，监控 S3 存储桶，然后将记录插入 DynamoDB。`
- [x] Configure an S3 event to invoke a Lambda function that inserts records into DynamoDB. `配置一个 S3 事件，以调用插入记录到 DynamoDB 的 Lambda 函数。`
- [ ] Create a Lambda function that will poll the S3 bucket and then insert the records into DynamoDB. `创建一个 Lambda 函数来轮询 S3 存储桶，然后将记录插入 DynamoDB。`
- [ ] Create a cron job that will run at a scheduled time and insert the records into DynamoDB. `创建一个计划任务，在预定时间运行并插入记录到 DynamoDB。`

### A company has implemented AWS CodeDeploy as part of its cloud native CI/CD stack. The company enables automatic rollbacks while deploying a new version of a popular web application from in-place to Amazon EC2. What occurs if the deployment of the new version fails due to code regression?
> 一家公司已将 AWS CodeDeploy 作为其云原生 CI/CD 堆栈的一部分。该公司在将流行 Web 应用程序的新版本从原地部署到 Amazon EC2 时启用了自动回滚。如果由于代码回归导致新版本的部署失败，会发生什么情况？

- [ ] The last known good deployment is automatically restored using the snapshot stored in Amazon S3. `使用存储在 Amazon S3 中的快照自动恢复最后一个已知的良好部署。`
- [x] CodeDeploy switches the Amazon Route 53 alias records back to the known good green deployment and terminates the failed blue deployment. `CodeDeploy 将 Amazon Route 53 别名记录切换回已知的良好绿色部署，并终止失败的蓝色部署。`
- [ ] A new deployment of the last known version of the application is deployed with a new deployment ID. `最后一个已知版本的应用程序的新部署会使用新的部署 ID 进行部署。`
- [ ] AWS CodePipeline promotes the most recent deployment with a SUCCEEDED status to production. `AWS CodePipeline 将最新的状态为 SUCCEEDED 的部署推广到生产环境。`

### A Developer uses Amazon S3 buckets for static website hosting. The Developer creates one S3 bucket for the code and another S3 bucket for the assets, such as image and video files. Access is denied when a user attempts to access the assets bucket from the code bucket, with the website application showing a 403 error. How should the Developer solve this issue?
> 开发人员使用 Amazon S3 存储桶进行静态网站托管。开发人员创建一个 S3 存储桶用于代码，另一个 S3 存储桶用于资产，例如图像和视频文件。当用户尝试从代码存储桶访问资产存储桶时，访问被拒绝，网站应用程序显示 403 错误。开发人员应该如何解决此问题？

- [ ] Create an IAM role and apply it to the assets bucket for the code bucket to be granted access. `创建一个 IAM 角色并将其应用于资产存储桶，以便授予代码存储桶访问权限。`
- [x] Edit the bucket policy of the assets bucket to allow access from the code bucket. `编辑资产存储桶的桶策略以允许来自代码存储桶的访问。`
- [ ] Edit the bucket policy of the assets bucket to open access to all principals. `编辑资产存储桶的桶策略以向所有主体开放访问。`
- [ ] Change the code bucket to use AWS Lambda functions instead of static website hosting. `将代码存储桶更改为使用 AWS Lambda 函数而不是静态网站托管。`

### A company has implemented AWS CodePipeline to automate its release pipelines. The Development team is writing an AWS Lambda function that will send notifications for state changes of each of the actions in the stages. Which steps must be taken to associate the Lambda function with the event source?
> 一家公司实施了 AWS CodePipeline 来自动化其发布管道。开发团队正在编写一个 AWS Lambda 函数，用于发送每个阶段中每个操作状态更改的通知。必须采取哪些步骤将 Lambda 函数与事件源关联？

- [ ] Create a trigger that invokes the Lambda function from the Lambda console by selecting CodePipeline as the event source. `从 Lambda 控制台创建一个触发器，选择 CodePipeline 作为事件源以调用 Lambda 函数。`
- [x] Create an event trigger and specify the Lambda function from the CodePipeline console. `创建一个事件触发器并从 CodePipeline 控制台指定 Lambda 函数。`
- [ ] Create an Amazon CloudWatch alarm that monitors status changes in Code Pipeline and triggers the Lambda function. `创建一个 Amazon CloudWatch 警报，监控 CodePipeline 中的状态更改并触发 Lambda 函数。`
- [ ] Create an Amazon CloudWatch Events rule that uses CodePipeline as an event source. `创建一个使用 CodePipeline 作为事件源的 Amazon CloudWatch Events 规则。`

### A Developer has built an application running on AWS Lambda using AWS Serverless Application Model (AWS SAM). What is the correct order of execution to successfully deploy the application?
> 开发人员使用 AWS 无服务器应用程序模型（AWS SAM）构建了一个在 AWS Lambda 上运行的应用程序。成功部署应用程序的正确执行顺序是什么？

- [ ] 1. Build the SAM template in Amazon EC2. 2. Package the SAM template to Amazon EBS storage. 3. Deploy the SAM template from Amazon EBS. `1. 在 Amazon EC2 中构建 SAM 模板。2. 将 SAM 模板打包到 Amazon EBS 存储。3. 从 Amazon EBS 部署 SAM 模板。`
- [x] 1. Build the SAM template locally. 2. Package the SAM template onto Amazon S3. 3. Deploy the SAM template from Amazon S3. `1. 在本地构建 SAM 模板。2. 将 SAM 模板打包到 Amazon S3。3. 从 Amazon S3 部署 SAM 模板。`
- [ ] 1. Build the SAM template locally. 2. Deploy the SAM template from Amazon S3. 3. Package the SAM template for use. `1. 在本地构建 SAM 模板。2. 从 Amazon S3 部署 SAM 模板。3. 打包 SAM 模板以供使用。`
- [ ] 1. Build the SAM template locally. 2. Package the SAM template from AWS CodeCommit. 3. Deploy the SAM template to CodeCommit. `1. 在本地构建 SAM 模板。2. 从 AWS CodeCommit 打包 SAM 模板。3. 部署 SAM 模板到 CodeCommit。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A company wants to migrate an imaging service to Amazon EC2 while following security best practices. The images are sourced and read from a non-public Amazon S3 bucket. What should a Developer do to meet these requirements?
> 一家公司希望将成像服务迁移到 Amazon EC2，同时遵循安全最佳实践。图像来自非公共的 Amazon S3 存储桶并被读取。开发人员应该怎么做才能满足这些要求？

- [ ] Create an IAM user with read-only permissions for the S3 bucket. Temporarily store the user credentials in the Amazon EBS volume of the EC2 instance. `创建一个具有 S3 存储桶只读权限的 IAM 用户。将用户凭证临时存储在 EC2 实例的 Amazon EBS 卷中。`
- [ ] Create an IAM user with read-only permissions for the S3 bucket. Temporarily store the user credentials in the user data of the EC2 instance. `创建一个具有 S3 存储桶只读权限的 IAM 用户。将用户凭证临时存储在 EC2 实例的用户数据中。`
- [x] Create an EC2 service role with read-only permissions for the S3 bucket. Attach the role to the EC2 instance. `创建一个具有 S3 存储桶只读权限的 EC2 服务角色。将该角色附加到 EC2 实例。`
- [ ] Create an S3 service role with read-only permissions for the S3 bucket. Attach the role to the EC2 instance. `创建一个具有 S3 存储桶只读权限的 S3 服务角色。将该角色附加到 EC2 实例。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Development team wants to immediately build and deploy an application whenever there is a change to the source code. Which approaches could be used to trigger the deployment? (Choose TWO)
> 开发团队希望在源代码发生更改时立即构建和部署应用程序。可以使用哪些方法来触发部署？（选择两个）

- [ ] Store the source code in an Amazon S3 bucket. Configure AWS CodePipeline to start whenever a file in the bucket changes. `将源代码存储在 Amazon S3 存储桶中。配置 AWS CodePipeline，以便在存储桶中的文件更改时启动。`
- [x] Store the source code in an encrypted Amazon EBS volume. Configure AWS CodePipeline to start whenever a file in the volume changes. `将源代码存储在加密的 Amazon EBS 卷中。配置 AWS CodePipeline，以便在卷中的文件更改时启动。`
- [x] Store the source code in an AWS CodeCommit repository. Configure AWS CodePipeline to start whenever a change is committed to the repository. `将源代码存储在 AWS CodeCommit 存储库中。配置 AWS CodePipeline，以便在对存储库进行更改时启动。`
- [ ] Store the source code in an Amazon S3 bucket. Configure AWS CodePipeline to start every 15 minutes. `将源代码存储在 Amazon S3 存储桶中。配置 AWS CodePipeline 每 15 分钟启动一次。`
- [ ] Store the source code in an Amazon EC2 instance's ephemeral storage. Configure the instance to start AWS CodePipeline whenever there are changes to the source code. `将源代码存储在 Amazon EC2 实例的临时存储中。配置实例在源代码发生更改时启动 AWS CodePipeline。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### An application ingests a large number of small messages and stores them in a database. The application uses AWS Lambda. A Development team is making changes to the application's processing logic. In testing, it is taking more than 15 minutes to process each message. The team is concerned the current backend may time out. Which changes should be made to the backend system to ensure each message is processed in the MOST scalable way?
> 一个应用程序接收大量小消息并将其存储在数据库中。该应用程序使用 AWS Lambda。开发团队正在对应用程序的处理逻辑进行更改。在测试中，处理每条消息的时间超过 15 分钟。团队担心当前的后端可能会超时。应对后端系统进行哪些更改以确保以最可扩展的方式处理每条消息？

- [ ] Add the messages to an Amazon SQS queue. Set up an Amazon EC2 instance to poll the queue and process messages as they arrive. `将消息添加到 Amazon SQS 队列。设置一个 Amazon EC2 实例以轮询队列并处理到达的消息。`
- [x] Add the messages to an Amazon SQS queue. Set up Amazon EC2 instances in an Auto Scaling group to poll the queue and process the messages as they arrive. `将消息添加到 Amazon SQS 队列。设置一个 Auto Scaling 组中的 Amazon EC2 实例以轮询队列并处理到达的消息。`
- [ ] Create a support ticket to increase the Lambda timeout to 60 minutes to allow for increased processing time. `创建一个支持工单以将 Lambda 超时时间增加到 60 分钟，以允许增加处理时间。`
- [ ] Change the application to directly insert the body of the message into an Amazon RDS database. `更改应用程序以直接将消息主体插入 Amazon RDS 数据库。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Software Engineer developed an AWS Lambda function in Node.js to do some CPU-intensive data processing. With the default settings, the Lambda function takes about 5 minutes to complete. Which approach should a Developer take to increase the speed of completion?
> 一名软件工程师开发了一个用 Node.js 编写的 AWS Lambda 函数，用于进行一些 CPU 密集型的数据处理。在默认设置下，该 Lambda 函数完成大约需要 5 分钟。开发人员应该采取哪种方法来提高完成速度？

- [ ] Instead of using Node.js, rewrite the Lambda function using Python. `不要使用 Node.js，而是使用 Python 重写 Lambda 函数。`
- [ ] Instead of packaging the libraries in the ZIP file with the function, move them to a Lambda layer and use the layer with the function. `不要将库打包在 ZIP 文件中，而是将它们移动到 Lambda 层并与函数一起使用。`
- [ ] Allocate the maximum available CPU units to the function. `将可用的最大 CPU 单元分配给该函数。`
- [x] Increase the available memory to the function. `增加函数可用的内存。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### An online retail company has deployed a serverless application with AWS Lambda, Amazon API Gateway, Amazon S3, and Amazon DynamoDB using AWS CloudFormation. The company rolled out a new release with major upgrades to the Lambda function and deployed the release to production. Subsequently, the application stopped working. Which solution should bring the application back up as quickly as possible?
> 一家在线零售公司使用 AWS CloudFormation 部署了一个无服务器应用程序，该应用程序包括 AWS Lambda、Amazon API Gateway、Amazon S3 和 Amazon DynamoDB。公司推出了一个新版本，对 Lambda 函数进行了重大升级并将其部署到生产环境中。随后，应用程序停止工作。哪种解决方案应该尽快使应用程序恢复运行？

- [ ] Redeploy the application on Amazon EC2 so the Lambda function can resolve dependencies. `在 Amazon EC2 上重新部署应用程序，以便 Lambda 函数可以解决依赖关系。`
- [ ] Migrate DynamoDB to Amazon RDS and redeploy the Lambda function. `将 DynamoDB 迁移到 Amazon RDS 并重新部署 Lambda 函数。`
- [x] Roll back the Lambda function to the previous version. `将 Lambda 函数回滚到先前的版本。`
- [ ] Deploy the latest Lambda function in a different Region. `在不同的区域中部署最新的 Lambda 函数。`

### A Developer is writing an application that will run on Amazon EC2 instances in an Auto Scaling group. The Developer wants to externalize session state to support the application. Which services will meet these needs? (Choose TWO)
> 开发人员正在编写一个将在 Auto Scaling 组中的 Amazon EC2 实例上运行的应用程序。开发人员希望将会话状态外部化以支持该应用程序。哪些服务可以满足这些需求？（选择两个）

- [x] Amazon DynamoDB. 
- [ ] Amazon Cognito. 
- [x] Amazon ElastiCache. 
- [ ] Amazon EBS. 
- [ ] Amazon SQS.
