### A Developer has a legacy application that is hosted on-premises. Other applications hosted on AWS depend on the on-premises application for proper functioning. In case of any application errors, the Developer wants to be able to use Amazon CloudWatch to monitor and troubleshoot all applications from one place. How can the Developer accomplish this?
> 开发人员有一个托管在本地的遗留应用程序。其他托管在 AWS 上的应用程序依赖于本地应用程序的正常运行。开发人员希望能够使用 Amazon CloudWatch 从一个地方监控和排除所有应用程序的故障。如果出现任何应用程序错误，开发人员该如何实现？

- [ ] Install an AWS SDK on the on-premises server to automatically send logs to CloudWatch. `在本地服务器上安装 AWS SDK 以自动将日志发送到 CloudWatch。`
- [x] Download the CloudWatch agent to the on-premises server. Configure the agent to use IAM user credentials with permissions for CloudWatch. `将 CloudWatch 代理下载到本地服务器。配置代理以使用具有 CloudWatch 权限的 IAM 用户凭证。`
- [ ] Upload log files from the on-premises server to Amazon S3 and have CloudWatch read the files. `从本地服务器将日志文件上传到 Amazon S3，并让 CloudWatch 读取文件。`
- [ ] Upload log files from the on-premises server to an Amazon EC2 instance and have the instance forward the logs to CloudWatch. `从本地服务器将日志文件上传到 Amazon EC2 实例，并让该实例将日志转发到 CloudWatch。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A company is developing an application that will be accessed through the Amazon API Gateway REST API. Registered users should be the only ones who can access certain resources of this API. The token being used should expire automatically and needs to be refreshed periodically. How can a Developer meet these requirements?
> 一家公司正在开发一个将通过 Amazon API Gateway REST API 访问的应用程序。只有注册用户才能访问此 API 的某些资源。所使用的令牌应自动过期，并需要定期刷新。开发人员如何满足这些要求？

- [ ] Create an Amazon Cognito identity pool, configure the Amazon Cognito Authorizer in API Gateway, and use the temporary credentials generated by the identity pool. `创建一个 Amazon Cognito 身份池，在 API Gateway 中配置 Amazon Cognito 授权者，并使用身份池生成的临时凭证。`
- [ ] Create and maintain a database record for each user with a corresponding token and use an AWS Lambda authorizer in API Gateway. `为每个用户创建并维护一个数据库记录及相应的令牌，并在 API Gateway 中使用 AWS Lambda 授权者。`
- [x] Create an Amazon Cognito user pool, configure the Cognito Authorizer in API Gateway, and use the identity or access token. `创建一个 Amazon Cognito 用户池，在 API Gateway 中配置 Cognito 授权者，并使用身份或访问令牌。`
- [ ] Create an IAM user for each API user, attach an invoke permissions policy to the API, and use an IAM authorizer in API Gateway. `为每个 API 用户创建一个 IAM 用户，为 API 附加一个调用权限策略，并在 API Gateway 中使用 IAM 授权者。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Developer is working on a serverless project based in Java. Initial testing shows a cold start takes about 8 seconds on average for AWS Lambda functions. What should the Developer do to reduce the cold start time? (Choose TWO)
> 一名开发人员正在进行一个基于 Java 的无服务器项目。初步测试显示，AWS Lambda 函数的冷启动平均需要约 8 秒。开发人员应该做什么来减少冷启动时间？（选择两个）

- [x] Add the Spring Framework to the project and enable dependency injection. `将 Spring 框架添加到项目中并启用依赖注入。`
- [ ] Reduce the deployment package by including only needed modules from the AWS SDK for Java. `通过仅包含 AWS SDK for Java 中所需的模块来减少部署包。`
- [ ] Increase the memory allocation setting for the Lambda function. `增加 Lambda 函数的内存分配设置。`
- [ ] Increase the timeout setting for the Lambda function. `增加 Lambda 函数的超时设置。`
- [x] Change the Lambda invocation mode from synchronous to asynchronous. `将 Lambda 调用模式从同步更改为异步。`

### A Developer is leveraging a Border Gateway Protocol (BGP)-based AWS VPN connection to connect from on-premises to Amazon EC2 instances in the Developer's account. The Developer is able to access an EC2 instance in subnet A, but is unable to access an EC2 instance in subnet B in the same VPC. Which logs can the Developer use to verify whether the traffic is reaching subnet B?
> 开发人员正在利用基于边界网关协议（BGP）的 AWS VPN 连接，从本地连接到开发人员账户中的 Amazon EC2 实例。开发人员能够访问子网 A 中的 EC2 实例，但无法访问同一 VPC 中子网 B 的 EC2 实例。开发人员可以使用哪些日志来验证流量是否到达子网 B？

- [ ] VPN logs. `VPN 日志。`
- [ ] BGP logs `BGP 日志。`
- [x] VPC Flow Logs. `VPC 流日志。`
- [ ] AWS CloudTrail logs. `AWS CloudTrail 日志。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Developer has created a new AWS IAM user that has s3 putObject permission to write to a specific Amazon S3 bucket. This S3 bucket uses server-side encryption with AWS KMS managed keys (SSE-KMS) as the default encryption. Using the access key and secret key of the IAM user, the application received an access denied error when calling the PutObject API. How can this issue be resolved?
> 开发人员创建了一个具有 s3 putObject 权限的新 AWS IAM 用户，以写入特定的 Amazon S3 存储桶。该 S3 存储桶使用 AWS KMS 管理的密钥 (SSE-KMS) 进行服务器端加密作为默认加密。使用 IAM 用户的访问密钥和秘密密钥，应用程序在调用 PutObject API 时收到访问被拒绝的错误。如何解决此问题？

- [ ] Update the policy of the IAM user to allow the s3 Encrypt action. `更新 IAM 用户的策略以允许 s3 Encrypt 操作。`
- [ ] Update the bucket policy of the S3 bucket to allow the IAM user to upload objects. `更新 S3 存储桶的存储桶策略，以允许 IAM 用户上传对象。`
- [x] Update the policy of the IAM user to allow the kms:GenerateDataKey action. `更新 IAM 用户的策略以允许 kms:GenerateDataKey 操作。`
- [ ] Update the ACL of the S3 bucket to allow the IAM user to upload objects. `更新 S3 存储桶的 ACL 以允许 IAM 用户上传对象。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A company has a web application that uses an Amazon Cognito user pool for authentication. The company wants to create a login page with the company logo. What should a Developer do to meet these requirements?
> 一家公司有一个使用 Amazon Cognito 用户池进行身份验证的 web 应用程序。公司希望创建一个带有公司标志的登录页面。开发人员应该怎么做才能满足这些要求？

- [ ] Create a hosted user interface in Amazon Cognito and customize it with the company logo. `在 Amazon Cognito 中创建一个托管的用户界面，并使用公司标志进行自定义。`
- [ ] Create a login page with the company logo and upload it to Amazon Cognito. `创建带有公司标志的登录页面，并将其上传到 Amazon Cognito。`
- [ ] Create a login page in Amazon API Gateway with the logo and save the link in Amazon Cognito. `在 Amazon API Gateway 中创建带有公司标志的登录页面，并将链接保存在 Amazon Cognito 中。`
- [x] Upload the logo to the Amazon Cognito app settings and point to the logo on a custom login page. `将标志上传到 Amazon Cognito 应用程序设置中，并在自定义登录页面上指向该标志。`

### A Developer is working on an AWS Lambda function that accesses Amazon DynamoDB. The Lambda function must retrieve an item and update some of its attributes, or create the item if it does not exist. The Lambda function has access to the primary key. Which IAM permissions should the Developer request for the Lambda function to achieve this functionality?
> 开发人员正在开发一个访问 Amazon DynamoDB 的 AWS Lambda 函数。该 Lambda 函数必须检索一个项目并更新其某些属性，或者如果项目不存在则创建它。Lambda 函数可以访问主键。开发人员应为 Lambda 函数请求哪些 IAM 权限以实现此功能？

- [ ] dynamodb:DeleteItem dynamodb:GetItem dynamodb:PutItem.
- [ ] dynamodb:UpdateItem dynamodb:GetItem dynamodb:DescribeTable.
- [ ] dynamodb:GetRecords dynamodb:PutItem dynamodb:UpdateTable.
- [x] dynamodb:UpdateItem dynamodb:GetItem dynamodb:PutItem.

### A Developer is storing sensitive data generated by an application in Amazon S3. The Developer wants to encrypt the data at rest. A company policy requires an audit trail of when the master key was used and by whom. Which encryption option will meet these requirements?
> 开发人员正在将应用程序生成的敏感数据存储在 Amazon S3 中。开发人员希望对静态数据进行加密。公司政策要求提供主密钥何时被使用以及由谁使用的审计记录。哪种加密选项可以满足这些要求？

- [ ] Server-side encryption with Amazon S3 managed keys (SSE-S3). `使用 Amazon S3 管理的密钥进行服务器端加密 (SSE-S3)。`
- [x] Server-side encryption with AWS KMS managed keys (SSE-KMS). `使用 AWS KMS 管理的密钥进行服务器端加密 (SSE-KMS)。`
- [ ] Server-side encryption with customer-provided keys (SSE-C). `使用客户提供的密钥进行服务器端加密 (SSE-C)。`
- [ ] Server-side encryption with self-managed keys. `使用自管密钥进行服务器端加密。`

### A company's website runs on an Amazon EC2 instance and uses Auto Scaling to scale the environment during peak times. Website users across the world are experiencing high latency due to static content on the EC2 instance, even during non-peak hours. Which combination of steps will resolve the latency issue? (Choose TWO)
> 一家公司的网站运行在 Amazon EC2 实例上，并使用 Auto Scaling 在高峰时刻扩展环境。全球的用户在非高峰时段也由于 EC2 实例上的静态内容而遇到高延迟问题。哪些步骤组合可以解决延迟问题？（选择两个）

- [ ] Double the Auto Scaling group's maximum number of servers. `将 Auto Scaling 组的最大服务器数量增加一倍。`
- [ ] Host the application code on AWS Lambda. `将应用程序代码托管在 AWS Lambda 上。`
- [ ] Scale vertically by resizing the EC2 instances. `通过调整 EC2 实例的大小进行垂直扩展。`
- [x] Create an Amazon CloudFront distribution to cache the static content. `创建 Amazon CloudFront 分发以缓存静态内容。`
- [x] Store the application's static content in Amazon S3. `将应用程序的静态内容存储在 Amazon S3 中。`

### A company is developing a web application that allows its employees to upload a profile picture to a private Amazon S3 bucket. There is no size limit for the profile pictures, which should be displayed every time an employee logs in. For security reasons, the pictures cannot be publicly accessible. What is a viable long-term solution for this scenario?
> 一家公司正在开发一个网络应用程序，允许其员工将个人资料照片上传到一个私有的 Amazon S3 存储桶。个人资料照片没有大小限制，并且应在员工每次登录时显示。出于安全原因，这些照片不能公开访问。针对这种情况，什么是可行的长期解决方案？

- [ ] Generate a presigned URL when a picture is uploaded. Save the URL in an Amazon DynamoDB table. Return the URL to the browser when the employee logs in. `在上传图片时生成一个预签名 URL。将该 URL 保存在 Amazon DynamoDB 表中。当员工登录时，将 URL 返回给浏览器。`
- [x] Save the picture's S3 key in an Amazon DynamoDB table. Create an Amazon S3 VPC endpoint to allow the employees to download pictures once they log in. `将图片的 S3 键保存在 Amazon DynamoDB 表中。创建一个 Amazon S3 VPC 终端节点，允许员工登录后下载图片。`
- [ ] Encode a picture using base64. Save the base64 string in an Amazon DB table. Allow the browser to retrieve the string and convert it to a picture. `使用 base64 编码图片。将 base64 字符串保存在 Amazon 数据库表中。允许浏览器检索该字符串并将其转换为图片。`
- [ ] Save the picture's S3 key in an Amazon DynamoDB table. Use a function to generate a presigned URL every time an employee logs in. Return the URL to the browser. `将图片的 S3 键保存在 Amazon DynamoDB 表中。每次员工登录时，使用一个函数生成预签名 URL 并返回给浏览器。`

### A Developer is going to deploy an AWS Lambda function that requires significant CPU utilization. Which approach will MINIMIZE the average runtime of the function?
> 一名开发人员准备部署一个需要大量 CPU 利用率的 AWS Lambda 函数。哪种方法可以最大限度地减少该函数的平均运行时间？

- [ ] Deploy the function into multiple AWS Regions. `将该函数部署到多个 AWS 区域。`
- [ ] Deploy the function into multiple Availability Zones. `将该函数部署到多个可用区。`
- [ ] Deploy the function using Lambda layers. `使用 Lambda 层部署该函数。`
- [x] Deploy the function with its memory allocation set to the maximum amount. `将该函数的内存分配设置为最大值进行部署。`

### A company has a legacy application that was migrated to a fleet of Amazon EC2 instances. The application stores data in a MySQL database that is currently installed on a single EC2 instance. The company has decided to migrate the database from the EC2 instance to MySQL on Amazon RDS. What should the Developer do to update the application to support data storage in Amazon RDS?
> 一家公司有一个已迁移到一组 Amazon EC2 实例上的旧应用程序。该应用程序将数据存储在当前安装在单个 EC2 实例上的 MySQL 数据库中。公司决定将数据库从 EC2 实例迁移到 Amazon RDS 上的 MySQL。开发人员应如何更新应用程序以支持在 Amazon RDS 中的数据存储？

- [x] Update the database connection parameters in the application to point to the new RDS instance. `更新应用程序中的数据库连接参数以指向新的 RDS 实例。`
- [ ] Add a script to the EC2 instance that implements an AWS SDK for requesting database credentials. `向 EC2 实例添加一个脚本，该脚本实现 AWS SDK 来请求数据库凭证。`
- [ ] Create a new EC2 instance with an IAM role that allows access to the new RDS database. `创建一个带有允许访问新 RDS 数据库的 IAM 角色的新 EC2 实例。`
- [ ] Create an AWS Lambda function that will route traffic, from the EC2 instance to the RDS database. `创建一个 AWS Lambda 函数，将流量从 EC2 实例路由到 RDS 数据库。`

### A Developer has an e-commerce API hosted on Amazon ECS. Variable and spiking demand on the application is causing order processing to take too long. The application processes Amazon SQS queues. The ApproximateNumberOfMessagesVisible metric spikes at very high values throughout the day, which cause Amazon CloudWatch alarm breaches. Other ECS metrics for the API containers are well within limits. What can the Developer implement to improve performance while keeping costs low?
> 一名开发人员托管了一个基于 Amazon ECS 的电子商务 API。应用程序的需求波动和激增导致订单处理时间过长。应用程序处理 Amazon SQS 队列。ApproximateNumberOfMessagesVisible 指标在一天中多次飙升至非常高的值，导致 Amazon CloudWatch 报警超限。API 容器的其他 ECS 指标均在限值内。开发人员可以实现什么来提高性能同时保持较低成本？

- [x] Step scaling policy. `分步缩放策略。`
- [ ] Target tracking scaling policy. `目标跟踪缩放策略。`
- [ ] Docker Swarm. `Docker Swarm。`
- [ ] Service scheduler. `服务调度器。`

### A company wants to implement authentication for its new REST service using Amazon API Gateway. To authenticate the calls, each request must include HTTP headers with a client ID and user ID. These credentials must be compared to authentication data in an Amazon DynamoDB table. What MUST the company do to implement this authentication in API Gateway?
> 一家公司希望使用 Amazon API Gateway 为其新的 REST 服务实施身份验证。为了验证调用，每个请求必须包含带有客户端 ID 和用户 ID 的 HTTP 头。这些凭证必须与 Amazon DynamoDB 表中的身份验证数据进行比较。公司必须采取什么措施来实现 API Gateway 中的身份验证？

- [x] Implement an AWS Lambda authorizer that references the DynamoDB authentication table. `实现一个引用 DynamoDB 身份验证表的 AWS Lambda 授权器。`
- [ ] Create a model that requires the credentials, then grant API Gateway access to the authentication table. `创建一个需要凭证的模型，然后授予 API Gateway 对身份验证表的访问权限。`
- [ ] Modify the integration requests to require the credentials, then grant API Gateway access to the authentication table. `修改集成请求以要求凭证，然后授予 API Gateway 对身份验证表的访问权限。`
- [ ] Implement an Amazon Cognito authorizer that references the DynamoDB authentication table. `实现一个引用 DynamoDB 身份验证表的 Amazon Cognito 授权器。`

### A Developer is trying to make API calls using SDK. The IAM user credentials used by the application require multi-factor authentication for all API calls. Which method should the Developer use to access the multi-factor authentication protected API?
> 一位开发者正在尝试使用 SDK 进行 API 调用。应用程序使用的 IAM 用户凭证要求所有 API 调用都进行多因素身份验证。开发者应该使用哪种方法来访问受多因素身份验证保护的 API？

### An application is running on a cluster of Amazon EC2 instances. While trying to read objects stored within a single Amazon S3 bucket that are encrypted with server-side encryption with AWS KMS managed keys (SSE-KMS), the application receives the following error. Which combination of steps should be taken to prevent this failure? (Choose TWO)
> 一个应用程序在一组 Amazon EC2 实例上运行。在尝试读取存储在单个 Amazon S3 存储桶中的使用 AWS KMS 管理密钥（SSE-KMS）加密的对象时，应用程序收到以下错误。为了防止这种失败，应采取哪两种步骤？（选择两个）

- [ ] Contact AWS Support to request an AWS KMS rate limit increase. `联系 AWS 支持请求增加 AWS KMS 速率限制。`
- [ ] Perform error retries with exponential backoff in the application code. `在应用程序代码中执行指数退避的错误重试。`
- [x] Contact AWS Support to request a S3 rate limit increase. `联系 AWS 支持请求增加 S3 速率限制。`
- [x] Import a customer master key (CMK) with a larger key size. `导入一个具有更大密钥大小的客户主密钥（CMK）。`
- [ ] Use more than one customer master key (CMK) to encrypt S3 data. `使用多个客户主密钥（CMK）来加密 S3 数据。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### When developing an AWS Lambda function that processes Amazon Kinesis Data Streams, Administrators within the company must receive a notice that includes the processed data. How should the Developer write the function to send processed data to the Administrators?
> 在开发一个处理 Amazon Kinesis 数据流的 AWS Lambda 函数时，公司内的管理员必须收到包含处理数据的通知。开发人员应如何编写函数以将处理后的数据发送给管理员？

- [ ] Separate the Lambda handler from the core logic. `将 Lambda 处理程序与核心逻辑分离。`
- [x] Use Amazon CloudWatch Events to send the processed data. `使用 Amazon CloudWatch Events 发送处理后的数据。`
- [ ] Publish the processed data to an Amazon SNS topic. `将处理后的数据发布到 Amazon SNS 主题。`
- [ ] Push the processed data to Amazon SQS. `将处理后的数据推送到 Amazon SQS。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Developer is storing sensitive documents in Amazon S3 that will require encryption at rest. The encryption keys must be rotated annually, at least. What is the easiest way to achieve this?
> 开发人员正在 Amazon S3 中存储需要静态加密的敏感文档。加密密钥必须至少每年轮换一次。实现这一目标的最简单方法是什么？

- [ ] Encrypt the data before sending it to Amazon S3. `在将数据发送到 Amazon S3 之前对其进行加密。`
- [x] Import a custom key into AWS KMS with annual rotation enabled. `将自定义密钥导入 AWS KMS，并启用年度轮换。`
- [ ] Use AWS KMS with automatic key rotation. `使用 AWS KMS 进行自动密钥轮换。`
- [ ] Export a key from AWS KMS to encrypt the data. `从 AWS KMS 导出密钥以加密数据。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A company is creating a REST service using an Amazon API Gateway with AWS Lambda integration. The service must run different versions for testing purposes. What would be the BEST way to accomplish this?
> 一家公司正在使用 Amazon API Gateway 和 AWS Lambda 集成创建 REST 服务。该服务必须运行不同版本以便进行测试。实现这一目标的最佳方法是什么？

- [ ] Use an x-Version header to denote which version is being called and pass that header to the Lambda function(s). `使用 x-Version 头来表示正在调用哪个版本，并将该头传递给 Lambda 函数。`
- [ ] Create an API Gateway Lambda authorizer to route API clients to the correct API version. `创建 API Gateway Lambda 授权器以将 API 客户端路由到正确的 API 版本。`
- [ ] Create an API Gateway resource policy to isolate versions and provide context to the Lambda function(s). `创建 API Gateway 资源策略以隔离版本并为 Lambda 函数提供上下文。`
- [x] Deploy the API versions as unique stages with unique endpoints and use stage variables to provide further context. `将 API 版本作为唯一阶段与唯一端点一起部署，并使用阶段变量提供进一步的上下文。`

### A Developer must encrypt a 100-GB object using AWS KMS. What is the BEST approach?
> 开发人员必须使用 AWS KMS 加密一个 100-GB 的对象。最佳方法是什么？

- [ ] Make an Encrypt API call to encrypt the plaintext data as ciphertext using a customer master key (CMK). `调用 Encrypt API 以使用客户主密钥 (CMK) 将明文数据加密为密文。`
- [ ] Make an Encrypt API call to encrypt the plaintext data as ciphertext using a customer master key (CMK) with imported key material. `调用 Encrypt API 以使用带有导入密钥材料的客户主密钥 (CMK) 将明文数据加密为密文。`
- [ ] Make an GenerateDataKey API call that returns a plaintext key and an encrypted copy of a data key. Use a plaintext key to encrypt the data. `调用 GenerateDataKey API，该 API 返回一个明文密钥和数据密钥的加密副本。使用明文密钥来加密数据。`
- [x] Make an GenerateDataKeyWithoutPlaintext API call that returns an encrypted copy of a data key. Use an encrypted key to encrypt the data. `调用 GenerateDataKeyWithoutPlaintext API，该 API 返回数据密钥的加密副本。使用加密密钥来加密数据。`

### After launching an instance that you intend to serve as a NAT (Network Address Translation) device in a public subnet you modify your route tables to have the NAT device be the target of internet bound traffic of your private subnet. When you try and make an outbound connection to the Internet from an instance in the private subnet, you are not successful. NAT device be the target of internet bound traffic of your private subnet. Which of the following steps could resolve the issue?
> 在启动一个实例以用作公共子网中的 NAT（网络地址转换）设备后，您修改了路由表，使 NAT 设备成为私有子网的互联网流量的目标。当您尝试从私有子网中的实例进行出站连接到 Internet 时，未能成功。NAT 设备成为私有子网的互联网流量的目标。以下哪个步骤可以解决此问题？

- [ ] Attaching a second Elastic Network interface (ENI) to the NAT instance, and placing it in the private subnet. `将第二个弹性网络接口 (ENI) 附加到 NAT 实例，并将其放置在私有子网中。`
- [ ] Attaching a second Elastic Network Interface (ENI) to the instance in the private subnet, and placing it in the public subnet. `将第二个弹性网络接口 (ENI) 附加到私有子网中的实例，并将其放置在公共子网中。`
- [x] Disabling the Source/Destination Check attribute on the NAT instance. `禁用 NAT 实例上的源/目标检查属性。`
- [ ] Attaching an Elastic IP address to the instance in the private subnet. `将弹性 IP 地址附加到私有子网中的实例。`

### You attempt to store an object in the US-STANDARD region in Amazon S3, and receive a confirmation that it has been successfully stored. You then immediately make another API call and attempt to read this object. S3 tells you that the object does not exist. What could explain this behavior?
> 您尝试在 Amazon S3 的 US-STANDARD 区域存储一个对象，并收到确认该对象已成功存储。然后，您立即进行另一个 API 调用并尝试读取该对象。S3 告诉您该对象不存在。什么可以解释这种行为？

- [x] US-STANDARD uses eventual consistency and it can take time for an object to be readable in a bucket. `US-STANDARD 使用最终一致性，可能需要一些时间才能在存储桶中读取对象。`
- [ ] Objects in Amazon S3 do not become visible until they are replicated to a second region. `在 Amazon S3 中，对象在复制到第二个区域之前不会变得可见。`
- [ ] US-STANDARD imposes a 1 second delay before new objects are readable. `US-STANDARD 在新对象可读之前会强加 1 秒的延迟。`
- [ ] You exceeded the bucket object limit, and once this limit is raised the object will be visible. `您超过了存储桶对象限制，一旦该限制提高，对象将变得可见。`

### A startup's photo-sharing site is deployed in a VPC. An ELB distributes web traffic across two subnets. ELB session stickiness is configured to use the AWS-generated session cookie, with a session TTL of 5 minutes. The webserver Auto Scaling Group is configured as: min-size=4, max-size=4. The startup's preparing for a public launch by running load-testing software installed on a single EC2 instance running in us-west-2. After 60 minutes of load-testing, the webserver logs show: Which recommendations can help ensure load-testing HTTP requests are evenly distributed across the four webservers? (Choose TWO)
> 一家初创公司的照片分享网站部署在VPC中。一个ELB将Web流量分配到两个子网。ELB会话粘性配置为使用AWS生成的会话cookie，会话TTL为5分钟。Web服务器自动扩展组的配置为：最小大小=4，最大大小=4。初创公司正在准备公共发布，运行在us-west-2中单个EC2实例上安装的负载测试软件。在60分钟的负载测试后，Web服务器日志显示：哪些建议可以帮助确保负载测试的HTTP请求均匀分布在四个Web服务器上？（选择两个）

- [ ] Launch and run the load-tester EC2 instance from us-east-1 instead. `改为从us-east-1启动并运行负载测试EC2实例。`
- [x] Re-configure the load-testing software to re-resolve DNS for each web request. `重新配置负载测试软件以在每个Web请求中重新解析DNS。`
- [x] Use a 3rd-party load-testing service which offers globally-distributed test clients. `使用提供全球分布式测试客户端的第三方负载测试服务。`
- [ ] Configure ELB and Auto Scaling to distribute across us-west-2a and us-west-2c. `配置ELB和自动扩展以在us-west-2a和us-west-2c之间分配。`
- [ ] Configure ELB session stickiness to use the app-specific session cookie. `配置ELB会话粘性以使用应用程序特定的会话cookie。`

### Company C has recently launched an online commerce site for bicycles on AWS. They have a 'Product' DynamoDB table that stores details for each bicycle, such as, manufacturer, color, price, quantity and size to display in the online store. Due to customer demand, they want to include an image for each bicycle along with the existing details. Which approach below provides the least impact to provisioned throughput on the 'Product' table?
> 公司C最近在AWS上推出了一个在线自行车商城。他们有一个“Product”DynamoDB表，用于存储每辆自行车的详细信息，例如制造商、颜色、价格、数量和尺寸，以便在在线商店中显示。由于客户需求，他们希望在现有详细信息中为每辆自行车添加一张图片。以下哪个方法对“Product”表的预配吞吐量影响最小？

- [ ] Serialize the image and store it in multiple DynamoDB tables. `序列化图片并将其存储在多个DynamoDB表中。`
- [ ] Create an 'Images' DynamoDB table to store the Image with a foreign key constraint to the 'Product' table. `创建一个“Images”DynamoDB表来存储图片，并与“Product”表建立外键约束。`
- [ ] Add an image data type to the 'Product' table to store the images in binary format. `在“Product”表中添加一个图像数据类型，以二进制格式存储图片。`
- [x] Store the images in Amazon S3 and add an S3 URL pointer to the 'Product' table item for each image. `将图片存储在Amazon S3中，并为“Product”表中的每个图片添加一个S3 URL指针。`

### When a Simple Queue Service message triggers a task that takes 5 minutes to complete, which process below will result in successful processing of the message and remove it from the queue while minimizing the chances of duplicate processing?
> 当一个简单队列服务消息触发一个需要5分钟完成的任务时，以下哪个过程将导致成功处理该消息并将其从队列中删除，同时最小化重复处理的可能性？

- [x] Retrieve the message with an increased visibility timeout, process the message, delete the message from the queue. `以增加的可见性超时检索消息，处理消息，然后从队列中删除消息。`
- [ ] Retrieve the message with an increased visibility timeout, delete the message from the queue, process the message. `以增加的可见性超时检索消息，从队列中删除消息，然后处理消息。`
- [ ] Retrieve the message with increased DelaySeconds, process the message, delete the message from the queue. `以增加的DelaySeconds检索消息，处理消息，然后从队列中删除消息。`
- [ ] Retrieve the message with increased DelaySeconds, delete the message from the queue, process the message. `以增加的DelaySeconds检索消息，从队列中删除消息，然后处理消息。`

### Company A has an S3 bucket containing premier content that they intend to make available to only paid subscribers of their website. The S3 bucket currently has default permissions of all objects being private to prevent inadvertent exposure of the premier content to non-paying website visitors. How can Company A provide only paid subscribers the ability to download a premier content file in the S3 bucket?
> 公司A有一个S3桶，其中包含他们打算仅向网站的付费订阅者提供的优质内容。该S3桶目前的默认权限是所有对象都是私有的，以防止优质内容意外暴露给未付费的网站访客。公司A如何仅向付费订阅者提供在S3桶中下载优质内容文件的能力？

- [ ] Apply a bucket policy that grants anonymous users to download the content from the S3 bucket. `应用一个桶策略，允许匿名用户从S3桶下载内容。`
- [x] Generate a pre-signed object URL for the premier content file when a paid subscriber requests a download. `在付费订阅者请求下载时，为优质内容文件生成一个预签名对象URL。`
- [ ] Add a bucket policy that requires Multi-Factor Authentication for requests to access the S3 bucket objects. `添加一个桶策略，要求请求访问S3桶对象时进行多因素认证。`
- [ ] Enable server side encryption on the S3 bucket for data protection against the non-paying website visitors. `在S3桶上启用服务器端加密，以保护数据免受未付费网站访客的影响。`

- [x] User ID, where the application has many different users. `用户ID，应用程序有许多不同的用户。`
- [ ] Status Code where most status codes are the same. `状态代码，大多数状态代码是相同的。`

### An application stores payroll information nightly in DynamoDB for a large number of employees across hundreds of offices. Item attributes consist of individual name, office identifier, and cumulative daily hours. Managers run reports for ranges of names working in their office. One query is. 'Return all Items in this office for names starting with A through E'. Which table configuration will result in the lowest impact on provisioned throughput for this query?
> 一款应用程序每晚在DynamoDB中存储大量员工的工资信息，涉及数百个办公室。项目属性包括个人姓名、办公室标识符和累积日工时。经理们根据在其办公室工作的姓名范围运行报告。一个查询是：“返回此办公室中以A到E开头的所有项目”。哪种表配置将对该查询的预置吞吐量产生最小影响？

- [ ] Configure the table to have a hash index on the name attribute, and a range index on the office identifier. `将表配置为在名称属性上具有哈希索引，并在办公室标识符上具有范围索引。`
- [x] Configure the table to have a range index on the name attribute, and a hash index on the office identifier. `将表配置为在名称属性上具有范围索引，并在办公室标识符上具有哈希索引。`
- [ ] Configure a hash index on the name attribute and no range index. `在名称属性上配置哈希索引，而不配置范围索引。`
- [ ] Configure a hash index on the office Identifier attribute and no range index. `在办公室标识符属性上配置哈希索引，而不配置范围索引。`

### Games-R-Us is launching a new game app for mobile devices. Users will log into the game using their existing Facebook account and the game will record player data and scoring information directly to a DynamoDB table. What is the most secure approach for signing requests to the DynamoDB API?

- [ ] Establish cross account access between the mobile app and the DynamoDB table to sign the requests. `在移动应用和DynamoDB表之间建立跨账户访问以签署请求。`

### Company B provides an online image recognition service and utilizes SQS to decouple system components for scalability. The SQS consumers poll the imaging queue as often as possible to keep end-to-end throughput as high as possible. However, Company B is realizing that polling in tight loops is burning CPU cycles and increasing costs with empty responses. How can Company B reduce the number of empty responses?
> B公司提供在线图像识别服务，并利用SQS解耦系统组件以实现可扩展性。SQS消费者尽可能频繁地轮询图像队列，以保持端到端吞吐量尽可能高。然而，B公司意识到紧密循环的轮询正在消耗CPU周期并增加空响应的成本。B公司如何减少空响应的数量？

- [ ] Set the imaging queue visibility Timeout attribute to 20 seconds. `将图像队列的可见性超时属性设置为20秒。`
- [x] Set the Imaging queue ReceiveMessageWaitTimeSeconds attribute to 20 seconds. `将图像队列的ReceiveMessageWaitTimeSeconds属性设置为20秒。`
- [ ] Set the imaging queue MessageRetentionPeriod attribute to 20 seconds. `将图像队列的消息保留期属性设置为20秒。`
- [ ] Set the DelaySeconds parameter of a message to 20 seconds. `将消息的DelaySeconds参数设置为20秒。`

### You have written an application that uses the Elastic Load Balancing service to spread traffic to several web servers. Your users complain that they are sometimes forced to login again in the middle of using your application, after they have already logged in. This is not behavior you have designed. What is a possible solution to prevent this happening?
> 您编写了一个应用程序，使用弹性负载均衡服务将流量分配到多个Web服务器。您的用户抱怨他们在使用应用程序的过程中，有时被迫重新登录，尽管他们已经登录。这不是您设计的行为。有什么可能的解决方案可以防止这种情况发生？

- [ ] Use instance storage to save session state. `使用实例存储保存会话状态。`
- [ ] Use EBS to save session state. `使用EBS保存会话状态。`

### You run an ad-supported photo sharing website using S3 to serve photos to visitors of your site. At some point you find out that other sites have been linking to the photos on your site, causing loss to your business. What is an effective method to mitigate this?
> 您运行一个支持广告的照片分享网站，使用S3向访客提供照片。某个时候，您发现其他网站链接到您网站上的照片，导致您的业务损失。有什么有效的方法可以缓解这种情况？

### A corporate web application is deployed within an Amazon VPC, and is connected to the corporate data center via IPSec VPN. The application must authenticate against the on-premise LDAP server. Once authenticated, logged-in users can only access an S3 keyspace specific to the user. Which two approaches can satisfy the objectives? (Choose TWO)
> 某公司Web应用程序部署在Amazon VPC中，并通过IPSec VPN连接到公司数据中心。该应用程序必须使用本地LDAP服务器进行身份验证。身份验证通过后，已登录用户只能访问特定于用户的S3命名空间。哪两种方法可以满足这一目标？（选择两个）

- [ ] The application authenticates against LDAP. The application then calls the IAM Security Service to login to IAM using the LDAP credentials. The application can use the 1AM temporary credentials to access the appropriate S3 bucket. `应用程序通过LDAP进行身份验证。应用程序然后调用IAM安全服务，使用LDAP凭证登录IAM。应用程序可以使用IAM临时凭证访问相应的S3桶。`
- [x] The application authenticates against LDAP, and retrieves the name of an IAM role associated with the user. The application then calls the IAM Security Token Service to assume that IAM Role. The application can use the temporary credentials to access the appropriate S3 bucket. `应用程序通过LDAP进行身份验证，并检索与用户关联的IAM角色名称。然后应用程序调用IAM安全令牌服务（STS）以假设该IAM角色。应用程序可以使用临时凭证访问相应的S3桶。`
- [ ] The application authenticates against IAM Security Token Service using the LDAP credentials. The application uses those temporary AWS security credentials to access the appropriate S3 bucket. `应用程序使用LDAP凭证对IAM安全令牌服务进行身份验证。应用程序使用这些临时的AWS安全凭证访问相应的S3桶。`
- [x] Develop an identity broker which authenticates against LDAP, and then calls IAM Security Token Service to get IAM federated user credentials. The application calls the identity broker to get IAM federated user credentials with access to the appropriate S3 bucket. `开发一个身份代理，该代理通过LDAP进行身份验证，然后调用IAM安全令牌服务获取IAM联合用户凭证。应用程序调用身份代理以获取具有访问相应S3桶权限的IAM联合用户凭证。`
- [ ] Develop an identity broker which authenticates against IAM Security Token Service to assume an IAM Role to get temporary AWS security credentials. The application calls the identity broker to get AWS temporary security credentials with access to the appropriate S3 bucket. `开发一个身份代理，通过IAM安全令牌服务进行身份验证，以假设IAM角色并获取临时AWS安全凭证。应用程序调用身份代理以获取具有访问相应S3桶权限的AWS临时安全凭证。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### Company C is currently hosting their corporate site in an Amazon S3 bucket with Static Website Hosting enabled. Currently, when visitors go to http://www.companyc.com the index.html page is returned. Company C now would like a new page welcome.html to be returned when a visitor enters http://www.companyc.com in the browser. Which of the following steps will allow Company C to meet this requirement? (Choose TWO)
> 公司C当前在启用了静态网站托管的Amazon S3存储桶中托管其公司网站。目前，当访问者访问http://www.companyc.com时，将返回index.html页面。公司C现在希望当访问者在浏览器中输入http://www.companyc.com时返回一个新的页面welcome.html。以下哪些步骤可以帮助公司C实现此需求？（选择两个）

- [x] Upload an html page named welcome.html to their S3 bucket. `将名为welcome.html的html页面上传到他们的S3存储桶中。`
- [ ] Create a welcome subfolder in their S3 bucket. `在他们的S3存储桶中创建一个welcome子文件夹。`
- [x] Set the Index Document property to welcome.html. `将索引文档属性设置为welcome.html。`
- [ ] Move the index.html page to a welcome subfolder. `将index.html页面移动到welcome子文件夹中。`
- [ ] Set the Error Document property to welcome.html. `将错误文档属性设置为welcome.html。`

### A Development team wants to instrument their code to provide more detailed information to AWS X-Ray than simple outgoing and incoming requests. This will generate large amounts of data, so the Development team wants to implement indexing so they can filter the data. What should the Development team do to achieve this?
> 开发团队希望为代码进行检测，以提供比简单的传出和传入请求更详细的信息给AWS X-Ray。这将生成大量数据，因此开发团队希望实现索引，以便过滤数据。开发团队应该怎么做来实现这一点？

- [ ] Configure the necessary X-Ray environment variables. `配置必要的X-Ray环境变量。`

### A team of Developers must migrate an application running inside an AWS Elastic Beanstalk environment from a Classic Load Balancer to an Application Load Balancer. Which steps should be taken to accomplish the task using the AWS Management Console?
> 开发团队必须将运行在AWS Elastic Beanstalk环境中的应用程序从经典负载均衡器迁移到应用程序负载均衡器。使用AWS管理控制台完成任务应该采取哪些步骤？

- [x] 1. Update the application code in the existing deployment. 2. Select a new load balancer type before running the deployment. 3. Deploy the new version of the application code to the environment. `在现有部署中更新应用程序代码。2. 在运行部署之前选择新的负载均衡器类型。3. 将新的应用程序代码版本部署到环境中。`
- [ ] 1. Create a new environment with the same configurations except for the load balancer type. 2. Deploy the same application version as used in the original environment. 3. Run the swap-environment-cnames action. `创建一个与现有环境配置相同但负载均衡器类型不同的新环境。2. 部署与原环境中相同的应用程序版本。3. 运行交换环境CNAME操作。`
- [ ] 1. Clone the existing environment, changing the associated load balancer type. 2. Deploy the same application version as used in the original environment. 3. Run the swap-environment-cnames action. `克隆现有环境，改变关联的负载均衡器类型。2. 部署与原环境中相同的应用程序版本。3. 运行交换环境CNAME操作。`
- [ ] 1. Edit the environment definitions in the existing deployment. 2. Change the associated load balancer type according to the requirements. 3. Rebuild the environment with the new load balancer type. `编辑现有部署中的环境定义。2. 根据要求更改关联的负载均衡器类型。3. 使用新负载均衡器类型重建环境。`

### A Developer created a new AWS account and must create a scalable AWS Lambda function that meets the following requirements for concurrent execution: Average execution time of 100 seconds 50 requests per second. Which step must be taken prior to deployment to prevent errors?
> 一名开发人员创建了一个新的AWS账户，并必须创建一个可扩展的AWS Lambda函数，以满足以下并发执行要求：平均执行时间为100秒，每秒50个请求。在部署之前必须采取哪个步骤以防止错误？

- [ ] Implement dead-letter queues to capture invocation errors. `实施死信队列以捕获调用错误。`

### A Developer is building a three-tier web application that should be able to handle a minimum of 5000 requests per minute. Requirements state that the web tier should be completely stateless while the application maintains session state for the users. How can session data be externalized, keeping latency at the LOWEST possible value?
> 一名开发人员正在构建一个三层Web应用程序，该应用程序应该能够处理每分钟至少5000个请求。要求表明，Web层应完全无状态，而应用程序应为用户维护会话状态。如何外部化会话数据，同时保持最低的延迟值？

- [x] Create an Amazon RDS instance, then implement session handling at the application level to leverage a database inside the RDS database instance for session data storage. `创建一个Amazon RDS实例，然后在应用程序级别实现会话处理，以利用RDS数据库实例中的数据库进行会话数据存储。`
- [ ] Implement a shared file system solution across the underlying Amazon EC2 instances, then implement session handling at the application level to leverage the shared file system for session data storage. `在底层Amazon EC2实例之间实施共享文件系统解决方案，然后在应用程序级别实现会话处理，以利用共享文件系统进行会话数据存储。`
- [ ] Create an Amazon ElastiCache Memcached cluster, then implement session handling at the application level to leverage the cluster for session data storage. `创建一个Amazon ElastiCache Memcached集群，然后在应用程序级别实现会话处理，以利用该集群进行会话数据存储。`
- [ ] Create an Amazon DynamoDB table, then implement session handling at the application level to leverage the table for session data storage. `创建一个Amazon DynamoDB表，然后在应用程序级别实现会话处理，以利用该表进行会话数据存储。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### An Amazon DynamoDB table uses a Global Secondary Index (GSI) to support read queries. The primary table is write-heavy, whereas the GSI is used for read operations. Looking at Amazon CloudWatch metrics, the Developer notices that write operations to the primary table are throttled frequently under heavy write activity. However, write capacity units to the primary table are available and not fully consumed. Why is the table being throttled?
> 一个Amazon DynamoDB表使用全局二级索引（GSI）来支持读取查询。主表写入负载重，而GSI用于读取操作。通过查看Amazon CloudWatch指标，开发人员注意到在大量写入活动下，主表的写入操作经常被限制。然而，主表的写入容量单位可用且未完全消耗。为什么表被限制？

- [x] The GSI write capacity units are underprovisioned. `GSI的写入容量单位配置不足。`
- [ ] There are not enough read capacity units on the primary table. `主表的读取容量单位不足。`
- [ ] Amazon DynamoDB Streams is not enabled on the table. `未在表上启用Amazon DynamoDB Streams。`
- [ ] A large write operation is being performed against another table. `正在对另一个表执行大写操作。`

### A company runs an e-commerce website that uses Amazon DynamoDB where pricing for items is dynamically updated in real time. At any given time, multiple updates may occur simultaneously for pricing information on a particular product. This is causing the original editor's changes to be overwritten without a proper review process. Which DynamoDB write option should be selected to prevent this overwriting?
> 一家公司运行一个电子商务网站，使用Amazon DynamoDB，商品价格实时动态更新。在任何给定时刻，特定产品的价格信息可能会同时发生多个更新。这导致原始编辑的更改在没有适当审核流程的情况下被覆盖。为了防止这种覆盖，应选择哪个DynamoDB写入选项？

- [ ] Concurrent writes. `并发写入。`
- [x] Conditional writes. `条件写入。`
- [ ] Atomic writes. `原子写入。`
- [ ] Batch writes. `批量写入。`

### A Developer has been asked to create an AWS Lambda function that is triggered any time updates are made to items in an Amazon DynamoDB table. The function has been created, and appropriate permissions have been added to the Lambda execution role. Amazon DynamoDB streams have been enabled for the table, but the function is still not being triggered. Which option would enable DynamoDB table updates to trigger the Lambda function?
> 开发者被要求创建一个AWS Lambda函数，该函数在对Amazon DynamoDB表中的项目进行更新时触发。函数已创建，并且已将适当的权限添加到Lambda执行角色中。已为该表启用Amazon DynamoDB流，但该函数仍未被触发。哪个选项将使DynamoDB表更新触发Lambda函数？

- [ ] Change the StreamViewType parameter value to NEW_AND_OLD_IMAGES for the DynamoDB table. `将DynamoDB表的StreamViewType参数值更改为NEW_AND_OLD_IMAGES。`
- [x] Configure event source mapping for the Lambda function. `为Lambda函数配置事件源映射。`
- [ ] Map an Amazon SNS topic to the DynamoDB streams. `将Amazon SNS主题映射到DynamoDB流。`
- [ ] Increase the maximum execution time (timeout) setting of the Lambda function. `增加Lambda函数的最大执行时间（超时）设置。`

### A company is running a Docker application on Amazon ECS. The application must scale based on user load in the last 15 seconds. How should a Developer instrument the code so that the requirement can be met?

- [ ] Create a standard-resolution custom Amazon CloudWatch metric for user activity data, then publish data every 5 seconds. `创建一个标准分辨率的自定义Amazon CloudWatch指标，用于用户活动数据，然后每5秒发布数据。`

### A company needs to ingest terabytes of data each hour from thousands of sources that are delivered almost continually throughout the day. Which approach will meet these requirements?

- [ ] Use AWS Data Pipeline to automate the movement and transformation of data. `使用AWS Data Pipeline自动化数据的移动和转换。`
- [x] Use Amazon Kinesis Data Streams with Kinesis Client Library to ingest and deliver messages. `使用Amazon Kinesis数据流和Kinesis客户端库来摄取和交付消息。`

### A Developer is working on an application that handles 10MB documents that contain highly-sensitive data. The application will use AWS KMS to perform clientside encryption. What steps must be followed?
> 开发人员正在开发一个处理包含高度敏感数据的10MB文档的应用程序。该应用程序将使用AWS KMS执行客户端加密。必须遵循哪些步骤？

- [ ] Invoke the Encrypt API passing the plaintext data that must be encrypted, then reference the customer managed key ARN in the KeyId parameter. `调用Encrypt API，传入必须加密的明文数据，然后在KeyId参数中引用客户管理的密钥ARN。`
- [ ] Invoke the GenerateRandom API to get a data encryption key, then use the data encryption key to encrypt the data. `调用GenerateRandom API以获取数据加密密钥，然后使用该密钥加密数据。`
- [ ] Invoke the GenerateDataKey API to retrieve the encrypted version of the data encryption key to encrypt the data. `调用GenerateDataKey API以检索数据加密密钥的加密版本来加密数据。`
- [x] Invoke the GenerateDataKey API to retrieve the plaintext version of the data encryption key to encrypt the data. `调用GenerateDataKey API以检索数据加密密钥的明文版本来加密数据。`

### An application writes items to an Amazon DynamoDB table. As the application scales to thousands of instances, calls to the DynamoDB API generate occasional ThrottlingException errors. The application is coded in a language incompatible with the AWS SDK. How should the error be handled?

### An e-commerce web application that shares session state on-premises is being migrated to AWS. The application must be fault tolerant, natively highly scalable, and any service interruption should not affect the user experience. What is the best option to store the session state?
> 一个共享会话状态的本地电子商务Web应用程序正在迁移到AWS。该应用程序必须具备容错能力，原生高度可扩展，且任何服务中断都不应影响用户体验。存储会话状态的最佳选项是什么？

### A Developer has a stateful web server on-premises that is being migrated to AWS. The Developer must have greater elasticity in the new design. How should the Developer re-factor the application to make it more elastic? (Choose TWO)
> 一名开发人员有一个有状态的本地Web服务器，正在迁移到AWS。开发人员在新设计中必须有更大的弹性。开发人员应该如何重构应用程序以使其更具弹性？（选择两个）

- [ ] Use pessimistic concurrency on Amazon DynamoDB. `在Amazon DynamoDB上使用悲观并发控制。`
- [ ] Use Amazon CloudFront with an Auto Scaling group. `将Amazon CloudFront与自动扩展组结合使用。`
- [ ] Use Amazon CloudFront with an AWS Web Application Firewall. `将Amazon CloudFront与AWS Web应用防火墙结合使用。`
- [x] Store session state data in an Amazon DynamoDB table. `将会话状态数据存储在Amazon DynamoDB表中。`
- [x] Use an ELB with an Auto Scaling group. `使用一个负载均衡器（ELB）与自动扩展组结合使用。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Developer must analyze performance issues with production-distributed applications written as AWS Lambda functions. These distributed Lambda applications invoke other components that make up the applications. How should the Developer identify and troubleshoot the root cause of the performance issues in production?
> 开发人员必须分析用AWS Lambda函数编写的生产分布式应用程序的性能问题。这些分布式Lambda应用程序调用组成应用程序的其他组件。开发人员应如何识别并排除生产中的性能问题的根本原因？

- [ ] Add logging statements to the Lambda functions, then use Amazon CloudWatch to view the logs. `向Lambda函数中添加日志语句，然后使用Amazon CloudWatch查看日志。`
- [ ] Use AWS Cloud Trail and then examine the logs. `使用AWS CloudTrail，然后检查日志。`
- [x] Use AWS X-Ray, then examine the segments and errors. `使用AWS X-Ray，然后检查段和错误。`
- [ ] Run Amazon Inspector agents and then analyze performance. `运行Amazon Inspector代理程序，然后分析性能。`

### A Developer wants to debug an application by searching and filtering log data. The application logs are stored in Amazon CloudWatch Logs. The Developer creates a new metric filter to count exceptions in the application logs. However, no results are returned from the logs. What is the reason that no filtered results are being returned?
> 开发人员希望通过搜索和过滤日志数据来调试应用程序。应用程序日志存储在Amazon CloudWatch Logs中。开发人员创建了一个新的指标过滤器来计算应用程序日志中的异常。然而，日志没有返回任何结果。导致没有返回过滤结果的原因是什么？

- [ ] A setup of the Amazon CloudWatch interface VPC endpoint is required for filtering the CloudWatch Logs in the VPC. `需要设置Amazon CloudWatch接口VPC端点，以过滤VPC中的CloudWatch日志。`
- [x] CloudWatch Logs only publishes metric data for events that happen after the filter is created. `CloudWatch Logs只会发布过滤器创建后发生的事件的指标数据。`
- [ ] The log group for CloudWatch Logs should be first streamed to Amazon Elasticsearch Service before metric filtering returns the results. `CloudWatch Logs的日志组应首先流式传输到Amazon Elasticsearch Service，才能通过指标过滤返回结果。`
- [ ] Metric data points for logs groups can be filtered only after they are exported to an Amazon S3 bucket. `日志组的指标数据点只能在导出到Amazon S3存储桶后进行过滤。`

### A Developer is investigating an issue whereby certain requests are passing through an Amazon API Gateway endpoint /MyAPI, but the requests do not reach the AWS Lambda function backing /MyAPI. The Developer found that a second Lambda function sometimes runs at maximum concurrency allowed for the given AWS account. How can the Developer address this issue?
> 一位开发人员正在调查某些请求通过Amazon API Gateway端点/MyAPI，但这些请求未到达支持/MyAPI的AWS Lambda函数的问题。开发人员发现，第二个Lambda函数有时会达到该AWS账户允许的最大并发限制。开发人员如何解决这个问题？

- [ ] Manually reduce the concurrent execution limit at the account level. `手动减少账户级别的并发执行限制。`
- [ ] Add another API Gateway stage for /MyAPI, and shard the requests. `为/MyAPI添加另一个API Gateway阶段，并对请求进行分片。`
- [x] Configure the second Lambda function's concurrency execution limit. `配置第二个Lambda函数的并发执行限制。`
- [ ] Reduce the throttling limits in the API Gateway /MyAPI endpoint. `减少API Gateway /MyAPI端点的限流限制。`

### A company is migrating a single-server, on-premises web application to AWS. The company intends to use multiple servers behind an Elastic Load Balancer (ELB) to balance the load, and will also store session data in memory on the web server. The company does not want to lose that session data if a server fails or goes offline, and it wants to minimize user's downtime. Where should the company move session data to MOST effectively reduce downtime and make users' session data more fault tolerant?
> 一家公司正在将单服务器的本地Web应用程序迁移到AWS。公司计划使用多个服务器，并在它们后面部署弹性负载均衡器（ELB）来平衡负载，还会将会话数据存储在Web服务器的内存中。公司不希望在服务器故障或离线时丢失会话数据，并希望最大限度地减少用户的停机时间。公司应将会话数据迁移到哪里，才能最有效地减少停机时间并使用户的会话数据更加容错？

- [x] An Amazon ElastiCache for Redis cluster. `Amazon ElastiCache for Redis 集群。`
- [ ] A second Amazon EBS volume. `第二个Amazon EBS卷。`
- [ ] The web server's primary disk. `Web服务器的主磁盘。`
- [ ] An Amazon EC2 instance dedicated to session data. `专用于会话数据的Amazon EC2实例。`

### An e-commerce site allows returning users to log in to display customized web pages. The workflow is shown in the image below. An application is running on EC2 instances. ![Question 299](images/question299.jpeg)

- [ ] Batch login requests from hundreds of users together as a single read request to the database. `将数百个用户的登录请求批处理为对数据库的单个读取请求。`

### A company maintains a REST service using Amazon API Gateway and the API Gateway native API key validation. The company recently launched a new registration page, which allows users to sign up for the service. The registration page creates a new API key using CreateApiKey and sends the new key to the user. When the user attempts to call the API using this key, the user receives a 403 Forbidden error. Existing users are unaffected and can still call the API. What code updates will grant these new users access to the API?
> 一家公司使用 Amazon API Gateway 维护 REST 服务，并使用 API Gateway 原生 API 密钥验证。该公司最近推出了一个新的注册页面，允许用户注册该服务。注册页面使用 CreateApiKey 创建新的 API 密钥并将新密钥发送给用户。当用户尝试使用此密钥调用 API 时，收到 403 Forbidden 错误。现有用户不受影响，仍然可以调用 API。什么代码更新将授予这些新用户访问 API 的权限？

- [ ] The createDeployment method must be called so the API can be redeployed to include the newly created API key. `必须调用 createDeployment 方法，以便 API 可以重新部署以包含新创建的 API 密钥。`
- [ ] The updateAuthorizer method must be called to update the API's authorizer to include the newly created API key. `必须调用 updateAuthorizer 方法以更新 API 的授权器以包含新创建的 API 密钥。`
- [ ] The importApiKeys method must be called to import all newly created API keys into the current stage of the API. `必须调用 importApiKeys 方法将所有新创建的 API 密钥导入 API 的当前阶段。`
- [x] The createUsagePlanKey method must be called to associate the newly created API key with the correct usage plan. `必须调用 createUsagePlanKey 方法将新创建的 API 密钥与正确的使用计划关联。`

### A Developer is writing a mobile application that allows users to view images from an S3 bucket. The users must be able to log in with their Amazon login, as well as Facebook and/or Google accounts. How can the Developer provide this authentication functionality?

- [ ] Use AWS STS AssumeRole in the application code and assume a role with Get* permissions on the S3 bucket. `在应用程序代码中使用 AWS STS AssumeRole，并假设一个具有 S3 存储桶上 Get* 权限的角色。`

### A Developer wants access to make the log data of an application running on an EC2 instance available to systems administrators. Which of the following enables monitoring of this metric in Amazon CloudWatch?

### A nightly batch job loads 1 million new records into a DynamoDB table. The records are only needed for one hour, and the table needs to be empty by the next night's batch job. Which is the MOST efficient and cost-effective method to provide an empty table?
> 每晚的批处理作业将 100 万条新记录加载到 DynamoDB 表中。这些记录仅在一小时内需要，并且表格需要在下一晚的批处理作业之前清空。提供一个空表的最有效且具有成本效益的方法是什么？

- [x] Use DeleteItem using a ConditionExpression. `使用 DeleteItem 和 ConditionExpression。`
- [ ] Use BatchWriteItem to empty all of the rows. `使用 BatchWriteItem 清空所有行。`
- [ ] Write a recursive function that scans and calls out DeleteItem. `编写一个递归函数，扫描并调用 DeleteItem。`
- [ ] Create and then delete the table after the task has completed. `创建表并在任务完成后删除。`

### A company has an application that logs all information to Amazon S3. Whenever there is a new log file, an AWS Lambda function is invoked to process the log files. The code works, gathering all of the necessary information. However, when checking the Lambda function logs, duplicate entries with the same request ID are found. What is causing the duplicate entries?
> 一家公司有一个应用程序，将所有信息记录到 Amazon S3 中。每当有新的日志文件时，就会调用 AWS Lambda 函数来处理这些日志文件。代码正常工作，收集了所有必要的信息。然而，在检查 Lambda 函数日志时，发现具有相同请求 ID 的重复条目。造成重复条目的原因是什么？

- [ ] The S3 bucket name was specified incorrectly. `S3 存储桶名称指定不正确。`
- [x] The Lambda function failed, and the Lambda service retried the invocation with a delay. `Lambda 函数失败，Lambda 服务延迟重试了调用。`
- [ ] There was an S3 outage, which caused duplicate entries of the sale log file. `发生了 S3 中断，导致销售日志文件的重复条目。`
- [ ] The application stopped intermittently and then resumed. `应用程序间歇性停止，然后恢复。`

### A Development team has pushed out 10 applications running on several Amazon EC2 instances. ### A company uses Amazon DynamoDB for managing and tracking orders. The DynamoDB table is partitioned based on the order date. The company receives a huge increase in orders during a sales event, causing DynamoDB writes to throttle, and the consumed throughput is far below the provisioned throughput. According to AWS best practices, how can this issue be resolved with MINIMAL costs?
> 一家公司使用 Amazon DynamoDB 来管理和跟踪订单。DynamoDB 表根据订单日期进行分区。在促销活动期间，公司收到大量订单，导致 DynamoDB 写入速率被限制，且消耗的吞吐量远低于预配置的吞吐量。根据 AWS 最佳实践，如何以最低成本解决此问题？

- [ ] Create a new DynamoDB table for every order date. `为每个订单日期创建一个新的 DynamoDB 表。`
- [x] Increase the read and write capacity units of the DynamoDB table. `增加 DynamoDB 表的读写容量单位。`
- [ ] Add a random number suffix to the partition key values. `在分区键值中添加随机数字后缀。`
- [ ] Add a global secondary index to the DynamoDB table. `为 DynamoDB 表添加全局二级索引。`

### In a multi-container Docker environment in AWS Elastic Beanstalk, what is required to configure container instances in the environment?
> 在 AWS Elastic Beanstalk 的多容器 Docker 环境中，配置环境中的容器实例需要什么？

- [x] An Amazon ECS task definition. `一个 Amazon ECS 任务定义。`
- [ ] An Amazon ECS cluster. `一个 Amazon ECS 集群。`
- [ ] A Dockerfile in an application package. `应用程序包中的 Dockerfile。`
- [ ] A CLI for Elastic Beanstalk. `Elastic Beanstalk 的命令行接口。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### An application that runs on an Amazon EC2 instance needs to access and make API calls to multiple AWS services. What is the MOST secure way to provide access to the AWS services with MINIMAL management overhead?
> 在 Amazon EC2 实例上运行的应用程序需要访问并调用多个 AWS 服务的 API。提供访问 AWS 服务的最安全方式是什么，且管理开销最小？

- [ ] Use AWS KMS to store and retrieve credentials. `使用 AWS KMS 存储和检索凭证。`
- [x] Use EC2 instance profiles. `使用 EC2 实例配置文件。`
- [ ] Use AWS root user to make requests to the application. `使用 AWS 根用户向应用程序发出请求。`
- [ ] Store and retrieve credentials from AWS CodeCommit. `从 AWS CodeCommit 存储和检索凭证。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A company maintains an application responsible for processing several thousand external callbacks each day. The company's System administrators want to know how many callbacks are being received on a rolling basis, and they want this data available for 10 days. The company also wants the ability to issue automated alerts if the number of callbacks exceeds the defined thresholds. What is the MOST cost-effective way to address the need to track and alert on these statistics?
> 一家公司维护一个应用程序，负责处理每天数千个外部回调。公司的系统管理员想知道在滚动基础上接收到多少个回调，并希望这些数据可用 10 天。公司还希望能够在回调数量超过定义的阈值时发出自动警报。解决跟踪和提醒这些统计数据需求的最具成本效益的方法是什么？

- [ ] Push callback data to an Amazon RDS database that can be queried to show historical data and to alert on exceeded thresholds. `将回调数据推送到 Amazon RDS 数据库，以便查询显示历史数据并对超过阈值发出警报。`
- [ ] Push callback data to AWS X-Ray and use AWS Lambda to query, display, and alert on exceeded thresholds. `将回调数据推送到 AWS X-Ray，并使用 AWS Lambda 查询、显示并对超过阈值发出警报。`
- [ ] Push callback data to Amazon Kinesis Data Streams and invoke an AWS Lambda function that stores data in Amazon DynamoDB and sends the required alerts. `将回调数据推送到 Amazon Kinesis 数据流，并调用一个 AWS Lambda 函数，将数据存储在 Amazon DynamoDB 中并发送所需的警报。`
- [x] Push callback data to Amazon CloudWatch as a custom metric and use the CloudWatch alerting mechanisms to alert System Administrators. `将回调数据作为自定义指标推送到 Amazon CloudWatch，并使用 CloudWatch 警报机制通知系统管理员。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A company has a website that is developed in PHP and WordPress and is launched using AWS Elastic Beanstalk. There is a new version of the website that needs to be deployed in the Elastic Beanstalk environment. The company cannot tolerate having the website offline if an update fails. Deployments must have minimal impact and rollback as soon as possible. What deployment method should be used?
> 一家公司有一个使用 PHP 和 WordPress 开发的网站，并通过 AWS Elastic Beanstalk 启动。需要在 Elastic Beanstalk 环境中部署网站的新版本。如果更新失败，公司无法容忍网站离线。部署必须对业务影响最小，并尽快回滚。应使用哪种部署方法？

- [ ] All at once. `一次性全部更新。`
- [ ] Rolling. `滚动更新。`
- [ ] Snapshots. `快照。`
- [x] Immutable. `不可变更新。`

### A company has a multi-tiered web application on AWS. During a recent spike in traffic, one of the primary relational databases on Amazon RDS could not serve all the traffic. Some read queries for repeatedly accessed items failed, so users received error messages. What can be done to minimize the impact on database read queries MOST efficiently during future traffic spikes?
> 一家公司在 AWS 上拥有一个多层 Web 应用程序。在最近的流量激增期间，Amazon RDS 上的一个主要关系数据库无法处理所有流量。一些重复访问项目的读取查询失败，用户收到了错误消息。在未来的流量激增期间，如何最有效地减少对数据库读取查询的影响？

- [ ] Use Amazon S3 to cache database query results. `使用 Amazon S3 缓存数据库查询结果。`
- [ ] Use Amazon RDS as a custom origin for Amazon CloudFront. `将 Amazon RDS 用作 Amazon CloudFront 的自定义源。`
- [ ] Use local storage and memory on Amazon EC2 instances to cache data. `在 Amazon EC2 实例上使用本地存储和内存缓存数据。`
- [x] Use Amazon ElastiCache in front of the primary database to cache data. `在主数据库前使用 Amazon ElastiCache 缓存数据。`

### A Developer must build an application that uses Amazon DynamoDB. The requirements state that the items being stored in the DynamoDB table will be 7KB in size and that reads must be strongly consistent. The maximum read rate is 3 items per second, and the maximum write rate is 10 items per second. How should the Developer size the DynamoDB table to meet these requirements?
> 开发人员必须构建一个使用 Amazon DynamoDB 的应用程序。要求是存储在 DynamoDB 表中的项目大小为 7KB，并且读取必须是强一致性的。最大读取速率为每秒 3 个项目，最大写入速率为每秒 10 个项目。开发人员应该如何调整 DynamoDB 表的大小以满足这些要求？

- [ ] Read: 3 read capacity unitsWrite: 70 write capacity units. `读取：3 读取容量单位，写入：70 写入容量单位。`
- [x] Read: 6 read capacity unitsWrite: 70 write capacity units. `读取：6 读取容量单位，写入：70 写入容量单位。`
- [ ] Read: 6 read capacity unitsWrite: 10 write capacity units. `读取：6 读取容量单位，写入：10 写入容量单位。`
- [ ] Read: 3 read capacity unitsWrite: 10 write capacity units. `读取：3 读取容量单位，写入：10 写入容量单位。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Developer is creating an AWS Lambda function to process a stream of data from an Amazon Kinesis Data Stream. When the Lambda function parses the data and encounters a missing field, it exits the function with an error. The function is generating duplicate records from the Kinesis stream. When the Developer looks at the stream output without the Lambda function, there are no duplicate records. What is the reason for the duplicates?
> 开发人员正在创建一个 AWS Lambda 函数，以处理来自 Amazon Kinesis 数据流的数据流。当 Lambda 函数解析数据并遇到缺失字段时，它以错误退出该函数。该函数从 Kinesis 流中生成重复记录。当开发人员查看没有 Lambda 函数的流输出时，没有重复记录。导致重复记录的原因是什么？

- [x] The Lambda function did not advance the Kinesis stream pointer to the next record after the error. `Lambda 函数在出错后未将 Kinesis 流指针移动到下一个记录。`
- [ ] The Lambda event source used asynchronous invocation, resulting in duplicate records. `Lambda 事件源使用异步调用，导致重复记录。`
- [ ] The Lambda function did not handle the error, and the Lambda service attempted to reprocess the data. `Lambda 函数未处理错误，Lambda 服务试图重新处理数据。`
- [ ] The Lambda function is not keeping up with the amount of data coming from the stream. `Lambda 函数无法跟上来自流的数据量。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A company is developing an application that will run on several Amazon EC2 instances in an Auto Scaling group and can access a database running on Amazon EC2. The application needs to store secrets required to connect to the database. The application must allow for periodic secret rotation, and there should be no changes to the application when a secret changes. What is the SAFEST way to meet these requirements?
> 一家公司正在开发一个将在自动扩展组中的多个 Amazon EC2 实例上运行的应用程序，并且可以访问在 Amazon EC2 上运行的数据库。该应用程序需要存储连接数据库所需的秘密。应用程序必须允许定期更换秘密，并且在秘密更改时不应对应用程序进行更改。满足这些要求的最安全方法是什么？

- [ ] Associate an IAM role to the EC2 instance where the application is running with permission to access the database. `将 IAM 角色关联到运行应用程序的 EC2 实例，允许其访问数据库。`
- [x] Use AWS Systems Manager Parameter Store with the SecureString data type to store secrets. `使用 AWS Systems Manager Parameter Store 和 SecureString 数据类型来存储秘密。`
- [ ] Configure the application to store secrets in Amazon S3 object metadata. `配置应用程序将秘密存储在 Amazon S3 对象元数据中。`
- [ ] Hard code the database secrets in the application code itself. `在应用程序代码中硬编码数据库秘密。`

### A Developer writes an AWS Lambda function and uploads the code in a .ZIP file to Amazon S3. The Developer makes changes to the code and uploads a new .ZIP file to Amazon S3. However, Lambda executes the earlier code. How can the Developer fix this in the LEAST disruptive way?
> 开发人员编写了一个 AWS Lambda 函数，并将代码以 .ZIP 文件上传到 Amazon S3。开发人员对代码进行了更改，并将新的 .ZIP 文件上传到 Amazon S3。然而，Lambda 执行的是早期的代码。开发人员如何以最小的干扰修复此问题？

- [ ] Create another Lambda function and specify the new .ZIP file. `创建另一个 Lambda 函数并指定新的 .ZIP 文件。`
- [x] Call the update-function-code API. `调用 update-function-code API。`
- [ ] Remove the earlier .ZIP file first, then add the new .ZIP file. `先删除早期的 .ZIP 文件，然后添加新的 .ZIP 文件。`
- [ ] Call the create-alias API. `调用 create-alias API。`

### An AWS Lambda function must read data from an Amazon RDS MySQL database in a VPC and also reach a public endpoint over the internet to get additional data. Which steps must be taken to allow the function to access both the RDS resource and the public endpoint? (Select TWO)
> 一个 AWS Lambda 函数必须从 VPC 中的 Amazon RDS MySQL 数据库读取数据，并且还需要通过互联网访问公共端点以获取额外的数据。必须采取哪些步骤以允许该函数同时访问 RDS 资源和公共端点？（选择两个）

- [x] Modify the default configuration for the Lambda function to associate it with an Amazon VPC private subnet. `修改 Lambda 函数的默认配置，以将其与 Amazon VPC 私有子网关联。`
- [ ] Modify the default network access control list to allow outbound traffic. `修改默认网络访问控制列表以允许出站流量。`
- [x] Add a NAT Gateway to the VPC. `向 VPC 添加 NAT 网关。`
- [ ] Modify the default configuration of the Lambda function to associate it with a VPC public subnet. `修改 Lambda 函数的默认配置，以将其与 VPC 公共子网关联。`
- [ ] Add an environmental variable to the Lambda function to allow outbound internet access. `向 Lambda 函数添加环境变量以允许出站互联网访问。`

### A Developer has been asked to make changes to the source code of an AWS Lambda function. The function is managed using an AWS CloudFormation template. The template is configured to load the source code from an Amazon S3 bucket. The Developer manually created a .ZIP file deployment package containing the changes and put the file into the correct location on Amazon S3. When the function is invoked, the code changes have not been applied. What step is required to update the function with the changes?
> 开发人员被要求对 AWS Lambda 函数的源代码进行更改。该函数是使用 AWS CloudFormation 模板管理的。模板配置为从 Amazon S3 存储桶加载源代码。开发人员手动创建了一个包含更改的 .ZIP 文件部署包，并将文件放入 Amazon S3 的正确位置。当函数被调用时，代码更改没有被应用。要更新函数以应用这些更改，需要执行什么步骤？

- [ ] Delete the .ZIP file on S3, and re-upload by using a different object key name. `删除 S3 上的 .ZIP 文件，并使用不同的对象键名称重新上传。`
- [x] Update the CloudFormation stack with the correct values for the function code properties S3Bucket, S3Key, or S3ObjectVersion. `使用函数代码属性 S3Bucket、S3Key 或 S3ObjectVersion 的正确值更新 CloudFormation 堆栈。`
- [ ] Ensure that the function source code is base64-encoded before uploading the deployment package to S3. `确保在将部署包上传到 S3 之前，函数源代码被进行 base64 编码。`
- [ ] Modify the execution role of the Lambda function to allow S3 access permission to the deployment package .ZIP file. `修改 Lambda 函数的执行角色，以允许对部署包 .ZIP 文件的 S3 访问权限。`

### A Developer wants to enable AWS X-Ray for a secure application that runs in an Amazon ECS environment. What combination of steps will enable X-Ray? (Select THREE)
> 开发人员希望为在 Amazon ECS 环境中运行的安全应用程序启用 AWS X-Ray。哪三步组合将启用 X-Ray？（选择三项）

- [ ] Register the application with X-Ray. `将应用程序注册到 X-Ray。`
- [ ] Configure and use an IAM role for tasks. `配置并使用任务的 IAM 角色。`

### A Developer is designing a new application that uses Amazon S3. To satisfy compliance requirements, the Developer must encrypt the data at rest. How can the Developer accomplish this?
> 开发人员正在设计一个使用 Amazon S3 的新应用程序。为了满足合规要求，开发人员必须加密静态数据。开发人员可以如何实现这一目标？

- [ ] Use s3:x-amz-acl as a condition in the S3 bucket policy. `在 S3 存储桶策略中使用 s3:x-amz-acl 作为条件。`
- [ ] Use Amazon RDS with default encryption. `使用具有默认加密的 Amazon RDS。`
- [ ] Use aws:SecureTransport as a condition in the S3 bucket policy. `在 S3 存储桶策略中使用 aws:SecureTransport 作为条件。`
- [x] Turn on S3 default encryption for the S3 bucket. `为 S3 存储桶启用 S3 默认加密。`

### A Developer wants to find a list of items in a global secondary index from an Amazon DynamoDB table. Which DynamoDB API call can the Developer use in order to consume the LEAST number of read capacity units?
> 开发人员想要从 Amazon DynamoDB 表的全局二级索引中查找一组项目。开发人员可以使用哪个 DynamoDB API 调用来消耗最少的读取容量单位？

- [ ] Scan operation using eventually-consistent reads. `使用最终一致性读取的扫描操作。`
- [ ] Query operation using strongly-consistent reads. `使用强一致性读取的查询操作。`
- [x] Query operation using eventually-consistent reads. `使用最终一致性读取的查询操作。`
- [ ] Scan operation using strongly-consistent reads. `使用强一致性读取的扫描操作。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Developer has published an update to an application that is served to a global user base using Amazon CloudFront. After deploying the application, users are not able to see the updated changes. How can the Developer resolve this issue?
> 开发人员已经发布了一个更新的应用程序，该应用程序通过 Amazon CloudFront 服务于全球用户。部署应用程序后，用户无法看到更新的更改。开发人员如何解决这个问题？

- [ ] Remove the origin from the CloudFront configuration and add it again. `从 CloudFront 配置中移除源并重新添加。`
- [ ] Disable forwarding of query strings and request headers from the CloudFront distribution configuration. `在 CloudFront 分发配置中禁用查询字符串和请求头的转发。`
- [x] Invalidate all the application objects from the edge caches. `使所有应用程序对象在边缘缓存中失效。`
- [ ] Disable the CloudFront distribution and enable it again to update all the edge locations. `禁用 CloudFront 分发，然后重新启用以更新所有边缘位置。`

### A Developer must deploy a new AWS Lambda function using an AWS CloudFormation template. Which procedures will deploy a Lambda function? (Select TWO)
> 开发人员必须使用 AWS CloudFormation 模板部署一个新的 AWS Lambda 函数。哪些程序将部署 Lambda 函数？（选择两个）

- [x] Upload the code to an AWS CodeCommit repository, then add a reference to it in an AWS::Lambda::Function resource in the template. `将代码上传到 AWS CodeCommit 存储库，然后在模板中的 AWS::Lambda::Function 资源中添加对它的引用。`
- [x] Create an AWS::Lambda::Function resource in the template, then write the code directly inside the CloudFormation template. `在模板中创建一个 AWS::Lambda::Function 资源，然后直接在 CloudFormation 模板中编写代码。`
- [ ] Upload a .ZIP file containing the function code to Amazon S3, then add a reference to it in an AWS::Lambda::Function resource in the template. `将包含函数代码的 .ZIP 文件上传到 Amazon S3，然后在模板中的 AWS::Lambda::Function 资源中添加对它的引用。`
- [ ] Upload a .ZIP file to AWS CloudFormation containing the function code, then add a reference to it in an AWS::Lambda::Function resource in the template. `将包含函数代码的 .ZIP 文件上传到 AWS CloudFormation，然后在模板中的 AWS::Lambda::Function 资源中添加对它的引用。`
- [ ] Upload the function code to a private Git repository, then add a reference to it in an AWS::Lambda::Function resource in the template. `将函数代码上传到私有 Git 存储库，然后在模板中的 AWS::Lambda::Function 资源中添加对它的引用。`

### How should custom libraries be utilized in AWS Lambda?

- [ ] Host the library on Amazon S3 and reference to it from the Lambda function. `将库托管在 Amazon S3 上，并从 Lambda 函数引用它。`
- [x] Install the library locally and upload a ZIP file of the Lambda function. `在本地安装库并上传包含 Lambda 函数的 ZIP 文件。`
- [ ] Import the necessary Lambda blueprint when creating the function. `在创建函数时导入必要的 Lambda 蓝图。`
- [ ] Modify the function runtime to include the necessary library. `修改函数运行时以包含必要的库。`

### A company needs to secure its existing website running behind an Elastic Load Balancer. The website's Amazon EC2 instances are CPU-constrained. What should be done to secure the website while not increasing the CPU load on the EC2 web servers? (Select TWO)
> 一家公司需要保护其在弹性负载均衡器后运行的现有网站。该网站的 Amazon EC2 实例受限于 CPU。为了在不增加 EC2 Web 服务器 CPU 负载的情况下保护网站，应采取哪些措施？（选择两个）

- [ ] Configure an Elastic Load Balancer with SSL pass-through. `配置具有 SSL 直通的弹性负载均衡器。`
- [x] Configure SSL certificates on an Elastic Load Balancer. `在弹性负载均衡器上配置 SSL 证书。`
- [ ] Configure an Elastic Load Balancer with a Loadable Storage System. `配置具有可加载存储系统的弹性负载均衡器。`
- [ ] Install SSL certificates on the EC2 instances. `在 EC2 实例上安装 SSL 证书。`
- [x] Configure an Elastic Load Balancer with SSL termination. `配置具有 SSL 终止的弹性负载均衡器。`

### A Developer is writing an imaging micro service on AWS Lambda. The service is dependent on several libraries that are not available in the Lambda runtime environment. Which strategy should the Developer follow to create the Lambda deployment package?
> 开发人员正在 AWS Lambda 上编写一个图像微服务。该服务依赖于一些在 Lambda 运行时环境中不可用的库。开发人员应遵循哪种策略来创建 Lambda 部署包？

- [x] Create a ZIP file with the source code and all dependent libraries. `创建一个包含源代码和所有依赖库的 ZIP 文件。`
- [ ] Create a ZIP file with the source code and a script that installs the dependent libraries at runtime. `创建一个包含源代码和一个在运行时安装依赖库的脚本的 ZIP 文件。`
- [ ] Create a ZIP file with the source code. Stage the dependent libraries on an Amazon S3 bucket indicated by the Lambda environment variable LD_LIBRARY_PATH. `创建一个仅包含源代码的 ZIP 文件。将依赖库放置在 Lambda 环境变量 LD_LIBRARY_PATH 指定的 Amazon S3 存储桶中。`
- [ ] Create a ZIP file with the source code and a buildspec.yaml file that installs the dependent libraries on AWS Lambda. `创建一个包含源代码和 buildspec.yaml 文件的 ZIP 文件，该文件在 AWS Lambda 上安装依赖库。`

### A Developer is designing a fault-tolerant environment where client sessions will be saved. How can the Developer ensure that no sessions are lost if an Amazon EC2 instance fails?
> 开发人员正在设计一个容错环境，以保存客户端会话。开发人员如何确保如果 Amazon EC2 实例失败，则不会丢失任何会话？

- [ ] Use sticky sessions with an Elastic Load Balancer target group. `使用 Elastic Load Balancer 目标组的粘性会话。`
- [ ] Use Amazon SQS to save session data. `使用 Amazon SQS 保存会话数据。`
- [x] Use Amazon DynamoDB to perform scalable session handling. `使用 Amazon DynamoDB 进行可扩展的会话处理。`
- [ ] Use Elastic Load Balancer connection draining to stop sending requests to failing instances. `使用 Elastic Load Balancer 连接排空来停止向故障实例发送请求。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### In a move toward using microservices, a company's Management team has asked all Development teams to build their services so that API requests depend only on that service's data store. One team is building a Payments service which has its own database; the service needs data that originates in the Accounts database. Both are using Amazon DynamoDB. What approach will result in the simplest, decoupled, and reliable method to get near-real time updates from the Accounts database?
> 为了向微服务转型，公司的管理团队要求所有开发团队构建他们的服务，使得 API 请求仅依赖于该服务的数据存储。一组正在构建一个拥有自己数据库的支付服务；该服务需要来自账户数据库的数据。两者都使用 Amazon DynamoDB。哪种方法将导致最简单、最解耦且可靠的方式来获取来自账户数据库的近实时更新？

- [ ] Use Amazon Glue to perform frequent ETL updates from the Accounts database to the Payments database. `使用 Amazon Glue 进行频繁的 ETL 更新，将账户数据库的数据更新到支付数据库。`
- [ ] Use Amazon ElastiCache in Payments, with the cache updated by triggers in the Accounts database. `在支付服务中使用 Amazon ElastiCache，通过账户数据库中的触发器更新缓存。`
- [ ] Use Amazon Kinesis Data Firehouse to deliver all changes from the Accounts database to the Payments database. `使用 Amazon Kinesis Data Firehouse 将所有更改从账户数据库传递到支付数据库。`
- [x] Use Amazon DynamoDB Streams to deliver all changes from the Accounts database to the Payments database. `使用 Amazon DynamoDB Streams 将所有更改从账户数据库传递到支付数据库。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A company needs a fully-managed source control service that will work in AWS. The service must ensure that revision control synchronizes multiple distributed repositories by exchanging sets of changes peer-to-peer. All users need to work productively even when not connected to a network. Which source control service should be used?
> 一家公司需要一个完全托管的源代码控制服务，该服务能够在 AWS 中工作。该服务必须确保修订控制通过点对点交换变更集来同步多个分布式代码库。所有用户即使在离线状态下也需要能够高效工作。应该使用哪个源代码控制服务？

- [ ] Subversion.

### A Developer is writing a serverless application that requires that an AWS Lambda function be invoked every 10 minutes. What is an automated and serverless way to trigger the function?
> 一位开发者正在编写一个无服务器应用程序，该应用程序要求每10分钟调用一次AWS Lambda函数。有什么自动化和无服务器的方法来触发该函数？

- [ ] Deploy an Amazon EC2 instance based on Linux, and edit its /etc/crontab file by adding a command to periodically invoke the Lambda function. `部署一个基于Linux的Amazon EC2实例，并通过添加命令编辑其 /etc/crontab 文件，以定期调用Lambda函数。`
- [ ] Configure an environment variable named PERIOD for the Lambda function. Set the value to 600. `为Lambda函数配置名为PERIOD的环境变量。将值设置为600。`
- [x] Create an Amazon CloudWatch Events rule that triggers on a regular schedule to invoke the Lambda function. `创建一个Amazon CloudWatch Events规则，以定期触发以调用Lambda函数。`
- [ ] Create an Amazon SNS topic that has a subscription to the Lambda function with a 600-second timer. `创建一个Amazon SNS主题，并对Lambda函数进行订阅，设置为600秒的计时器。`

### A company is building an application to track athlete performance using an Amazon DynamoDB table. Each item in the table is identified by a partition key (user_id) and a sort key (sport_name). The table design is shown below. (Note: Not all table attributes are shown) A Developer is asked to write a leaderboard application to display the top performers (user_id) based on the score for each sport_name. What process will allow the Developer to extract results MOST efficiently from the DynamoDB table?
> 一家公司正在构建一个应用程序，使用Amazon DynamoDB表来跟踪运动员的表现。表中的每个项由分区键（user_id）和排序键（sport_name）标识。表的设计如下所示。（注意：并未显示所有表属性）开发者被要求编写一个排行榜应用程序，以根据每个sport_name的分数显示顶尖表现者（user_id）。什么过程将允许开发者最有效地从DynamoDB表中提取结果？

![Question 337](images/question337.jpg)

- [ ] Use a DynamoDB query operation with the key attributes of user_id and sport_name and order the results based on the score attribute. `使用具有user_id和sport_name键属性的DynamoDB查询操作，并根据score属性对结果进行排序。`
- [x] Create a global secondary index with a partition key of sport_name and a sort key of score, and get the results. `创建一个具有sport_name作为分区键和score作为排序键的全局二级索引，并获取结果。`
- [ ] Use a DynamoDB scan operation to retrieve scores and user_id based on sport_name, and order the results based on the score attribute. `使用DynamoDB扫描操作根据sport_name检索分数和user_id，并根据score属性对结果进行排序。`
- [ ] Create a local secondary index with a primary key of sport_name and a sort key of score and get the results based on the score attribute. `创建一个主键为sport_name和排序键为score的局部二级索引，并根据score属性获取结果。`

### A Developer is creating a mobile application that will not require users to log in. What is the MOST efficient method to grant users access to AWS resources?

- [ ] Create credentials using AWS KMS and apply these credentials to users when using the application. `使用AWS KMS创建凭证，并在用户使用应用程序时应用这些凭证。`
- [x] Use Amazon Cognito to associate unauthenticated users with an IAM role that has limited access to resources. `使用Amazon Cognito将未身份验证的用户与具有有限资源访问权限的IAM角色关联。`

### An application running on Amazon EC2 instances must access objects within an Amaon S3 busket that are encrypted using server-side encryption using AWS KMS encryption keys (SSE-KMS). The application must have access to the customer master key (CMK) to decrypt the objects. Which combination of steps will grant the application access? (Select TWO)
> 一个运行在Amazon EC2实例上的应用程序必须访问使用AWS KMS加密密钥（SSE-KMS）进行服务器端加密的Amazon S3存储桶中的对象。该应用程序必须能够访问客户主密钥（CMK）以解密对象。哪种步骤组合将授予应用程序访问权限？（选择两个）

- [x] Write an S3 bucket policy that grants the bucket access to the key. `编写一个S3存储桶策略，授予存储桶对密钥的访问权限。`
- [x] Grant access to the key in the IAM EC2 role attached to the application's EC2 instances. `在附加到应用程序的EC2实例的IAM EC2角色中授予对密钥的访问权限。`
- [ ] Write a key policy that enables IAM policies to grant access to the key. `编写一个密钥策略，允许IAM策略授予对密钥的访问权限。`
- [ ] Grant access to the key in the S3 bucket's ACL. `在S3存储桶的ACL中授予对密钥的访问权限。`
- [ ] Create a Systems Manager parameter that exposes the KMS key to the EC2 instances. `创建一个Systems Manager参数，将KMS密钥暴露给EC2实例。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### What does an Amazon SQS delay queue accomplish?
> Amazon SQS延迟队列的作用是什么？

- [x] Messages are hidden for a configurable amount of time when they are first added to the queue. `消息在首次添加到队列时会被隐藏一段可配置的时间。`
- [ ] Messages are hidden for a configurable amount of time after they are consumed from the queue. `消息在从队列中消费后会被隐藏一段可配置的时间。`
- [ ] The consumer can poll the queue for a configurable amount of time before retrieving a message. `消费者可以在检索消息之前轮询队列一段可配置的时间。`
- [ ] Message cannot be deleted for a configurable amount of time after they are consumed from the queue. `消息在从队列中消费后无法在可配置的时间内被删除。`

### A company has multiple Developers located across the globe who are updating code incrementally for a development project. When Developers upload code concurrently, internet connectivity is slow and it is taking a long time to upload code for deployment in AWS Elastic Beanstalk. Which step will result in minimized upload and deployment time with the LEAST amount of administrative effort?
> 一家公司在全球范围内有多个开发人员，他们正在为一个开发项目增量更新代码。当开发人员并发上传代码时，互联网连接速度慢，上传代码以在AWS Elastic Beanstalk中进行部署所需的时间很长。哪个步骤可以以最少的管理工作量最小化上传和部署时间？

- [ ] Allow the Developers to upload the code to an Amazon S3 bucket, and deploy it directly to Elastic Beanstalk. `允许开发人员将代码上传到Amazon S3存储桶，并直接部署到Elastic Beanstalk。`
- [ ] Allow the Developers to upload the code to a central FTP server to deploy the application to Elastic Beanstalk. `允许开发人员将代码上传到中央FTP服务器，以将应用程序部署到Elastic Beanstalk。`
- [x] Create an AWS CodeCommit repository, allow the Developers to commit code to it, and then directly deploy the code to Elastic Beanstalk. `创建一个AWS CodeCommit存储库，允许开发人员向其提交代码，然后直接将代码部署到Elastic Beanstalk。`
- [ ] Create a code repository on an Amazon EC2 instance so that all Developers can update the code, and deploy the application from the instance to Elastic Beanstalk. `在Amazon EC2实例上创建一个代码存储库，以便所有开发人员都可以更新代码，并从该实例向Elastic Beanstalk部署应用程序。`

### A Development team is working on a case management solution that allows medical claims to be processed and reviewed. Users log in to provide information related to their medical and financial situations. As part of the application, sensitive documents such as medical records, medical imaging, bank statements, and receipts are uploaded to Amazon S3. All documents must be securely transmitted and stored. All access to the documents must be recorded for auditing. What is the MOST secure approach?
> 一个开发团队正在开发一个案例管理解决方案，允许处理和审查医疗索赔。用户登录以提供与其医疗和财务状况相关的信息。作为应用程序的一部分，敏感文件，如医疗记录、医学影像、银行对账单和收据被上传到Amazon S3。所有文档必须安全地传输和存储。所有访问文档的操作必须记录以供审计。最安全的方法是什么？

- [ ] Use S3 default encryption using Advanced Encryption Standard-256 (AES-256) on the destination bucket. `在目标桶上使用先进的加密标准-256（AES-256）进行S3默认加密。`
- [ ] Use Amazon Cognito for authorization and authentication to ensure the security of the application and documents. `使用Amazon Cognito进行授权和身份验证，以确保应用程序和文档的安全性。`
- [ ] Use AWS Lambda to encrypt and decrypt objects as they are placed into the S3 bucket. `使用AWS Lambda在对象被放入S3桶时进行加密和解密。`
- [x] Use client-side encryption/decryption with Amazon S3 and AWS KMS. `使用客户端加密/解密与Amazon S3和AWS KMS。`

### A stock market monitoring application uses Amazon Kinesis for data ingestion. During simulated tests of peak data rates, the Kinesis stream cannot keep up with the incoming data. What step will allow Kinesis to accommodate the traffic during peak hours?
> 一个股票市场监控应用程序使用Amazon Kinesis进行数据摄取。在高峰数据速率的模拟测试中，Kinesis流无法跟上输入数据。哪个步骤可以让Kinesis在高峰时段适应流量？

- [x] Install the Kinesis Producer Library (KPL) for ingesting data into the stream. `安装Kinesis生产者库(KPL)以将数据摄取到流中。`
- [ ] Reduce the data retention period to allow for more data ingestion using DecreaseStreamRetentionPeriod. `减少数据保留期，以允许更多数据摄取，使用DecreaseStreamRetentionPeriod。`
- [ ] Increase the shard count of the stream using UpdateShardCount. `使用UpdateShardCount增加流的分片数量。`
- [ ] Ingest multiple records into the stream in a single call using PutRecords. `使用PutRecords在单个调用中将多个记录摄取到流中。`

### A company has an AWS CloudFormation template that is stored as a single file. The template is able to launch and create a full infrastructure stack. Which best practice would increase the maintainability of the template?

- [x] Use nested stacks for common template patterns. `对常见模板模式使用嵌套堆栈。`
- [ ] Embed credentials to prevent typos. `嵌入凭证以防止输入错误。`

### An on-premises application makes repeated calls to store files to Amazon S3. As usage of the application has increased, 'LimitExceeded' errors are being logged. What should be changed to fix this error?

### A company caches session information for a web application in an Amazon DynamoDB table. The company wants an automated way to delete old items from the table. What is the simplest way to do this?
> 一家公司在Amazon DynamoDB表中缓存Web应用程序的会话信息。该公司希望有一种自动化的方法来删除表中的旧项。最简单的方法是什么？

- [ ] Write a script that deletes old records; schedule the scripts as a cron job on an Amazon EC2 instance. `编写一个脚本来删除旧记录；将脚本安排为Amazon EC2实例上的cron作业。`
- [x] Add an attribute with the expiration time; enable the Time To Live feature based on that attribute. `添加一个具有过期时间的属性；根据该属性启用“生存时间（TTL）”功能。`
- [ ] Each day, create a new table to hold session data; delete the previous day's table. `每天创建一个新表以保存会话数据；删除前一天的表。`
- [ ] Add an attribute with the expiration time; name the attribute ItemExpiration. `添加一个具有过期时间的属性；将该属性命名为ItemExpiration。`

### An application is expected to process many files. Each file takes four minutes to process each AWS Lambda invocation. The Lambda function does not return any important data. What is the fastest way to process all the files?
> 预期一个应用程序将处理许多文件。每个文件处理每个AWS Lambda调用需要四分钟。Lambda函数不返回任何重要数据。处理所有文件的最快方法是什么？

- [ ] First split the files to make them smaller, then process with synchronous RequestResponse Lambda invocations. `首先将文件拆分成更小的部分，然后通过同步的RequestResponse Lambda调用进行处理。`
- [ ] Make synchronous RequestResponse Lambda invocations and process the files one by one. `进行同步的RequestResponse Lambda调用，并逐个处理文件。`
- [x] Make asynchronous Event Lambda invocations and process the files in parallel. `进行异步事件Lambda调用，并并行处理文件。`
- [ ] First join all the files, then process it all at once with an asynchronous Event Lambda invocation. `首先将所有文件合并，然后通过异步事件Lambda调用一次性处理。`
