### AWS CodeBuild builds code for an application, creates the Docker image, pushes the image to Amazon Elastic Container Registry (Amazon ECR), and tags the image with a unique identifier. If the Developers already have AWS CLI configured on their workstations, how can the Docker images be pulled to the workstations?
> AWS CodeBuild为应用程序构建代码，创建Docker镜像，将镜像推送到Amazon Elastic Container Registry（Amazon ECR），并使用唯一标识符标记该镜像。如果开发人员的工作站上已经配置了AWS CLI，如何将Docker镜像拉取到工作站？

- [ ] Run the following: docker pull REPOSITORY URI : TAG. `运行以下命令：docker pull REPOSITORY URI : TAG。`
- [x] Run the output of the following: aws ecr get-login and then run: docker pull REPOSITORY URI : TAG. `运行以下命令的输出：aws ecr get-login，然后运行：docker pull REPOSITORY URI : TAG。`
- [ ] Run the following: aws ecr get-login and then run: docker pull REPOSITORY URI : TAG. `运行以下命令：aws ecr get-login，然后运行：docker pull REPOSITORY URI : TAG。`
- [ ] Run the output of the following: aws ecr get-download-url-for-layer and then run: docker pull REPOSITORY URI : TAG. `运行以下命令的输出：aws ecr get-download-url-for-layer，然后运行：docker pull REPOSITORY URI : TAG。`

### A company needs a new REST API that can return information about the contents of an Amazon S3 bucket, such as a count of the objects stored in it. The company has decided that the new API should be written as a microservice using AWS Lambda and Amazon API Gateway. How should the Developer ensure that the microservice has the necessary access to the Amazon S3 bucket, while adhering to security best practices?
> 一家公司需要一个新的 REST API，该 API 可以返回有关 Amazon S3 存储桶内容的信息，例如存储在其中的对象计数。公司决定将新 API 编写为使用 AWS Lambda 和 Amazon API Gateway 的微服务。开发人员应该如何确保微服务具有对 Amazon S3 存储桶的必要访问权限，同时遵循安全最佳实践？

- [ ] Create an IAM user that has permissions to access the Amazon S3 bucket, and store the IAM user credentials in the Lambda function source code. `创建一个具有访问 Amazon S3 存储桶权限的 IAM 用户，并将 IAM 用户凭据存储在 Lambda 函数源代码中。`
- [x] Create an IAM role that has permissions to access the Amazon S3 bucket and assign it to the Lambda function as its execution role. `创建一个具有访问 Amazon S3 存储桶权限的 IAM 角色，并将其分配给 Lambda 函数作为其执行角色。`
- [ ] Create an Amazon S3 bucket policy that specifies the Lambda service as its principal and assign it to the Amazon S3 bucket. `创建一个指定 Lambda 服务为其主体的 Amazon S3 存储桶策略，并将其分配给 Amazon S3 存储桶。`
- [ ] Create an IAM role, attach the AmazonS3FullAccess managed policy to it, and assign the role to the Lambda function as its execution role. `创建一个 IAM 角色，将 AmazonS3FullAccess 管理策略附加到该角色，并将该角色分配给 Lambda 函数作为其执行角色。`

### An organization is using Amazon CloudFront to ensure that its users experience low-latency access to its web application. The organization has identified a need to encrypt all traffic between users and CloudFront, and all traffic between CloudFront and the web application. How can these requirements be met? (Choose TWO)
> 一家组织正在使用 Amazon CloudFront 确保其用户能够低延迟访问其 web 应用程序。该组织已确定需要加密用户与 CloudFront 之间的所有流量，以及 CloudFront 与 web 应用程序之间的所有流量。如何满足这些要求？（选择两个）

- [ ] Use AWS KMS to encrypt traffic between CloudFront and the web application. `使用 AWS KMS 加密 CloudFront 与 web 应用程序之间的流量。`
- [x] Set the Origin Protocol Policy to 'HTTPS Only'. `将源协议策略设置为“仅 HTTPS”。`
- [ ] Set the Origin's HTTP Port to 443. `将源的 HTTP 端口设置为 443。`
- [x] Set the Viewer Protocol Policy to 'HTTPS Only' or 'Redirect HTTP to HTTPS'. `将查看器协议策略设置为“仅 HTTPS”或“将 HTTP 重定向到 HTTPS”。`
- [ ] Enable the CloudFront option Restrict Viewer Access. `启用 CloudFront 选项限制查看器访问。`

### An application is using Amazon DynamoDB as its data store, and should be able to read 100 items per second as strongly consistent reads. Each item is 5 KB in size. To what value should the table's provisioned read throughput be set?

- [ ] 50 read capacity units. `50 个读取容量单位。`
- [ ] 100 read capacity units. `100 个读取容量单位。`
- [x] 200 read capacity units. `200 个读取容量单位。`
- [ ] 500 read capacity units. `500 个读取容量单位。`

### A Developer is creating a Lambda function that will generate and export a file. The function requires 100 MB of temporary storage for temporary files while executing. These files will not be needed after the function is complete. How can the Developer MOST efficiently handle the temporary files?
> 开发人员正在创建一个 Lambda 函数，该函数将生成并导出一个文件。该函数在执行时需要 100 MB 的临时存储用于临时文件。这些文件在函数完成后不再需要。开发人员如何以最高效的方式处理临时文件？

- [ ] Store the files in EBS and delete the files at the end of the Lambda function. `将文件存储在 EBS 中，并在 Lambda 函数结束时删除文件。`
- [ ] Copy the files to EFS and delete the files at the end of the Lambda function. `将文件复制到 EFS 中，并在 Lambda 函数结束时删除文件。`
- [x] Store the files in the /tmp directory and delete the files at the end of the Lambda function. `将文件存储在 /tmp 目录中，并在 Lambda 函数结束时删除文件。`
- [ ] Copy the files to an S3 bucket with a lifecycle policy to delete the files. `将文件复制到具有生命周期策略以删除文件的 S3 存储桶中。`

### According to best practice, how should access keys be managed in AWS? (Choose TWO)

- [ ] Use the same access key in all applications for consistency. `在所有应用程序中使用相同的访问密钥以保持一致性。`
- [x] Delete all access keys for the account root user. `删除所有账户根用户的访问密钥。`
- [ ] Leave unused access keys in the account for tracking purposes. `在账户中保留未使用的访问密钥以便跟踪。`
- [ ] Embed and encrypt access keys in code for continuous deployment. `将访问密钥嵌入并加密在代码中以进行持续部署。`
- [x] Use Amazon IAM roles instead of access keys where possible. `尽可能使用 Amazon IAM 角色而不是访问密钥。`

### An application running on an Amazon Linux EC2 instance needs to manage the AWS infrastructure. How can the EC2 instance be configured to make AWS API calls securely?
> 在 Amazon Linux EC2 实例上运行的应用程序需要管理 AWS 基础设施。如何配置 EC2 实例以安全地进行 AWS API 调用？

- [ ] Sign the AWS CLI command using the signature version 4 process. `使用签名版本 4 过程对 AWS CLI 命令进行签名。`
- [ ] Run the aws configure AWS CLI command and specify the access key id and secret access key. `运行 aws configure AWS CLI 命令并指定访问密钥 ID 和秘密访问密钥。`
- [x] Specify a role for the EC2 instance with the necessary privileges. `为 EC2 实例指定具有必要权限的角色。`
- [ ] Pass the access key id and secret access key as parameters for each AWS CLI command. `将访问密钥 ID 和秘密访问密钥作为每个 AWS CLI 命令的参数传递。`

### An application needs to use the IP address of the client in its processing. The application has been moved into AWS and has been placed behind an Application Load Balancer (ALB). However, all the client IP addresses now appear to be the same. The application must maintain the ability to scale horizontally. Based on this scenario, what is the MOST cost-effective solution to this problem?
> 应用程序需要在处理过程中使用客户端的 IP 地址。应用程序已迁移到 AWS，并放置在应用程序负载均衡器 (ALB) 后面。然而，所有客户端的 IP 地址现在都显示为相同。应用程序必须保持水平扩展的能力。基于这种情况，解决此问题的最具成本效益的解决方案是什么？

- [ ] Remove the application from the ALB. Delete the ALB and change Amazon Route 53 to direct traffic to the instance running the application. `将应用程序从 ALB 中移除。删除 ALB，并更改 Amazon Route 53 将流量引导到运行应用程序的实例。`
- [ ] Remove the application from the ALB. Create a Classic Load Balancer in its place. Direct traffic to the application using the HTTP protocol. `将应用程序从 ALB 中移除。创建一个经典负载均衡器替代 ALB。使用 HTTP 协议将流量引导到应用程序。`
- [x] Alter the application code to inspect the X-Forwarded-For header. Ensure that the code can work properly if a list of IP addresses is passed in the header. `更改应用程序代码以检查 X-Forwarded-For 头。如果在头中传递了一系列 IP 地址，确保代码能够正常工作。`
- [ ] Alter the application code to inspect a custom header. Alter the client code to pass the IP address in the custom header. `更改应用程序代码以检查自定义头。更改客户端代码以在自定义头中传递 IP 地址。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A development team is using AWS Elastic Beanstalk to deploy a two-tier application that consists of a load-balanced web tier and an Amazon RDS database tier in production. The team would like to separate the RDS instance from the Elastic Beanstalk. How can this be accomplished?
> 一个开发团队正在使用 AWS Elastic Beanstalk 部署一个两层应用程序，该应用程序由负载均衡的 Web 层和 Amazon RDS 数据库层组成。团队希望将 RDS 实例与 Elastic Beanstalk 分开。如何实现这一点？

- [ ] Use the Elastic Beanstalk CLI to disassociate the database. `使用 Elastic Beanstalk CLI 解除数据库关联。`
- [ ] Use the AWS CLI to disassociate the database. `使用 AWS CLI 解除数据库关联。`
- [ ] Change the deployment policy to disassociate the database. `更改部署策略以解除数据库关联。`
- [x] Recreate a new Elastic Beanstalk environment without Amazon RDS. `重新创建一个不包含 Amazon RDS 的新的 Elastic Beanstalk 环境。`

### A company is using AWS CodePipeline to deliver one of its applications. The delivery pipeline is triggered by changes to the master branch of an AWS CodeCommit repository and uses AWS CodeBuild to implement the test and build stages of the process and AWS CodeDeploy to deploy the application. The pipeline has been operating successfully for several months and there have been no modifications. Following a recent change to the application's source code, AWS CodeDeploy has not deployed the updates application as expected. What are the possible causes? (Choose TWO)
> 一家公司正在使用 AWS CodePipeline 来交付其应用程序。交付管道是由 AWS CodeCommit 存储库的主分支上的更改触发的，并使用 AWS CodeBuild 实现过程的测试和构建阶段，使用 AWS CodeDeploy 部署应用程序。该管道已经成功运行了几个月，没有进行任何修改。在最近对应用程序源代码进行更改后，AWS CodeDeploy 并没有按预期部署更新的应用程序。可能的原因是什么？（选择两个）

- [x] The change was not made in the master branch of the AWS CodeCommit repository. `更改未在 AWS CodeCommit 存储库的主分支中进行。`
- [x] One of the earlier stages in the pipeline failed and the pipeline has terminated. `管道中的早期阶段之一失败，导致管道终止。`
- [ ] One of the Amazon EC2 instances in the company's AWS CodePipeline cluster is inactive. `公司 AWS CodePipeline 集群中的一个 Amazon EC2 实例处于非活动状态。`
- [ ] The AWS CodePipeline is incorrectly configured and is not executing AWS CodeDeploy. `AWS CodePipeline 配置不正确，未执行 AWS CodeDeploy。`
- [ ] AWS CodePipeline does not have permissions to access AWS CodeCommit. `AWS CodePipeline 无权访问 AWS CodeCommit。`

### A social media company is using Amazon Cognito in order to synchronize profiles across different mobile devices, to enable end users to have a seamless experience. Which of the following configurations can be used to silently notify users whenever an update is available on all other devices?
> 一家社交媒体公司正在使用 Amazon Cognito 以在不同的移动设备之间同步用户资料，以便最终用户能够获得无缝体验。以下哪种配置可用于在所有其他设备上有更新时静默通知用户？

- [ ] Modify the user pool to include all the devices which keep them in sync. `修改用户池以包含所有保持同步的设备。`
- [ ] Use the SyncCallback interface to receive notifications on the application. `使用 SyncCallback 接口在应用程序中接收通知。`
- [ ] Use an Amazon Cognito stream to analyze the data and push the notifications. `使用 Amazon Cognito 流来分析数据并推送通知。`
- [x] Use the push synchronization feature with the appropriate IAM role. `使用推送同步功能，并配置适当的 IAM 角色。`

### An application displays a status dashboard. The status is updated by 1 KB messages from an SQS queue. Although the status changes infrequently, the Developer must minimize the time between the message arrival in the queue and the dashboard update. What technique provides the shortest delay in updating the dashboard?
> 一个应用程序显示状态仪表板。状态通过来自 SQS 队列的 1 KB 消息进行更新。尽管状态不常变化，但开发者必须最小化消息到达队列和仪表板更新之间的时间。哪种技术能提供最短的仪表板更新延迟？

- [x] Retrieve the messages from the queue using long polling every 20 seconds. `每 20 秒使用长轮询从队列中检索消息。`
- [ ] Reduce the size of the messages by compressing them before sending. `在发送之前通过压缩来减小消息的大小。`
- [ ] Retrieve the messages from the queue using short polling every 10 seconds. `每 10 秒使用短轮询从队列中检索消息。`
- [ ] Reduce the size of each message payload by sending it in two parts. `通过将每条消息有效负载分成两个部分进行发送来减小每条消息的大小。`

### An on-premises legacy application is caching data files locally and writing shared images to local disks. What is necessary to allow for horizontal scaling when migrating the application to AWS?
> 一个本地遗留应用程序正在本地缓存数据文件，并将共享图像写入本地磁盘。在将应用程序迁移到 AWS 时，允许水平扩展需要做什么？

- [ ] Modify the application to have both shared images and caching data written to Amazon EBS. `修改应用程序以将共享图像和缓存数据写入 Amazon EBS。`
- [x] Modify the application to read and write cache data on Amazon S3, and also store shared images on S3. `修改应用程序以在 Amazon S3 上读取和写入缓存数据，并将共享图像存储在 S3 上。`
- [ ] Modify the application to use Amazon S3 for serving shared images; cache data can then be written to local disks. `修改应用程序以使用 Amazon S3 提供共享图像；然后可以将缓存数据写入本地磁盘。`
- [ ] Modify the application to read and write cache data on Amazon S3, while continuing to write shared images to local disks. `修改应用程序以在 Amazon S3 上读取和写入缓存数据，同时继续将共享图像写入本地磁盘。`

### A Developer must trigger an AWS Lambda function based on the item lifecycle activity in an Amazon DynamoDB table. How can the Developer create the solution?
> 开发人员必须基于 Amazon DynamoDB 表中的项目生命周期活动触发 AWS Lambda 函数。开发人员如何创建该解决方案？

- [x] Enable a DynamoDB stream, and trigger the Lambda function synchronously from the stream. `启用 DynamoDB 流，并通过流同步触发 Lambda 函数。`
- [ ] Enable a DynamoDB stream, and trigger the Lambda function asynchronously from the stream. `启用 DynamoDB 流，并通过流异步触发 Lambda 函数。`

### After installing the AWS CLI, a Developer tries to run the command aws configure but receives the following error: Error: aws: command not found. What is the most likely cause of this error?
> 在安装 AWS CLI 后，开发人员尝试运行命令 aws configure，但收到以下错误：错误：aws：命令未找到。导致此错误的最可能原因是什么？

- [x] The aws executable is not in the PATH environment variable. `aws 可执行文件不在 PATH 环境变量中。`

- [ ] Incorrect AWS credentials were provided. `提供了不正确的 AWS 凭据。`

### The Developer for a retail company must integrate a fraud detection solution into the order processing solution. The fraud detection solution takes between ten and thirty minutes to verify an order. At peak, the web site can receive one hundred orders per minute. What is the most scalable method to add the fraud detection solution to the order processing pipeline?
> 一家零售公司的开发人员必须将欺诈检测解决方案集成到订单处理解决方案中。欺诈检测解决方案需要十到三十分钟来验证一个订单。在高峰时段，网站每分钟可以接收一百个订单。将欺诈检测解决方案添加到订单处理流程的最可扩展方法是什么？

- [ ] Add all new orders to an Amazon SQS queue. Configure a fleet of 10 EC2 instances spanning multiple AZs with the fraud detection solution installed on them to pull orders from this queue. Update the order with a pass or fails status. `将所有新订单添加到 Amazon SQS 队列。配置一个跨多个可用区的 10 个 EC2 实例的集群，在其上安装欺诈检测解决方案，从该队列中提取订单。使用通过或失败的状态更新订单。`
- [x] Add all new orders to an SQS queue. Configure an Auto Scaling group that uses the queue depth metric as its unit of scale to launch a dynamically-sized fleet of EC2 instances spanning multiple AZs with the fraud detection solution installed on them to pull orders from this queue. Update the order with a pass or fails status. `将所有新订单添加到 SQS 队列。配置一个使用队列深度指标作为扩展单位的自动扩展组，启动一个动态大小的 EC2 实例集群，跨多个可用区安装欺诈检测解决方案，以从该队列中提取订单。使用通过或失败的状态更新订单。`
- [ ] Add all new orders to an Amazon Kinesis Stream. Subscribe a Lambda function to automatically read batches of records from the Kinesis Stream. The Lambda function includes the fraud detection software and will update the order with a pass or fail status. `将所有新订单添加到 Amazon Kinesis Stream。订阅一个 Lambda 函数以自动从 Kinesis Stream 读取记录批。该 Lambda 函数包含欺诈检测软件，并将使用通过或失败的状态更新订单。`
- [ ] Write all new orders to Amazon DynamoDB. Configure DynamoDB Streams to include all new orders. Subscribe a Lambda function to automatically read batches of records from the Kinesis Stream. The Lambda function includes the fraud detection software and will update the order with a pass or fail status. `将所有新订单写入 Amazon DynamoDB。配置 DynamoDB Streams 以包含所有新订单。订阅一个 Lambda 函数以自动从 Kinesis Stream 读取记录批。该 Lambda 函数包含欺诈检测软件，并将使用通过或失败的状态更新订单。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### When a Developer tries to run an AWS CodeBuild project, it raises an error because the length of all environment variables exceeds the limit for the combined maximum of characters. What is the recommended solution?
> 当开发人员尝试运行 AWS CodeBuild 项目时，出现错误，因为所有环境变量的长度超过了字符组合最大限制。推荐的解决方案是什么？

- [ ] Add the export LC_ALL="en_US.utf8" command to the pre_build section to ensure POSIX localization. `在 pre_build 部分添加 export LC_ALL="en_US.utf8" 命令以确保 POSIX 本地化。`
- [ ] Use Amazon Cognito to store key-value pairs for large numbers of environment variables. `使用 Amazon Cognito 存储大量环境变量的键值对。`
- [ ] Update the settings for the build project to use an Amazon S3 bucket for large numbers of environment variables. `更新构建项目的设置以使用 Amazon S3 存储大量环境变量。`
- [x] Use AWS Systems Manager Parameter Store to store large numbers of environment variables. `使用 AWS Systems Manager Parameter Store 存储大量环境变量。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A set of APIs are exposed to customers using the Amazon API Gateway. These APIs have caching enabled on the API Gateway. Customers have asked for an option to invalidate this cache for each of the APIs. What action can be taken to allow API customers to invalidate the API Cache?
> 一组 API 通过 Amazon API Gateway 向客户公开。这些 API 在 API Gateway 上启用了缓存。客户要求提供一个选项，以使每个 API 的缓存失效。可以采取什么措施来允许 API 客户失效 API 缓存？

- [ ] Ask customers to use AWS credentials to call the InvalidateCache API. `要求客户使用 AWS 凭证调用 InvalidateCache API。`
- [ ] Ask customers to invoke an AWS API endpoint which invalidates the cache. `要求客户调用一个 AWS API 端点以失效缓存。`
- [x] Ask customers to pass an HTTP header called Cache-Control:max-age=0. `要求客户传递一个名为 Cache-Control:max-age=0 的 HTTP 头。`
- [ ] Ask customers to add a query string parameter called 'INVALIDATE_CACHE' when making an API call. `要求客户在进行 API 调用时添加名为 'INVALIDATE_CACHE' 的查询字符串参数。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Developer has been asked to build a real-time dashboard web application to visualize the key prefixes and storage size of objects in Amazon S3 buckets. Amazon DynamoDB will be used to store the Amazon S3 metadata. What is the optimal and MOST cost-effective design to ensure that the real-time dashboard is kept up to date with the state of the objects in the Amazon S3 buckets?
> 开发人员被要求构建一个实时仪表板 Web 应用程序，以可视化 Amazon S3 存储桶中对象的关键前缀和存储大小。将使用 Amazon DynamoDB 存储 Amazon S3 元数据。什么是最佳和最具成本效益的设计，以确保实时仪表板与 Amazon S3 存储桶中对象的状态保持最新？

- [ ] Use an Amazon CloudWatch event backed by an AWS Lambda function. Issue an Amazon S3 API call to get a list of all Amazon S3 objects and persist the metadata within DynamoDB. Have the web application poll the DynamoDB table to reflect this change. `使用 Amazon CloudWatch 事件并由 AWS Lambda 函数支持。发出 Amazon S3 API 调用以获取所有 Amazon S3 对象的列表，并将元数据保留在 DynamoDB 中。让 Web 应用程序轮询 DynamoDB 表以反映此更改。`
- [x] Use Amazon S3 Event Notification backed by a Lambda function to persist the metadata into DynamoDB. Have the web application poll the DynamoDB table to reflect this change. `使用由 Lambda 函数支持的 Amazon S3 事件通知将元数据持久化到 DynamoDB。让 Web 应用程序轮询 DynamoDB 表以反映此更改。`
- [ ] Run a cron job within an Amazon EC2 instance to list all objects within Amazon S3 and persist the metadata into DynamoDB. Have the web application poll the DynamoDB table to reflect this change. `在 Amazon EC2 实例中运行一个 cron 作业以列出 Amazon S3 中的所有对象并将元数据持久化到 DynamoDB。让 Web 应用程序轮询 DynamoDB 表以反映此更改。`
- [ ] Create a new Amazon EMR cluster to get all the metadata about Amazon S3 objects; persist the metadata into DynamoDB. Have the web application poll the DynamoDB table to reflect this change. `创建一个新的 Amazon EMR 集群以获取有关 Amazon S3 对象的所有元数据；将元数据持久化到 DynamoDB。让 Web 应用程序轮询 DynamoDB 表以反映此更改。`

**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A Developer must repeatedly and consistently deploy a serverless RESTful API on AWS. Which techniques will work? (Choose TWO)
> 开发人员必须在 AWS 上重复且一致地部署无服务器 RESTful API。哪些技术可行？（选择两个）

- [ ] Define a Swagger file. Use AWS Elastic Beanstalk to deploy the Swagger file. `定义一个 Swagger 文件。使用 AWS Elastic Beanstalk 部署 Swagger 文件。`
- [ ] Define a Swagger file. Use AWS CodeDeploy to deploy the Swagger file. `定义一个 Swagger 文件。使用 AWS CodeDeploy 部署 Swagger 文件。`
- [x] Deploy a SAM template with an inline Swagger definition. `部署一个带有内联 Swagger 定义的 SAM 模板。`
- [x] Define a Swagger file. Deploy a SAM template that references the Swagger file. `定义一个 Swagger 文件。部署一个引用 Swagger 文件的 SAM 模板。`
- [ ] Define an inline Swagger definition in a Lambda function. Invoke the Lambda function. `在 Lambda 函数中定义内联 Swagger 定义。调用 Lambda 函数。`

**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### An existing serverless application processes uploaded image files. The process currently uses a single Lambda function that takes an image file, performs the processing, and stores the file in Amazon S3. Users of the application now require thumbnail generation of the images. Users want to avoid any impact to the time it takes to perform the image uploads. How can thumbnail generation be added to the application, meeting user requirements while minimizing changes to existing code?
> 现有的无服务器应用程序处理上传的图像文件。该过程当前使用单个 Lambda 函数，该函数接收图像文件，执行处理，并将文件存储在 Amazon S3 中。应用程序的用户现在要求生成图像的缩略图。用户希望避免对图像上传所需时间的任何影响。如何在满足用户需求的同时，将缩略图生成添加到应用程序中，同时最小化对现有代码的更改？

- [ ] Change the existing Lambda function handling the uploads to create thumbnails at the time of upload. Have the function store both the image and thumbnail in Amazon S3. `更改现有的处理上传的 Lambda 函数，以在上传时创建缩略图。让该函数将图像和缩略图都存储在 Amazon S3 中。`
- [ ] Create a second Lambda function that handles thumbnail generation and storage. Change the existing Lambda function to invoke it asynchronously. `创建一个第二个 Lambda 函数来处理缩略图生成和存储。更改现有的 Lambda 函数以异步调用它。`
- [x] Create an S3 event notification with a Lambda function destination. Create a new Lambda function to generate and store thumbnails. `创建一个带有 Lambda 函数目标的 S3 事件通知。创建一个新 Lambda 函数来生成和存储缩略图。`
- [ ] Create an S3 event notification to an SQS Queue. Create a scheduled Lambda function that processes the queue, and generates and stores thumbnails. `创建一个发送到 SQS 队列的 S3 事件通知。创建一个计划的 Lambda 函数来处理队列，并生成和存储缩略图。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A company is using Amazon API Gateway to manage access to a set of microservices implemented as AWS Lambda functions. Following a bug report, the company makes a minor breaking change to one of the APIs. In order to avoid impacting existing clients when the new API is deployed, the company wants to allow clients six months to migrate from v1 to v2. Which approach should the Developer use to handle this change?
> 一家公司正在使用 Amazon API Gateway 管理对一组实现为 AWS Lambda 函数的微服务的访问。在收到错误报告后，公司对其中一个 API 进行了小的破坏性更改。为了避免在新 API 部署时影响现有客户，公司希望允许客户有六个月的时间从 v1 迁移到 v2。开发人员应该使用哪种方法来处理此更改？

- [ ] Update the underlying Lambda function and provide clients with the new Lambda invocation URL. `更新底层 Lambda 函数，并向客户提供新的 Lambda 调用 URL。`
- [ ] Use API Gateway to automatically propagate the change to clients, specifying 180 days in the phased deployment parameter. `使用 API Gateway 自动将更改传播给客户，在阶段性部署参数中指定 180 天。`
- [x] Use API Gateway to deploy a new stage named v2 to the API and provide users with its URL. `使用 API Gateway 将名为 v2 的新阶段部署到 API，并向用户提供其 URL。`
- [ ] Update the underlying Lambda function, create an Amazon CloudFront distribution with the updated Lambda function as its origin. `更新底层 Lambda 函数，创建一个 Amazon CloudFront 分发，将更新的 Lambda 函数作为其源。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A company developed a set of APIs that are being served through the Amazon API Gateway. The API calls need to be authenticated based on OpenID identity providers such as Amazon or Facebook. The APIs should allow access based on a custom authorization model. Which is the simplest and MOST secure design to use to build an authentication and authorization model for the APIs?
> 一家公司开发了一组通过 Amazon API Gateway 提供的 API。这些 API 调用需要基于 OpenID 身份提供者（如 Amazon 或 Facebook）进行身份验证。API 应允许根据自定义授权模型进行访问。用于构建 API 身份验证和授权模型的最简单和最安全的设计是什么？

- [x] Use Amazon Cognito user pools and a custom authorizer to authenticate and authorize users based on JSON Web Tokens. `使用 Amazon Cognito 用户池和自定义授权者根据 JSON Web Token 对用户进行身份验证和授权。`
- [ ] Build a OpenID token broker with Amazon and Facebook. Users will authenticate with these identity providers and pass the JSON Web Token to the API to authenticate each API call. `构建一个与 Amazon 和 Facebook 的 OpenID 令牌代理。用户将与这些身份提供者进行身份验证，并将 JSON Web Token 传递给 API 以验证每个 API 调用。`
- [ ] Store user credentials in Amazon DynamoDB and have the application retrieve temporary credentials from AWS STS. Make API calls by passing user credentials to the APIs for authentication and authorization. `将用户凭证存储在 Amazon DynamoDB 中，让应用程序从 AWS STS 检索临时凭证。通过将用户凭证传递给 API 进行身份验证和授权。`
- [ ] Use Amazon RDS to store user credentials and pass them to the APIs for authentications and authorization. `使用 Amazon RDS 存储用户凭证，并将其传递给 API 进行身份验证和授权。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### Where should an Elastic Beanstalk configuration file named healthcheckur1.config be placed in the application source bundle?
> 名为 healthcheckur1.config 的 Elastic Beanstalk 配置文件应该放置在应用程序源包的哪里？

- [ ] In the root of the application. `在应用程序的根目录中。`
- [ ] In the bin folder. `在 bin 文件夹中。`
- [ ] In healthcheckur1.config.ebextension under root. `在根目录下的 healthcheckur1.config.ebextension 中。`
- [x] In the .ebextensions folder. `在 .ebextensions 文件夹中。`

### A Developer has implemented a Lambda function that needs to add new customers to an RDS database that is expected to run hundreds of times per hour. The Lambda function is configured to use 512MB of RAM and is based on the following pseudo code. After testing the Lambda function, the Developer notices that the Lambda execution time is much longer than expected. What should the Developer do to improve performance?
> 开发人员实现了一个 Lambda 函数，需要将新客户添加到预期每小时运行数百次的 RDS 数据库。该 Lambda 函数配置为使用 512MB 的 RAM，并基于以下伪代码。在测试 Lambda 函数后，开发人员注意到 Lambda 的执行时间比预期长得多。开发人员应该做什么来提高性能？

![Question 385](images/question385.jpg)

- [ ] Increase the amount of RAM allocated to the Lambda function, which will increase the number of threads the Lambda can use. `增加分配给 Lambda 函数的 RAM 量，这将增加 Lambda 可以使用的线程数。`
- [ ] Increase the size of the RDS database to allow for an increased number of database connections each hour. `增加 RDS 数据库的大小，以允许每小时增加数据库连接的数量。`
- [x] Move the database connection and close statement out of the handler. Place the connection in the global space. `将数据库连接和关闭语句移出处理程序。将连接放置在全局空间中。`
- [ ] Replace RDS with Amazon DynamoDB to implement control over the number of writes per second. `用 Amazon DynamoDB 替换 RDS，以实现对每秒写入次数的控制。`

**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### A static website is hosted in an Amazon S3 bucket. Several HTML pages on the site use JavaScript to download images from another Amazon S3 bucket. These images are not displayed when users browse the site. What is the possible cause for the issue?
> 一个静态网站托管在 Amazon S3 存储桶中。网站上的几个 HTML 页面使用 JavaScript 从另一个 Amazon S3 存储桶下载图像。当用户浏览网站时，这些图像未显示。造成此问题的可能原因是什么？

- [ ] The referenced Amazon S3 bucket is in another region. `引用的 Amazon S3 存储桶位于另一个区域。`
- [ ] The images must be stored in the same Amazon S3 bucket. `图像必须存储在同一个 Amazon S3 存储桶中。`
- [ ] Port 80 must be opened on the security group in which the Amazon S3 bucket is located. `必须在 Amazon S3 存储桶所在的安全组中打开端口 80。`
- [x] Cross Origin Resource Sharing must be enabled on the Amazon S3 bucket. `必须在 Amazon S3 存储桶上启用跨源资源共享。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**

### Amazon S3 has the following structure: S3://BUCKET/FOLDERNAME/FILENAME.zip Which S3 best practice would optimize performance with thousands of PUT request each second to a single bucket?
> Amazon S3 具有以下结构：S3://BUCKET/FOLDERNAME/FILENAME.zip。哪种 S3 最佳实践可以优化每秒对单个存储桶的数千个 PUT 请求的性能？

- [ ] Prefix folder names with user id; for example, s3://BUCKET/2013-FOLDERNAME/FILENAME.zip. `以用户 ID 为前缀的文件夹名称；例如，s3://BUCKET/2013-FOLDERNAME/FILENAME.zip。`
- [ ] Prefix file names with timestamps; for example, s3://BUCKET/FOLDERNAME/2013-26-05-15-00-00-FILENAME.zip. `以时间戳为前缀的文件名；例如，s3://BUCKET/FOLDERNAME/2013-26-05-15-00-00-FILENAME.zip。`
- [ ] Prefix file names with random hex hashes; for example, s3://BUCKET/FOLDERNAME/23a6-FILENAME.zip. `以随机十六进制哈希为前缀的文件名；例如，s3://BUCKET/FOLDERNAME/23a6-FILENAME.zip。`
- [x] Prefix folder names with random hex hashes; for example, s3://BUCKET/23a6-FOLDERNAME/FILENAME.zip. `以随机十六进制哈希为前缀的文件夹名称；例如，s3://BUCKET/23a6-FOLDERNAME/FILENAME.zip。`


**[⬆ Back to Top](#table-of-contents)**
